## 2026-07-03 ‚Äî Tuning Pass: `ActionWeights`/`ActionCatalog` (frequent-`Eat` artifact) ‚úÖ

Picked up the standing next-step item. Ran this as harness-driven tuning (no playtesting infra exists yet, and every prior constant table in this codebase ‚Äî `NeedDecayProfile` included ‚Äî was tuned the same way), per the model-assignment doctrine's "Sonnet 5 owns the harness + tuning iterations." **`NeedsDecayHarness` now 30/30 (was 20/20); full solution `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err; headless `--headless --quit` against the real dev save clean (schema v5, day 38, life-sim NPCs 137).** No schema/API surface touched ‚Äî pure constant retune plus a new diagnostic in the harness.

**Root cause (broader than the "Eat" label suggested).** Swept `UtilityCalculator.SelectAction` by hand before touching anything: at full satisfaction, a cheap action's non-deficit terms (temporal+financial+risk, all near-max when cost/time/risk are low) already land within **0.01‚Äì0.06 of Idle's fixed 0.8 baseline**. With `DefaultDeficitPower=2`, that gap closes at a trivial 11‚Äì16% deficit ‚Äî i.e. *every* cheap action, not just `Eat`, was firing at 84‚Äì89‚ÅÑ100 need value. `Eat` was simply the most visible symptom because Hunger decays fastest, so it hit its (already too-eager) crossover first and most often.

**Fix ‚Äî `UtilityCalculator.cs`:** `DefaultDeficitPower` 2‚Üí**5** (steeper convexity ‚Äî a small deficit now contributes far less), `DefaultWeights.NeedDeficitWeight` 1.0‚Üí**1.4** (compensates so a *genuine* deficit still dominates the stress-relief actions' flat bonus in the crisis fixture ‚Äî the two constants pull in opposite directions on the crossover point, so both had to move together; derived analytically, then confirmed bit-for-bit against the harness). All three existing hand-verified `SelectAction` fixtures still pick the same winners (satisfied‚Üí`Idle`, Hunger-critical+funded‚Üí`Eat`, Hunger-critical+broke‚Üí`PickArgument`), and the funded-crisis margin (`Eat` over `DrinkAlone`) actually **widened**, 0.074‚Üí0.091.

**New harness diagnostic ‚Äî `RunActionThresholdChecks`/`FindCrossoverValue` (`Tools/NeedsDecayHarness/Program.cs`).** A deterministic crossover sweep ‚Äî for each need-restoring action, the highest need value at which it first beats `Idle` (every other need full, funds ample) ‚Äî replacing "infer eagerness from a stochastic day trace" with a direct, precise number per action, asserted inside a sensible band (`25`‚Äì`75`: not trivial, but not so late it just duplicates the crisis override). Real before/after, all five actions (confirming the artifact was universal, not Eat-only):

| Action | Old crossover | New crossover |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Eat` | ~87 | **59** |
| `Shower` | ~89 | **61** |
| `Workout` | ~83 | **54** |
| `SocializeEvening` | ~76 | **46** |
| `Sleep` | ~68 | **41** |

**Emergent effect worth flagging, not a regression:** the 30-day `LifeSimManager` integration check's funded-NPC Hunger minimum dropped from 63.9 ‚Üí **8.7** (still passes "never bottoms out at literal 0"). Cause: `Sleep`'s own crossover also dropped, so the NPC now commits to 8-hour sleeps at a lower Sleep value than before; Hunger's accelerating decay curve can run unattended for most of that window and, once it crosses `CriticalThreshold` (20) *mid-sleep*, the hourly re-check doesn't catch it until the following hour's tick (one hour of lag), by which point it's dropped further. The crisis override then correctly interrupts sleep and eats. Read this as the override **provably firing for a well-funded NPC for the first time** ‚Äî under the old constants Hunger's minimum (63.9) never got remotely close to 20, so the override was effectively dead code for anyone with money; now it's exercised exactly as M3's exit criterion names it. Worth an eye once there's real play feel to judge against, but not treated as a bug here.

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) the crossover sweep only proves an action beats `Idle` in isolation, not that it wins the overall argmax against competing actions ‚Äî the Hunger-dips-near-critical dynamic above is exactly that interaction, and isn't itself checked by any fixture; (2) `25`/`75` crossover-band bounds are first-pass judgment calls (not derived from the design doc, which explicitly disclaims owning `q`'s exact value ‚Äî `life_sim_needs_decay.md` ¬ß7 calls it "a curve, not a law"); (3) still no per-action Environmental Multiplier or income mechanic, so this pass only retuned the existing action-vs-Idle balance, not the deeper "broke NPC's paid needs collapse" artifact (expected, no Phase 8 economy yet).

**Next steps:**

1. ~~**Per-action Environmental Multiplier** (¬ß4.1) once locations/activities exist to source it from; today every tick runs neutral (`E=1`).~~ ‚úÖ 2026-07-03 (entry below)
2. `RelationshipGraph.cs` (Phase 6) remains an untouched empty stub.
3. Once there's an actual play surface for the life sim (today it's headless-only), revisit the Hunger-dips-near-critical dynamic above against real play feel ‚Äî the harness proves it's bounded and self-correcting, not whether it *feels* right.

---

## 2026-07-03 ‚Äî Per-Action Environmental Multiplier ‚úÖ (design doc ¬ß4.1 ‚Äî the standing "every tick runs neutral" gap)

Fable 5 as lead (new architectural surface ‚Äî the E-sourcing data shape ‚Äî not a tunable-constant pass). **`NeedsDecayHarness` 39/39 (was 30/30, +9); full solution `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err; headless `--headless --quit` against the real dev save clean (schema v5, day 38, life-sim NPCs 137).** No schema change, no baseball-sim surface touched (MonteCarloHarness/CoreLoopHarness/SchemaValidator not re-run ‚Äî none of their compiled sources moved).

**The load-bearing decision ‚Äî the activity IS the location context.** ¬ß4.1 says E is "sourced from the current location/activity context," but no Location/place entity exists (NPCs aren't anywhere until Phase 7+ gritty-event venues). Rather than invent speculative Location surface, the minimal data shape is a per-need `EnvironmentalModifiers` vector **on each `NpcActionDefinition`**: what an NPC is doing already implies where they are (Sleep/Shower ‚áí at home, SocializeEvening ‚áí bar/party). The field is documented in-code as the composition point where a real location context would later fold in.

**`NeedsEngine.cs`:** new `EnvironmentalModifiers` readonly struct ‚Äî five floats mirroring `NeedsState`'s shape, `Uniform(x)` + `static readonly Neutral`, `Get(NeedType)` ‚Äî this is ¬ß4.1's "five-element E argument" target shape, with the scalar overload kept as the documented `E_all` degenerate case (now delegating through `Uniform`, one code path). New `DecayHour(in NeedsState, in EnvironmentalModifiers, float stressModifier)` overload applies per-need E. The ¬ß4.2 **combined `E¬∑S` ceiling** now actually exists in code: `MaxCombinedModifier = 3f`, product clamped to `[0, 3]` inside the scalar-value `DecayHour` (floor 0 also hardens the monotonicity property against a negative modifier; behavior at all existing call sites unchanged ‚Äî everything passed 1¬∑1).

**`ActionCatalog.cs`:** `NpcActionDefinition` gained `Environment` (optional ctor param, `null` ‚áí `Neutral`, so `Idle`/`Eat`/`DrinkAlone`/`PickArgument` stay at the calibrated baseline). Authored vectors use ¬ß4.1/¬ß6 anchors wherever the design doc provides one: `Sleep`/`Shower` = `Uniform(0.8)` ("resting at home"); `SocializeEvening` = Social √ó0.4 (bar/party ‚Äî decay-slowing is separate from the +35 restore, per ¬ß6's decay-vs-recovery split); `Workout` = Hunger √ó1.5 (the labor-hustle Hunger anchor) + Sleep √ó1.3 (**no doc anchor ‚Äî invented first-pass**, disclosed in-file), implementing ¬ß6's "actions trade needs against each other." The ¬ß4.1 labor-hustle Fitness √ó2.5 anchor is NOT used anywhere yet ‚Äî no Legal Work/hustle action exists in the catalog (gritty-events territory).

**`LifeSimManager.TickHour`:** the decay line now reads the current action's vector ‚Äî `DecayHour(npc.Needs, ActionCatalog.Get(npc.CurrentAction).Environment)`. `CurrentAction` is provably this hour's activity on every path (each hour either re-selects or is mid-action). Stress stays `1.0` ‚Äî the ¬ß4.2 stress scalar still has no live source until Gritty Events, same disclosed gap as the M3 entry.

**Harness (+9 checks, `RunModifierChecks`):** the design doc's ¬ß9 modifier fixtures verbatim ‚Äî written into the doc explicitly "to verify the ¬ß4 layer once E/S are wired to context," which is this pass (E=1.5¬∑S=1.5 ‚Üí 90.55; S=2.0 on Hunger 40 ‚Üí 26.76 vs calm 33.38); ¬ß4.2 ceiling clamp (E¬∑S=4 decays exactly like E=3, ‚Üí 87.40); scalar ‚â° uniform-vector bit-exact identity; per-need vector teeth (Workout env hits Hunger/Sleep exactly, other three bit-identical to neutral); catalog-wide [0.25, 3.0] range sweep. The 168h passive trace is **byte-identical** to the ¬ß9 trajectory fixture (neutral path provably untouched).

**Emergent month-run shifts (informative, direction predicted before running):** funded NPC's 30-day Hunger minimum **8.7 ‚Üí 14.3** ‚Äî sleeping at home (√ó0.8) slows the mid-sleep Hunger bleed, softening the Hunger-dips-near-critical dynamic the tuning pass flagged (next-step #3 above partially self-resolved, still worth a play-feel look). Broke NPC: Sleep min 10.5 ‚Üí 9.3, Hygiene 13.6 ‚Üí 10.8 (still managed, never floor); money-gated needs still collapse as expected. Crossover sweep numbers unchanged by construction ‚Äî `SelectAction` doesn't see environment (decay-side term, not a utility consideration; a future "prefer restful activities when worn down" coupling would be a deliberate design change, not this pass).

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) environment applies only to the decay side ‚Äî utility selection is environment-blind (see above); (2) `Workout` Sleep √ó1.3 and both `Uniform(0.8)` home vectors are the only invented/anchor-interpolated constants, tunable as data via `simulate_utility_decay` (SKILL.md gained an "environment vectors" tuning section + the new check list); (3) no Location entity ‚Äî when places land (Phase 7+), their context should *compose* with the action's vector (e.g. multiply, ceiling-clamped) rather than replace this field; (4) stress `S` still has no live source (unchanged).

**Next steps:**

1. ~~`RelationshipGraph.cs` (Phase 6) remains an untouched empty stub.~~ ‚úÖ 2026-07-04 (entry below)
2. Once there's an actual play surface for the life sim (today it's headless-only), revisit the Hunger-near-critical dynamic against real play feel (softened by this pass: funded-NPC Hunger min now 14.3).
3. When the first hustle/labor action enters the catalog (gritty events), its environment vector already has a ¬ß4.1 anchor waiting (Fitness √ó2.5, Hunger √ó1.5) ‚Äî and that's the natural moment to wire the ¬ß4.2 stress scalar's live source too.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Phase 6 (first slice): RelationshipGraph + Rivalry ‚Üí Baseball Probability Modifiers ‚úÖ

Fable 5 as lead (this is the Phase 6 work the model-assignment note explicitly reserved for it ‚Äî rivalry‚Üíprobability modifiers re-enter the calibrated core, carrying the "prove it with `run_monte_carlo_batch`" burden). **All harnesses green: `MonteCarloHarness` 85/85 (was 78, +7 ‚Äî new suite 8), `NeedsDecayHarness` 49/49 (was 39, +10), `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `SchemaValidator` 58/58; `dotnet build` 0/0; headless boot against the real save clean (`‚Ä¶ life-sim NPCs 137, relationships 0`).** No schema change ‚Äî the Relationships table has existed since v1 and its shape was re-validated against the live save via the `sqlite` MCP (No Blind Queries) before the one new query was written.

**Scope:** BUILD_PLAN Phase 6's first bullet ‚Äî the bidirectional affinity graph backed by the Relationships table, with rivalry scores feeding baseball probability modifiers via the event bus. The second bullet (heir mechanics / succession / 3-generation run) is untouched and remains the phase's exit-criteria work.

**The transport chain (each hop proven by a harness check):** `RelationshipGraph` (Life) ‚Üí `RivalryChangedEvent` (Core, new ‚Äî raw id pair + 0‚Äì100 intensity, canonical ordinal order) ‚Üí `RivalryLedger` (Baseball, new) ‚Üí version-gated slot√óslot byte cache inside each sim ‚Üí one array read per PA. Neither sim references the other's types anywhere (CoreLoopHarness's isolation checks still pass); the graph only publishes, the ledger only subscribes.

**`RelationshipGraph.cs` (Life, ~250 lines):** canonical-pair edge store (`CompareOrdinal` ordering ‚Äî the SAME canonicalization `PlayerQueries.UpsertRelationship` already enforced, so a flush upserts exactly the row hydration read) + per-player adjacency; affinity clamped [-100,100]; `RelationshipKind` deliberately mirrors Data's `RelationshipType` instead of referencing it (`NeedsDecayHarness` wildcard-compiles this folder Data-free; GameManager maps by explicit switch at the persistence boundary). Rivalry intensity = `-affinity` on a negative Rival edge, else 0 (positive-affinity rivals = grudging respect, no modifier). Publication discipline: `Seed()` is silent (hydration), `AttachTo(bus)` announces every active rivalry (the boot handshake ‚Äî no separate sync protocol), mutations publish only when intensity actually changes, no-op writes publish nothing. Persistence mirrors the needs pattern: `CollectDirty` drains a coalesced per-pair dirty set; GameManager upserts on the day-tick + exit-flush cadence, own batch transaction.

**Baseball side (`RivalryModifiers.cs`, new):** `RivalryLedger` (bus-fed pair‚Üíintensity dict + `Version` counter) and `RivalryEffects` ‚Äî the actual probability modifier, following the PED/fatigue precedent exactly: adjust effective ratings into the UNCHANGED `AtBatResolver`, never its calibration tables. At intensity 100: batter +8 power, pitcher +8 stuff (linear in intensity, round-half-up, capped at 100; PED's 1.5√ó applies on top, same as any rating source). Through the ¬ß4.1 matchup weights that is a **three-true-outcomes shift** ‚Äî harness-measured on the flat matchup: K% 22.5‚Üí23.9, HR/PA 3.20‚Üí3.32, 1B 14.3‚Üí13.6, walks essentially untouched.

**Sim wiring (both `LeagueSimulator` and `MicroGame`):** optional `public RivalryLedger? Rivalries` field (the `FeedSink` precedent ‚Äî no constructor churn, every existing call site untouched); slot√óslot byte cache (136¬≤ = 18 KB) rebuilt only when `Version` moves, at `SimulateGameDay`/`PlayGame` entry; per-PA cost is one branch + one byte read, and **intensity 0 takes the exact pre-rivalry call** ‚Äî the attached-but-empty-ledger season is harness-proven bit-identical to the no-ledger season (the M1-lines-cannot-move guarantee, same construction as the v4 mixture identity). In `MicroGame` the boost is applied upstream of BOTH paths (macro-resolved NPC PAs and the human pitch chain ‚Äî the anchor p\* shifts consistently, so a rivalry game feels the same physics everywhere).

**Harness proof (suite 8, +7 checks):** ledger bus contract (set / duplicate no-op / reverse-order clear); boost arithmetic + caps; analytic TTO direction; empty-ledger season bit-identity; 45 max-intensity cross-team rivalries (one lineup √ó one rotation) reach macro PAs (same-seed season diverges) **and that season still lands inside every ¬ß8 band** (.247/.316/.411, K 22.4%, BB 9.1%, HR 3.2%, R/G 4.20); micro-sim same-seed empty-identical/heated-diverges. NeedsDecayHarness (+10): canonical storage, bidirectional adjacency, clamping, intensity derivation, all four publication-discipline cases, AttachTo-after-Seed handshake, dirty-set coalescing.

**Also fixed in passing:** the v5 migration had left all three DB-touching harnesses' hardcoded `user_version` checks stale at 4 ‚Äî the exact gotcha the v3 entry warned about, confirmed missed because none of them were re-run during the needs-persistence session. Bumped to 5 in `MonteCarloHarness`, `CoreLoopHarness`, `SchemaValidator`.

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) **nothing generates rivalries organically yet** ‚Äî the graph is DB-authorable and event-driven, but the writers are Phase 7 Gritty Events / heir dynamics (same shipped-before-its-writer precedent as the PED flag); live boot correctly shows `relationships 0`. (2) Rivalry modifies the macro sim too, not just attended games ‚Äî a deliberate design choice (background rivals also play harder against each other) proven league-neutral in aggregate. (3) No edge-removal API ‚Äî Relationships rows only cascade-delete with a player; a dissolve is an affinity/kind change, not a row delete. (4) `RivalryEffects` constants (¬±8) are first-pass calibration data, tunable behind the existing suite-8 band check.

**Next steps (model assignments recorded 2026-07-04, same cost logic as the 2026-07-03 list ‚Äî cheap models wherever harnesses are tripwires, Fable 5 only for calibrated-core or cross-system-invariant work):**

1. **Phase 6 second bullet ‚Äî heir mechanics:** genetic stat blending, hidden `baseball_interest`, succession on retirement, game-over on lineage failure; exit criteria = simulated 3-generation run with succession handoffs. (The Relationships `Child` kind and the graph are now in place to hang lineage on.) **Split: Opus 4.8** designs (blending formula, interest-reveal model, succession/game-over rules); **Sonnet 5** implements the blending math/heir generation/queries/harness checks from that spec (no probability surface ‚Äî arithmetic on `Player_Ratings` rows); **Fable 5** owns the succession handoff itself (retiring the avatar, re-pointing `CareerManager`, both sims re-initializing mid-save ‚Äî this re-enters the Phase 5 career wiring where mistakes silently drift stat composition rather than failing loudly) plus the 3-generation harness suite.

When Phase 7 Gritty Events land, rivalry/affinity WRITERS arrive ‚Äî `RelationshipGraph.SetRelationship`/`AdjustAffinity` + the persistence loop are ready, and the stress scalar's live source lands at the same moment (standing item). **Fable 5** for the dispatcher skeleton (background polling thread publishing onto the bus ‚Äî threading + zero-GC); **Sonnet 5** for event content batches (with `check_event_graph_integrity` per batch) and the writer calls into the proven graph API.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Phase 6 (second bullet): Heir-Mechanics Design Doc ‚úÖ (Opus 4.8's design half ‚Äî STOPPED for Sonnet handoff)

Scope capped at the **design doc only** ‚Äî Opus 4.8's assigned half of the Phase 6 heir bullet (blending formula, interest-reveal model, succession/game-over rules). **No code written**, so no harness surface moved (none re-run). Mirrors how the two baseball design docs and the need-decay doc shipped their spec before any implementation. Grounded first in the live surfaces it hangs on: `Players.baseball_interest`/`age` and the `Child` `Relationships` kind already exist (no schema change), `CareerManager.CreateAvatar` is the template for heir insertion, and ‚Äî the one real gap found ‚Äî **no yearly player-aging tick exists anywhere** (`age` is written only at creation), so aging is a named dependency of the succession handoff.

**`docs/design/heir_mechanics.md` (Opus 4.8).** Companion to the three existing design docs, same house style (numbered sections, calibration table, worked fixtures that double as harness checks, implementation contract, model split). Load-bearing decisions:

- **Genetic blending = midparent ‚Üí regression-to-mean ‚Üí genetic lottery** (¬ß2.1): `child_r = clamp(round(50 + h¬∑(midparent‚àí50) + Spread¬∑bell))`, `h=0.5`, `Spread=12`, same triangular `bell` as `LeagueGenerator.RollRating`. Regression-to-the-mean is the calibration spine: ¬ß3 proves a lone-parent line fades `90‚Üí60‚Üí52.5‚Üí50` in two generations and a marry-well line steady-states at `mean + m/3`, so **a dynasty can never ratchet the league toward 100** ‚Äî `run_monte_carlo_batch` "no band moved" stays true across generations. All seven ratings blend regardless of position (latent genes carry forward); `is_pitcher`/role inherit from the avatar. Lone-parent (no `Partner`) regresses twice as hard (absent mate = 50-vector) ‚Üí "marrying well is the dynasty strategy," a forward hook into Phase 7 partners.
- **Hidden `baseball_interest` = nurture + luck, not nature** (¬ß4): `interest = clamp(round(55 + 15¬∑(childEdgeAffinity/100) + 30¬∑bell))`, deliberately *not* blending parent interest (NPCs carry 0). The wide `Spread=30` is the failure engine; the affinity term couples to the `Child`-edge (Phase 7 events re-weight a not-yet-revealed heir). "Hidden" is a UX/timing rule (stored plainly like `detection_risk`), **revealed at the succession decision**; binary gate `interest ‚â• 40` = willing.
- **Succession** (¬ß5): retire on `age ‚â• 42` OR `health_ceiling ‚â§ 40` (the PED-erosion coupling), evaluated yearly on `SeasonRolledOverEvent`. Eligible heir = willing AND `age ‚â• 19`. Handoff is a `CreateAvatar`-shaped promote-in-place of an existing Players row: retiree ‚Üí FA, heir rostered preserving the **9+5+3** invariant (same-role slot-inherit, else displace-and-backfill), `avatar_player_id` re-pointed, `dynasty_generation++`, both sims re-`Initialize`. Retiree persists as legacy (stats intact); heir starts a fresh ledger.
- **Game-over on lineage failure** (¬ß6): a retirement trigger with no eligible heir sets `Game_State.lineage_over_reason` (`NoHeirs`/`NoWillingHeir`/`NoPlayableHeir`) ‚Äî its presence *is* the flag. Multiple children are the emergent hedge.
- **Parent‚Üíchild direction is recovered by age** (older endpoint = parent), a maintained invariant, never a stored column ‚Äî so the undirected `Relationships` pair suffices with no schema change. Lineage state rides additive `Game_State` keys (`dynasty_generation`, `dynasty_founder_id`, `lineage_over_reason`).

**Model split pinned in ¬ß9.4:** **Sonnet 5** ‚Äî `HeirGenetics.cs` (pure engine-free static, Data-clean), `CareerManager.ConceiveChild` (heir generation, no roster mutation), the interest/`Child`-edge queries + new `GameStateKeys`, and ¬ß8 harness checks 1‚Äì6 (all arithmetic on rows, fully unblocked ‚Äî seed ages directly). **Fable 5** ‚Äî the ¬ß5.3‚Äì¬ß5.5 succession *handoff* (`Succeed`/`EvaluateSuccession`‚Üí`SuccessionOutcome`), roster-preservation + backfill, the **new yearly aging tick**, generation/game-over state, and the 3-generation harness suite (checks 7‚Äì11, carrying the `run_monte_carlo_batch` "no band moved" burden ‚Äî check 9). Seam: Sonnet produces and evaluates heirs (pure, testable); Fable owns the one dangerous mutation that swaps the avatar.

**Next steps:**

1. **Sonnet 5** implements ¬ß9.1/¬ß9.2 + checks 1‚Äì6 from `docs/design/heir_mechanics.md`. No schema change expected (re-validate the live save via the `sqlite` MCP per No Blind Queries before any query work). Then **hand back to Fable 5** for the ¬ß5 succession handoff + 3-generation suite (checks 7‚Äì11) ‚Äî the exit criteria for the Phase 6 bullet.
2. Everything else on the 2026-07-04 model-assignment list above (Phase 7 Gritty Events dispatcher, rivalry-at-bat feed flag, `RivalryEffects` retune) is unchanged.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Phase 6 (second bullet, Sonnet's half): Heir Genetics, `ConceiveChild` & the Blending/Interest Harness ‚úÖ (design doc ¬ß9.1/¬ß9.2 + ¬ß8 checks 1‚Äì6 ‚Äî STOPPED for Fable handoff)

Scope capped at exactly the Sonnet 5 half of the model split pinned in `docs/design/heir_mechanics.md` ¬ß9.4: the pure blending/interest math, heir generation, the small query surface it needed, and harness checks 1‚Äì6. **The succession handoff, the yearly aging tick, and the 3-generation suite (checks 7‚Äì11) are untouched ‚Äî Fable 5's to build next.** No schema change (re-confirmed against `SchemaDefinitions.sql` directly: `Players.baseball_interest`/`age`, `Player_Ratings`, `Pitcher_Roles`, and the `Child` `Relationships` kind all already exist at v5). **All harnesses green: `MonteCarloHarness` 95/95 (was 85, +10 ‚Äî new suite 9), `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `SchemaValidator` 58/58, `NeedsDecayHarness` 49/49 (unaffected, re-run anyway since shared Data-layer files moved); `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err across all 5 projects; headless `--headless --quit` against the real dev save clean** (schema v5, day 38, avatar present, life-sim NPCs 137, relationships 0 ‚Äî nothing shipped here is wired into boot, by design).

**`HeirGenetics.cs` (new, Assets/Simulation/Baseball) ‚Äî pure static, Data-clean, zero-DB, same profile as `AtBatResolver`.** `HeirGeneticsProfile` holds every constant named in ¬ß9.1 (`Mean`, `Heritability`, `Spread`, the three `Interest*` knobs, `BirthAffinity`, `InterestPlayThreshold`, `MaturityAge`, `MandatoryRetirementAge`, `HealthRetirementFloor` ‚Äî the last three staged now for Fable's ¬ß5 triggers, unused by this pass). `BlendRating`/`RollInterest` each expose a **deterministic core taking the genetic-lottery `bell` as a plain `double`**, plus an `RngState`-driven overload that draws its own `Bell()` ‚Äî the same separation `AtBatResolver.ComputeProbabilities`/`Resolve` established, one level deeper (bypassing RNG entirely lets the harness inject the exact `bell` values the design doc's ¬ß7 fixtures are written against, rather than reverse-engineering a seed). `BlendRatings` blends all seven ratings independently (`is_pitcher` is the caller's decision per ¬ß2.2); `AverageParent()` is the ¬ß2.3 all-50 vector. Rounding is pinned `MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero` per ¬ß2.1, exactly as the fixtures assume.

**`CareerManager.ConceiveChild` (extends CareerManager) ‚Äî mirrors `CreateAvatar` minus the roster mutation.** Parent A = the avatar's ratings; parent B = a `Partner` counterpart's real ratings when a `Partner` `Relationships` edge exists (new private `FindPartnerId`, built on the existing `LoadRelationshipsFor`) and they have a `Player_Ratings` row, else `HeirGenetics.AverageParent()` for blending ‚Äî but a **real** Partner still gets their own `Child` edge even without ratings (only the fully-degenerate no-partner-at-all case skips a second edge). `is_pitcher`/bullpen role inherit from parent A (default `Starter` if the avatar has no role row). One batch: insert the heir (`team_id NULL`, `age` = caller-supplied birth age default 0, `baseball_interest` = the ¬ß4.1 roll, `funds 0`, `health_ceiling 100`/`recklessness 0`/`detection_risk 0` matching `CreateAvatar`'s own "fresh person" defaults), upsert blended ratings, pitcher role + stuff-derived arsenal (`LeagueGenerator.GenerateArsenal`, spread 0) when applicable, and a `Child` edge to each **real** parent via the existing `PlayerQueries.UpsertRelationship`. **No sim re-init** ‚Äî the heir is invisible to both sims until succession rosters it (¬ß9.2's explicit instruction), so this never touches `_league`/`_micro`.

**New query surface (the minimum `ConceiveChild` needed beyond reuse):** `BaseballQueries.TryGetRatings`/`TryGetPitcherRole` ‚Äî single-row PK lookups by `player_id`, added because the existing `LoadRoster` join only covers **rostered** players, but a Partner or a not-yet-succeeded heir is unrostered by construction. `PlayerQueries.SetAge` ‚Äî a targeted single-player `UPDATE Players SET age = @age`, added purely so the harness can seed exact ages (design doc ¬ß5.5 explicitly names this as the unblocking mechanism: *"the harness sets ages directly"*); this is deliberately **not** the yearly `age = age + 1` tick, which stays Fable's per ¬ß5.5/¬ß9.4 and was not built here. `GameStateKeys` gained `DynastyGeneration`/`DynastyFounderId`/`LineageOverReason` as constants only ‚Äî no state-transition wiring, since ¬ß9.4 explicitly reserves "the `dynasty_generation`/`lineage_over_reason` state transitions" for Fable; `CreateAvatar` was deliberately left untouched (no founder-bootstrap write) so Fable's succession pass owns the whole lifecycle without a seam mismatch.

**Harness ‚Äî `Tools/MonteCarloHarness` suite 9 (+10 checks, ¬ß8 checks 1‚Äì6):** ¬ß7 fixtures F1/F2/F4 reproduce exactly under injected `bell` (F1 also asserted as a full seven-rating vector, proving the law applies identically to every field); the ¬ß3 regression identity (`child_r == round(50 + h¬∑(midparent‚àí50))` at `bell=0`, which zeroes the lottery term regardless of `Spread`'s actual value) holds across a parent-value sweep for both two-parent and lone-parent forms; every blended rating/rolled interest stays in [0,100] across extreme parents/affinity √ó extreme bell; the lottery is mean-zero over 100k draws (mean 65.019 vs the exact 65.0 target); the `interest ‚â• 40` gate classifies correctly at the precise rounding boundary (40 = willing, 39 = unwilling); the ¬ß1.2 direction invariant (older `Child`-edge endpoint always resolves as parent) holds through a real `ConceiveChild` run sweeping both the heir's birth age (0/5/10/15/18) and, via the new `SetAge`, the parent's age (35) too.

**Found and fixed: `F3` in the design doc doesn't reconcile.** "Both parents 55 ‚Üí lucky bell ‚Üí 72" is unreachable under the shipped model ‚Äî `Spread=12` bounds the lottery to ¬±12 off `blended=52.5`, so the ceiling is <64.5 at any valid `bell` (which is itself bounded to (‚àí1,1)); 72 would need `bell‚âà1.6`. F1/F2/F4 all independently verify the implementation is correct (reproduced to the exact stated values), so this is a design-doc arithmetic slip, not a code bug ‚Äî adapted into a qualitative "a lucky roll meaningfully beats the blended baseline" check (bell=0.9 ‚Üí 63) rather than silently fabricating a bell that hits the wrong number. Flagging back rather than quietly patching, per the project's own "Author: Claude Opus 4.8" attribution on that doc.

**Also fixed in passing:** `CoreLoopHarness`'s Life‚ÜîBaseball boundary scan is a **naive literal substring search** over raw file text (`File.ReadAllText(file).Contains("Simulation.Life")`), not a semantic reference check ‚Äî `HeirGenetics.cs`'s own doc comment describing what it *doesn't* reference ("never Simulation.Life, never the database") tripped a false positive by containing the forbidden string as prose. Reworded to "never the Life sim" (same meaning); re-verified 22/22. Worth remembering for any future Baseball-side doc comment that wants to talk *about* the boundary rule.

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) `ConceiveChild` is a callable seam with no production trigger yet ‚Äî same "shipped before its writer" precedent as the PED flag and the rivalry graph; Phase 7's marriage/time life-event is the eventual caller (¬ß11.2). (2) The three new `GameStateKeys` are unused by any write path so far ‚Äî Fable's founder-bootstrap (`dynasty_generation = 1` at `CreateAvatar`) and succession transitions land together in the next pass. (3) `SetAge` and the age-blind `ConceiveChild` mean nothing in today's build actually ages a player ‚Äî the yearly tick is entirely Fable's ¬ß5.5 surface. (4) The design doc's F3 fixture is arithmetically inconsistent as written (see above).

**Next steps (Phase 6 exit criteria ‚Äî the handoff named in `docs/design/heir_mechanics.md` ¬ß9.4):**

1. ~~**Fable 5** ‚Äî the ¬ß5.3‚Äì¬ß5.5 succession handoff (`CareerManager.Succeed`/`EvaluateSuccession` ‚Üí `SuccessionOutcome`), roster-preservation + backfill (same-role slot-inherit vs displace-and-backfill), the new yearly aging tick (`age = age + 1` on `SeasonRolledOverEvent`, a genuinely new surface per ¬ß5.5), the `dynasty_generation`/`dynasty_founder_id`/`lineage_over_reason` state transitions (including bootstrapping `dynasty_generation = 1` at founder creation ‚Äî `CreateAvatar` was deliberately left untouched this pass so this lands as one coherent piece), and the ¬ß8 checks 7‚Äì11 (the 3-generation suite, carrying the `run_monte_carlo_batch` "no band moved" burden on check 9). This closes Phase 6's exit criteria.~~ ‚úÖ 2026-07-04 (entry below)
2. Everything else on the 2026-07-04 model-assignment list (Phase 7 Gritty Events dispatcher, rivalry-at-bat feed flag, `RivalryEffects` retune) is unchanged and still open.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Phase 6 EXIT CRITERIA CLOSED: Succession Handoff, Yearly Aging Tick & the 3-Generation Suite ‚úÖ (design doc ¬ß5‚Äì¬ß6/¬ß8 checks 7‚Äì11 ‚Äî Fable's half)

Fable 5 as lead ‚Äî exactly the half ¬ß9.4 reserved: the succession handoff re-enters the Phase 5 career-wiring path where a roster miscount silently drifts stat composition, and check 9 carries the `run_monte_carlo_batch` "no band moved" burden. **All harnesses green: `MonteCarloHarness` 120/120 (was 95, +25 ‚Äî three new lineage suites), `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `SchemaValidator` 58/58, `NeedsDecayHarness` 49/49 (shared Data files moved, re-run per standing rule); `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err all 5 projects; headless boot against the real dev save clean ‚Äî and the save's Game_State now shows `dynasty_generation 1` / `dynasty_founder_id = avatar` (the one-time founder migration ran on first boot, verified via sqlite3).** No schema change; the one new query join (`LoadFreeAgents`) was plan-checked via the sqlite MCP before writing (No Blind Queries: idx_players_team seeks the `IS NULL` bucket, PK autoindexes probe the joins).

**The yearly aging tick (¬ß5.5 ‚Äî the genuinely new surface).** `PlayerQueries.AgeAllPlayers()` ‚Äî one set-based `UPDATE Players SET age = age + 1`, its own implicit transaction ‚Äî fired from `CareerManager`'s new `SeasonRolledOverEvent` subscriber **before** the succession check in the same handler (per-channel subscriber order makes "age 41‚Üí42 triggers retirement this rollover" true by construction). It runs unconditionally ‚Äî the world ages with or without an avatar, and **keeps aging after game-over** (the handler parks only the succession check). Harness-proven: one rollover ages founder/heir/an untouched NPC by exactly +1.

**The handoff (`CareerManager.Succeed` / `EvaluateSuccession` / `RunSuccessionCheck` ‚Üí `SuccessionOutcome`).** `EvaluateSuccession` is the read-only ¬ß5.1/¬ß5.2 decision (both triggers ‚Äî age ‚â• 42, health_ceiling ‚â§ 40 ‚Äî children gathered via the ¬ß1.2 older-endpoint-is-parent walk, interest read live at reveal, deterministic best-heir pick by summed role ratings with player_id ties, failure reasons `NoHeirs`/`NoWillingHeir`/`NoPlayableHeir`). `Succeed(heirId)` is the one dangerous mutation: validates loudly (must be an unrostered, willing, of-age **child** of the avatar), then one batch ‚Äî retiree ‚Üí FA, heir onto **the retiree's team** (the ¬ß5.4 reference rule; different-team signing is future UI), roster preserved per ¬ß5.4 (same role = exact slot inherit; mismatch = displace weakest same-role + backfill the vacated slot), `avatar_player_id` re-pointed, `dynasty_generation`++ ‚Äî then both sims re-Initialize + `ActivateAvatar`, identical to `CreateAvatar`'s tail (with `FlushPending` first, so mid-season handoffs lose nothing). `RunSuccessionCheck` = evaluate + apply (Succeed or persist `lineage_over_reason`), stores `LastSuccession` for the UI, and is the public seam a voluntary-retirement UI calls directly ‚Äî the rollover handler and the harness both use it.

**Backfill & the signability window (a disclosed ¬ß5.4 extension).** The FA pool (`BaseballQueries.LoadFreeAgents`) is windowed in SQL to *signable* people ‚Äî `age ‚àà [MaturityAge, MandatoryRetirementAge)`, `health_ceiling > HealthRetirementFloor` ‚Äî so an underage heir, a retired-by-age avatar, or a health-retired one can never be "promoted" back onto a roster (all pool reads also happen before anyone is benched, so the retiree can't backfill their own slot). Empty pool ‚Üí a replacement-level filler via `LeagueGenerator.GeneratePlayer` (now internal) at spread 0 (+ arsenal when the vacated role pitches), the EnsureV4 path. Both branches harness-proven with the 9+5+3 invariant asserted per team.

**Lineage state.** `CreateAvatar` now bootstraps `dynasty_generation = 1` + `dynasty_founder_id` in its batch; `LoadExistingAvatar` runs the same bootstrap once for pre-lineage saves and hydrates `LineageOverReason`. Game-over writes **only** the flag (world untouched, avatar stays rostered) ‚Äî the UI owns what "over" looks like.

**Harness (+25):** the 3-generation exit-criteria run through the real event loop (884 driven days, 2 rollover handoffs ‚Äî slot-inherit then pitcher-override mismatch ‚Äî `dynasty_generation == 3`, retiree stats intact, promoted-FA backfill, founder-not-signable, GS/W/L identities both succession seasons, **generation-3 season inside the ¬ß8 bands** `.248/.317`, drift bound `90 ‚Üí 56 ‚Üí 58` toward the mean, cold-reload rehydration mid-lineage); the failure ladder (all three reasons persisting the key, game-over mutating nothing else, post-game-over rollover aging-but-parked); the health trigger driven through a real `ApplyPedGameCosts` erosion (100‚Üí40 forces succession at age 30); the empty-pool filler handoff (player count +1, invariant holds).

**Found while testing (fixture rule, now in SKILL.md):** an age-seeded fixture that ages only one bloodline member can break the ¬ß1.2 invariant the real aging tick maintains by construction ‚Äî an early draft aged the gen-2 avatar to 42 while the health-retired founder was still 30, and `EvaluateSuccession` (correctly, per the age-recovery rule) resolved **grandpa as an eligible heir**. Fixtures must age the whole bloodline consistently; real play always does.

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) succession is fully automatic on the rollover ‚Äî ¬ß5.2's "the player chooses one (UI)" needs a succession screen; until then the deterministic autopilot pick stands (same precedent as `AutopilotAttendedGames`), with `LastSuccession` exposed for the UI to notice. (2) On rollover day the *outgoing* avatar plays the new season's day-1 game before succession fires (`DayAdvancedEvent` dispatches before `SeasonRolledOverEvent`) ‚Äî one farewell game, mechanically harmless (GS identities hold), arguably narratively right. (3) Game-over leaves the sim running (games keep playing); stopping is the UI's call when it lands. (4) Aging has no rating-decline curve (¬ß11.6 ‚Äî veterans don't fade yet). (5) `PlayerQueries.SetBaseballInterest` added as the harness-seeding write (SetAge precedent); it is also the write path Phase 7 events will want.

**Next steps (model assignments, same cost logic as prior lists):**

1. **Phase 7 Gritty Events dispatcher** (background polling loop publishing onto the bus ‚Äî threading + zero-GC): **Fable 5**. The stress scalar's live source and the first rivalry/affinity/interest writers land with it; `RelationshipGraph`'s API, `SetBaseballInterest`, and the `ConceiveChild` seam are all waiting.
2. **Event content batches** (JSON prerequisites/weights/branches, `check_event_graph_integrity` per batch) + the **rivalry-at-bat feed flag** (small `NpcPaFeedEvent` extension): **Sonnet 5**.
3. **Succession UI** (the reveal screen + heir choice + game-over screen, consuming `LastSuccession`/`EvaluateSuccession`/`LineageOverReason`): **Sonnet 5** after the scene-transport pattern for it is pinned (scene-mapper rules apply; the sim seam is already built and harness-proven).
4. **`RivalryEffects` ¬±8 retune after playtesting**: **Fable 5** (calibrated-core data behind the suite-8 band check).

Standing rule regardless of model: re-run `run_monte_carlo_batch` after anything that compiles into the sim assembly; escalate to Fable 5 if any band moves.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Phase 7: Gritty Event Dispatcher, Stress Scalar & the First Rivalry/Interest Writers ‚úÖ (exit-criteria cascade proven end-to-end)

Fable 5 as lead ‚Äî exactly the half the model-assignment list reserved (background polling thread + zero-GC + the cross-system writers); Sonnet's half (content batches at volume, event-choice UI, rivalry-at-bat feed flag) is unblocked behind the contracts pinned this session. **All suites green: new `Tools/GrittyEventsHarness` 38/38, `MonteCarloHarness` 120/120, `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `SchemaValidator` 58/58, `NeedsDecayHarness` 49/49; `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err across all 6 projects; headless boot against the real dev save clean ‚Äî `‚Ä¶ relationships 0, gritty events 4 (dispatcher polling)`, dispatcher thread stopped cleanly on quit.** No schema change (v5 as-is); Players/Entity_Flags/Game_State re-validated via the sqlite MCP before the one new query class was written, and `EXPLAIN QUERY PLAN` confirmed the poll rides `idx_entity_flags_active_name` ‚Äî the partial index v1 built *for this exact poll*, finally consumed.

**Design doc first ‚Äî `docs/design/gritty_event_framework.md` (Fable 5).** The content contract Sonnet authors batches against: threading model (¬ß1), JSON schema (¬ß2), condition algebra (¬ß3), the closed consequence vocabulary (¬ß4), stress wiring (¬ß5), probability/determinism (¬ß6), acceptance checks (¬ß7). `check_event_graph_integrity`'s SKILL.md rewritten against it (graph-level checks the loader can't see: orphaned prerequisite flags, dead-end set_flags, unpaced loops, weight sanity).

**The pipeline (each hop harness-proven):** `EventDispatcher` (Narrative, background thread) polls a **read-only WAL companion connection** ‚Äî `DatabaseManager.CreateReadOnlyView()`, a nested type so DatabaseManager stays the only class that opens connections; poll SQL lives in `NarrativePollQueries` (Data, view-bound, prepared) per database_rules. Steady state = one prepared `current_day` scalar per 250 ms; the full snapshot (players + active flags + avatar id) and evaluation sweep run **only when the day moves** ‚Äî the first observed day is recorded, never evaluated, so a reload can't re-roll a lived day; multi-day jumps catch up day-by-day against the current snapshot. Fires publish `GrittyEventFiredEvent` via the bus's thread-safe `Publish` (built for this caller in Phase 2, first real use). `EventConsequenceApplier` (main pump) autopilot-resolves the branching choice (weighted draw ‚Äî the AutopilotAttendedGames precedent; `GrittyEventResolvedEvent` is the future UI's seam), commits DB consequences in **its own batch**, then routes: funds/interest as new atomic clamped-in-SQL `PlayerQueries.AdjustFunds`/`AdjustBaseballInterest` (+ `FundsImpulseEvent` keeps the Life sim's in-memory mirror in step), flags through the existing `SetFlag` with `set_on_day` = fire day (the cascade clock), **relationships as direct `RelationshipGraph` calls** (create-or-deepen semantics; the graph stays publish-only and the untouched Phase-6 transport carries `RivalryChangedEvent` into both baseball sims ‚Äî the organic rivalry writer at last), and **stress via `StressImpulseEvent`** per the life_sim_needs_decay.md ¬ß10 bus mandate. Safety valves: one fire per subject per day, `MaxFiresPerDay = 8`, per-(event,subject) `cooldown_days`.

**The stress scalar goes live (closes ¬ß4.2):** per-NPC `stress ‚àà [0,100]` in `LifeSimManager` (in-memory, like needs pre-v5); `NeedsEngine.StressModifierFor` = the ¬ß4.2 mapping verbatim (`S_max 2.5`), fed into every hourly `DecayHour`; passive relaxation 0.4/hr; stress-relief actions discharge 15; and `UtilityCalculator.SelectAction` gained the **second override trigger** ‚Äî `stress ‚â• 70` engages the same crisis pass (temporal weight zeroed, relief bonus live) with zero need deficit. Stress 0 is bit-identical to every pre-Phase-7 trace (harness-proven; NeedsDecay's 49 checks untouched). SKILL.md gained the stress-knob tuning table.

**Seed content ‚Äî `Assets/Narrative/Events/Content/core_events.json`** (4 events, loaded per-folder so a Sonnet batch is a dropped-in file; **Phase 9 export note: Content/*.json needs the include filter, same as the .sql**): `back_alley_bribe` (the rules doc's own Funds<500 ‚àß Recklessness>75 example) ‚Üí `compromised_syndicate` ‚Üí `syndicate_shakedown` (`min_days_since: 365`), plus `beanball_grudge` (rivalry writer) and `backyard_catch` (heir interest writer, age<16).

**Harness ‚Äî `Tools/GrittyEventsHarness` (in sln; compiles Data+Core+Life+Narrative+RngState headless).** 38 checks: loader contract (5 loud rejections), condition truth table incl. the min_days_since boundary (day N ‚ä®, N‚àí1 ‚ä≠), day-gating/caps/cooldown-through-catch-up/avatar scope, **the exit-criteria cascade end-to-end** (bribe fires day 2 ‚Üí flag set_on_day 2 ‚Üí nothing on day 3 ‚Üí shakedown at day 367 exactly; funds floor-clamp 2100‚àí3000‚Üí0 proven en route), rivalry create-then-deepen (‚àí35‚Üí‚àí70, RivalryChangedEvent intensities 35/70 on the bus), interest clamp (8‚Üí100), choice-weight draw (zero-weight never picked), five stress checks (¬ß9 fixture 26.76 vs 33.38 through the live path, clamp, relaxation 25‚Üí15.4/day, high-stress override picks `DrinkAlone` on full needs, relief-discharge), **the real-thread test** (poller on its own WAL connection sees the main thread's committed day and fires through the real pump; Stop idempotent), idle-poll allocation ‚â§512 B (measured 464 ‚Äî one unavoidable ADO.NET reader+box per scalar; the sim hot paths stay 0 B), and seeded bit-for-bit fire-schedule determinism.

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) **stress is in-memory** ‚Äî quits lose it (needs-pre-v5 precedent; additive schema pass when it earns a migration). (2) **Choice resolution is 100% autopilot, avatar included** ‚Äî the event-choice UI consumes `GrittyEventFiredEvent`/`ResolvedEvent` when it ships. (3) Catch-up evaluates missed days against the *present* snapshot (historical prerequisites approximated; exact at interactive pace where N=1). (4) Cooldowns are in-memory pacing and reset on reload ‚Äî permanence is content's flag round-trip, by design (¬ß2). (5) Life-sim daily action *spending* still never persists to the DB (pre-existing gap, now more visible since prerequisites poll DB funds; event deltas themselves are consistent on both sides via the impulse) ‚Äî Phase 8 economy territory. (6) Seed weights/amounts are first-pass content calibration, unplaytested. (7) A relationship consequence on an existing edge adjusts affinity but never reclassifies the kind.

**Next steps (model assignments, same cost logic):**

1. **Event content batches** (JSON per the design doc ¬ß2‚Äì¬ß4, `check_event_graph_integrity` per batch ‚Äî its SKILL.md now carries the real checklist) + the **rivalry-at-bat feed flag** (small `NpcPaFeedEvent` extension) + the **succession UI** (unchanged from the prior list): **Sonnet 5.**
2. **Event-choice UI** (render a fired event's choices for the avatar instead of autopilot; the Fired/Resolved seam is built): **Sonnet 5**, after the scene transport is pinned per ui_conventions.
3. **Stress persistence** (additive schema v6 via the validation path ‚Äî bump the three harnesses' hardcoded user_version checks, the known gotcha) and the **`ConceiveChild`/marriage consequence** (partner-target semantics need a design pass): **Fable 5**, when prioritized.
4. **`RivalryEffects` ¬±8 retune after playtesting** (unchanged): **Fable 5.**

Standing rule regardless of model: re-run `run_monte_carlo_batch` after anything that compiles into the sim assembly; escalate to Fable 5 if any band moves.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Event Content Batch 2: Syndicate Escalation, Steroid Scandal, Injury & the First Friend/Partner Writers ‚úÖ (Sonnet 5 ‚Äî item 1 of the queued list)

Scope capped at exactly the assigned item ‚Äî event content authored against `docs/design/gritty_event_framework.md` ¬ß2‚Äì¬ß4, validated per `check_event_graph_integrity`. Did not touch event-choice UI, the rivalry-at-bat feed flag, or succession UI (the other three queued items, still open). **`GrittyEventsHarness` now 39/39 (was 38, +1); `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err across all 6 projects; live headless boot against the real dev save clean ‚Äî `‚Ä¶ gritty events 11 (dispatcher polling)` (was 4), no errors.** No schema/engine change ‚Äî pure content plus one harness gap closed.

**The gap found before authoring anything:** `check_event_graph_integrity`'s own item 1 ("load the whole Content folder together‚Ä¶ cross-batch duplicate ids fail here‚Ä¶ the fastest full check is running the harness") wasn't actually true ‚Äî `GrittyEventsHarness`'s only content check parsed `core_events.json` by hardcoded path, so a second batch file's ids were never merge-checked against the first, and GameManager's real multi-file `LoadGrittyEventContent()` path had no test coverage at all. Fixed first, before writing content: a new check in `RunContentChecks()` mirrors GameManager's `*.json` folder scan (`System.IO.Directory.GetFiles` standing in for Godot's `DirAccess`, same relationship as every other engine-free harness in this repo) and parses every file in `Content/` into one `GrittyEventLibrary` via the existing `GrittyEventJson.Parse(IReadOnlyList&lt;string&gt;)` overload ‚Äî which itself already throws on cross-batch duplicate ids, so "no exception" is the collision proof. Asserts today's true merged count (11) and that spot-checked ids from both files resolve. This is now a durable, permanent check for every future batch, not just this one.

**`Assets/Narrative/Events/Content/career_arc_events.json` (new batch, 7 events) ‚Äî a dropped-in file per the framework's own contract, `core_events.json` untouched.**

- **Closes the syndicate arc's disclosed dead-end.** `syndicate_shakedown`'s `defy_them` choice has set `syndicate_marked` since Phase 7 shipped, but nothing ever read it (flagged as a known artifact at the time). `syndicate_enforcers` (`flag_active: syndicate_marked`, `min_days_since: 14`) reads it: `pay_the_enforcers` clears the flag (a clean, permanent exit); `fight_back` doesn't (escalates a `Rival` edge to `league` instead), so the danger genuinely recurs ‚Äî paced by `cooldown_days: 60`, not an unpaced loop.
- **The steroid-scandal arc CLAUDE.md's mission statement names as the example gritty event.** `caught_juicing` gates on `detection_risk > 70` (reachable ‚Äî confirmed against `LeagueSimulator.PedDetectionRiskPerGame = 2`/game, so ~35 games of PED use crosses it well before the 60-game health-retirement threshold) and its own `flag_inactive: steroid_scandal_public`, so getting caught is a one-time beat; `redemption_tour` reads the flag at `min_days_since: 180` and clears it, so a repeat offender can be caught again ‚Äî checked, not assumed.
- **`injury_scare`** gates on `health_ceiling < 40` ‚Äî the exact same constant as `HeirGeneticsProfile.HealthRetirementFloor` (the succession health trigger), so this is the narrative beat for the same mechanical threshold that can end a career, not an arbitrary number.
- **The framework's first `friend`/`partner` consequences.** Every shipped relationship consequence before this batch was `rival`; `road_trip_bonding` (friend) and `spring_training_romance` (partner) are the first positive ones. `spring_training_romance` is the first-ever organic `Partner` writer ‚Äî `CareerManager.ConceiveChild`'s "real Partner counterpart" blending branch has been dead code in practice since it shipped (nothing ever created a `Partner` edge; every heir conceived so far silently used `HeirGenetics.AverageParent()`). Deliberately targets `teammate`, never `league`: `EventConsequenceApplier.IsCandidate`'s `league` pool is every Players row with no age filter (an heir of any age is eligible), while `teammate`/`opponent` are engine-guaranteed rostered-and-therefore-adult by construction (`LeagueGenerator.GeneratePlayer` rolls age 21‚Äì36; succession backfill's `LoadFreeAgents` windows to `[MaturityAge, MandatoryRetirementAge)`). Read but did not touch `EventConsequenceApplier`/`IsCandidate` ‚Äî this is a content-authoring workaround for a real engine gap (`league` has no age floor), not a fix; worth a look if a future batch wants a `league`-scoped relationship.
- **`benched_for_video_games`** mirrors `backyard_catch` as `baseball_interest`'s negative counterpart (`age < 16`, interest ‚àí8 vs the existing event's +8), additionally gated on `baseball_interest > 10` so it stops firing once a kid's interest has already floored rather than repeating a flavor beat against a clamped value.

**Self-audit against the skill's 6 checks** (documented per its own "list them in the batch review" instruction, since checks 2‚Äì6 are graph-level judgment calls the loader can't make):

1. Whole-folder merge ‚Äî proven by the new harness check (11 events, 2 files, no collisions).
2. No orphaned prerequisites ‚Äî `syndicate_marked` (read by `syndicate_enforcers`) and `steroid_scandal_public` (read by `redemption_tour`) are each set by a `set_flag` in the merged library; `compromised_syndicate` is unchanged from the seed batch.
3. No dead-end `set_flag` ‚Äî every flag this batch sets is read by an event in the merged library (see above); no new forward-hook flags introduced.
4. No unpaced loops ‚Äî `syndicate_enforcers`/`injury_scare`/`road_trip_bonding`/`spring_training_romance`/`benched_for_video_games` all carry `cooldown_days > 0`; `caught_juicing`/`redemption_tour` each break their own prerequisite via the flag they set/clear (cooldown incidental).
5. Scope sanity ‚Äî n/a, all seven are `scope: any` (none `avatar`-scoped).
6. Weight sanity ‚Äî `syndicate_enforcers` (0.15) and `injury_scare` (0.12) exceed the ~0.1 any-event guideline, justified the same way the shipped `syndicate_shakedown` (0.25) was: both gate on a narrow, rare state (`syndicate_marked`; `health_ceiling < 40`), not the full ~136-subject population. The other five sit at ‚â§0.08.

**Verified:** `dotnet build` 0/0 (all 6 projects). `dotnet run --project Tools/GrittyEventsHarness -c Release` ‚Üí 39/39. Live headless run via the Godot MCP against the real dev save: boot log moved from `gritty events 4` to `gritty events 11`, zero errors, clean `stop_project`. `MonteCarloHarness`/`CoreLoopHarness`/`NeedsDecayHarness`/`SchemaValidator` not re-run ‚Äî none of their compiled sources moved (content JSON + a `Tools`-only harness edit, no schema/sim/life-sim surface touched).

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) `EventConsequenceApplier`'s `league` target pool has no age floor ‚Äî a real engine gap, sidestepped here by never using `league` for a new relationship consequence, not fixed; worth a look before any future batch wants one. (2) All seven new events are unplaytested first-pass content, same disclosed status as the seed batch's weights/amounts. (3) `spring_training_romance`'s `partner` consequence only actually reclassifies an edge to `Partner` when no prior edge exists between the two picked players (¬ß4's documented "a feud deepens, it doesn't reclassify a marriage" rule) ‚Äî a teammate pair that already has a `Friend`/`Rival` edge just gets an affinity nudge on their existing kind instead; narratively harmless either way, but means `ConceiveChild`'s real-Partner path isn't guaranteed to activate on the event's first fire for any given pair.

**Next steps (unchanged from the model-assignment list ‚Äî items 2‚Äì4 still open, all Sonnet 5):**

1. Event-choice UI (render a fired event's choices for the avatar instead of autopilot) ‚Äî scene transport needs pinning first, per `gritty_event_framework.md` ¬ß9.
2. Rivalry-at-bat feed flag (small `NpcPaFeedEvent` extension).
3. Succession UI (heir reveal/choice + game-over screen, consuming `LastSuccession`/`EvaluateSuccession`/`LineageOverReason`).

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Rivalry-at-Bat Feed Flag ‚úÖ (Sonnet 5 ‚Äî item 2 of the queued list)

Scope capped at exactly the queued item: extend `NpcPaFeedEvent` so the attended-game feed flags a PA against a rival, same low-blast-radius pattern as the original NPC feed. Did not touch event-choice UI or succession UI (items 1 and 3, still open). **`MonteCarloHarness` 121/121 (was 120, +1); `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22 (boundary scan re-verified since Baseball-side doc comments moved); `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err across all 6 projects; headless boot against the real dev save clean (schema v5, day 38, relationships 0, gritty events 11).** No schema change, no new query, no new node ‚Äî pure UI/sim-glue.

**The wire:** `MicroGame.PlayHalfInning` already computes a per-PA `byte rivalry` (the same value driving the Phase 6 `RivalryEffects` ratings boost) once per plate appearance, in scope right through the existing `FeedSink.PublishNpcPa(...)` call at the PA boundary. `NpcPaFeedEvent` (`InteractiveBatterPolicy.cs`) gained a trailing `bool IsRivalryPa` field/ctor param ‚Äî the one production call site now passes `rivalry != 0`, so the flag is exactly "this PA's ratings were actually boosted," not a separately-defined notion of rivalry. Zero extra lookups, zero extra allocation ‚Äî the byte was already being read.

**UI (`AttendedGameScreen.cs`):** new `[Export] string NpcRivalryPaLineFormat` (default `"RIVAL {0}: {1}"`) alongside the existing `NpcPaLineFormat`, per `ui_conventions.md`'s "player-facing text lives on exported properties" rule. The NPC-feed dequeue loop in `_Process` picks the format by `npcPa.IsRivalryPa` before calling `AppendPlayLine` ‚Äî same call shape as before, one ternary added. No `.tscn` edit needed (neither format string was ever overridden there; both ride the C# default like `NpcPaLineFormat` always has).

**Harness (`MonteCarloHarness` suite 8, +1 check):** `PlayMicroGame` gained a trailing optional `PlayerIntentBridge? feedSink = null` (all three existing positional call sites untouched). New check (f) replays the suite's existing heated matchup (away lineup √ó home rotation/bullpen at intensity 100) with a bridge attached: away batters facing the home pitching staff are the ledger's rivalry side (always flagged), home batters facing the away pitcher were never entered into that ledger (never flagged) ‚Äî one game proves both bit states land correctly, cheaper than a separate control-game run.

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) the flag is UI-only, same as the rest of `NpcPaFeedEvent` ‚Äî it never round-trips into `Game_Logs` or any DB write. (2) No `CareerManager.Rivalries` proxy was added (unlike `FeedSink`, which `CareerManager` already forwards to `_micro`) ‚Äî out of scope for this slice since the harness proof works directly against `MicroGame`; a future pass wiring rivalries into a live `CareerManager`-driven attended game would need that proxy first. (3) `NpcRivalryPaLineFormat`'s default (`"RIVAL {0}: {1}"`) is unplaytested first-pass copy, trivially reskinned later per `ui_conventions.md`.

**Next steps (model assignments, same cost logic):**

1. Event-choice UI (render a fired event's choices for the avatar instead of autopilot) ‚Äî scene transport needs pinning first, per `gritty_event_framework.md` ¬ß9: **Sonnet 5**.
2. Succession UI (heir reveal/choice + game-over screen, consuming `LastSuccession`/`EvaluateSuccession`/`LineageOverReason`): **Sonnet 5**.
3. `RivalryEffects` ¬±8 retune after playtesting (unchanged, calibrated-core data behind the suite-8 band check): **Fable 5**.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Event-Choice UI & Succession UI ‚úÖ (both queued Sonnet 5 items)

Both items from the standing model-assignment list, built together since they share the same overlay/gating infrastructure. Planned via a full plan-mode pass first ‚Äî a Plan-agent pressure test read `CareerManager.cs`/`EventConsequenceApplier.cs`/both harnesses directly against the proposed design and caught one real bug before any code was written (below). **All suites green: `GrittyEventsHarness` 44/44 (was 39, +5 ‚Äî new pause/resolve/forfeit section), `MonteCarloHarness` 126/126 (was 121, +5 ‚Äî equivalence checks woven into the existing NotTriggered/GameOver√ó3/Succeeded fixtures, no new scratch db), `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `NeedsDecayHarness` 49/49, `SchemaValidator` 58/58; `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err across all 6 projects; headless boot via the godot MCP against the real dev save clean ‚Äî `day 38 ‚Ä¶ avatar 513568b0‚Ä¶, gritty events 11 (dispatcher polling)`, several seconds of live `_Process` polling on both new overlay scripts with zero runtime errors, clean stop.**

**The one real bug the plan-mode pressure test caught:** forfeiting a stale, unresolved pending succession choice by replaying its *stored* heir id through `Succeed()` can throw ‚Äî `Succeed()` independently re-validates willingness/age/rostered-state against LIVE data, and anything about that heir could have changed during the unresolved season (a Gritty Event dropping their interest, say). Fixed by having a stale-forfeit just re-run `RunSuccessionCheck()` fresh against current state instead (evaluates + applies in one already-proven step ‚Äî cannot throw from staleness).

**Event-choice UI:**

- **The schema had zero player-facing text anywhere** ‚Äî events/choices only ever carried machine ids (`back_alley_bribe`/`take_the_envelope`). Added optional `"prompt"` (event)/`"label"` (choice) JSON properties, parsed into new `GrittyEventDefinition.Prompt`/`EventChoice.Label` fields, falling back to a humanized version of the id (new `GrittyEventJson.Humanize`) when a batch omits them ‚Äî additive, so no existing harness fixture needed touching. Authored real prompt/label text into both `core_events.json` and `career_arc_events.json` (11 events) so the shipped UI isn't placeholder copy.
- **`EventConsequenceApplier`** gained `AutopilotAvatarChoices` (mirrors `CareerManager.AutopilotAttendedGames` exactly ‚Äî default true, headless/harness callers untouched) and a `GameStateQueries` constructor dependency ‚Äî deliberately **not** a `CareerManager` reference, which would have dragged the whole Baseball dependency graph into `GrittyEventsHarness`'s narrow compile surface (Data/Core/Life/Narrative + one cherry-picked `RngState.cs`, by design). The applier instead reads `GameStateKeys.AvatarPlayerId` directly ‚Äî mirroring how `EventDispatcher`'s own poll side already does this ‚Äî and compares it against `fired.SubjectPlayerId` (required, since an `EventScope.Any` event can roll the avatar as its subject by chance; scope alone can't gate this). `OnFired`'s existing consequence-application body moved verbatim into `ApplyChoice(fired, definition, choiceIndex)`; when the subject is the avatar and autopilot is off, the fire parks as a `PendingGrittyChoice` instead of resolving inline (forfeiting any still-unresolved prior one to its own autopilot draw first ‚Äî safe, since consequence application has no staleness-sensitive preconditions, unlike `Succeed`). New surface: `HasPendingChoice`/`TryGetPendingChoice`/`ResolveChoice(int)`.
- `GameManager`: `_grittyApplier` (private) ‚Üí `GrittyEventChoices` (public property, matching `Career`/`League`/`Micro`/`Relationships`'s existing style); constructor gains `GameState`; `AutopilotAvatarChoices = false` set right after construction ‚Äî the only place this flips.
- `Assets/UI/EventChoiceScreen.tscn`/`.cs` (new): thin `Control`/`VBoxContainer` slice, dirty-flag `_Process` (rebuilds choice buttons only when the pending fire's identity changes, never every idle frame), one button per `Choices[i].Label`, press ‚Üí `ResolveChoice(i)`.
- `GrittyEventsHarness` gained a new pause/resolve/forfeit section (+5 checks): avatar fires pause while an NPC fire on the same applier instance still auto-resolves; a stale unresolved choice forfeits deterministically (a zero-weight alternate choice makes the autopilot pick unambiguous) the moment a second avatar fire needs the slot; `ResolveChoice` applies and clears pending; `ResolveChoice` with nothing pending throws.

**Succession UI:**

- **`CareerManager.EvaluateSuccession()` collapsed every willing/of-age child down to just the single best-by-rating pick** ‚Äî no data existed for a UI to show the player *other* eligible heirs. Added `EvaluateSuccession(List&lt;HeirCandidate&gt; eligibleHeirs)`: the verbatim existing method body plus exactly one additive `eligibleHeirs.Add(...)` line at the point where a candidate is already confirmed to compete for `bestSum`/`bestHeirId` ‚Äî the zero-arg overload becomes a one-line wrapper over a scratch buffer. Proven behavior-identical, not just by inspection: the full 3-generation exit-criteria suite and every NotTriggered/GameOver-reason/Succeeded fixture in `MonteCarloHarness` now also calls the list overload right alongside the existing zero-arg calls and asserts the outcomes match exactly ‚Äî all 126 checks green, none of the pre-existing ones touched or re-authored.
- Added `AutopilotSuccession` (default true, same convention), `PersistGameOver(reason)` factored out of `RunSuccessionCheck` (shared by both the autopilot and interactive paths), and `HasPendingSuccessionChoice`/`TryGetPendingSuccessionChoice`/`ResolvePendingSuccession(heirId)`. `OnSeasonRolledOver`'s new interactive branch: `NotTriggered` ‚Üí no-op; `GameOver` ‚Üí applies immediately (there's no choice to make on a game-over); `Succeeded` ‚Üí parks every eligible candidate for the UI. A season rolling over on top of an already-unresolved pending choice re-runs `RunSuccessionCheck()` fresh rather than replaying the stale snapshot (the bug fix above) and treats that as the full succession handling for the tick.
- `GameManager`: `Career.AutopilotSuccession = false;` after construction ‚Äî headless/harness callers construct their own `CareerManager` and never touch the flag (confirmed via grep: `MonteCarloHarness` only ever calls `RunSuccessionCheck()`, so its default `true` autopilot is unaffected).
- `Assets/UI/SuccessionScreen.tscn`/`.cs` (new): two mutually-exclusive sub-panels ‚Äî a heir-reveal/choice panel (one dynamically-spawned button per `HeirCandidate`, showing name/age/revealed interest/headline ratings, press ‚Üí `ResolvePendingSuccession`) and a persistent game-over banner (`[Export]` text per `LineageFailure` reason) shown whenever `IsLineageOver` ‚Äî deliberately doesn't stop or pause the sim (the prior "stopping is the UI's call when it lands" deferral, Phase 6 entry, still stands; this is a notice, not a game-over flow).

**Shared wiring:**

- `Assets/Main.tscn`/`Main.cs`: introduced a `ScreenContainer` node that now owns just the swappable New-Game/Attended-Game screen (the free/re-add loop retargeted to it); `EventChoiceScreen` and `SuccessionScreen` are permanent siblings under `Main`, declared after it in the `.tscn` for draw order, each fully self-driven ‚Äî no coordination needed from `Main.cs` beyond being instantiated once at boot.
- `Assets/UI/AttendedGameScreen.cs`: `SetDayControlsEnabled`'s scattered call sites replaced with one unified `RefreshDayControlsEnabled()` called every `_Process` frame ‚Äî Play/Skip are disabled while a game is in flight (unchanged behavior) OR while either overlay has something pending, so a player cannot advance the day out from under an unresolved choice. This is what actually closes the "silent forfeit" gap in practice ‚Äî the backend forfeit-to-autopilot logic in both engine classes becomes a defensive safety net rather than the primary UX.

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) the `prompt`/`label` humanized-id fallback means a future content batch that omits them degrades gracefully rather than failing to load. (2) No "let autopilot decide this one" button on the event-choice screen ‚Äî every avatar-subject fire must be answered once the UI is live. (3) A pending choice of either kind is in-memory only; an unresolved one at quit is simply lost (same precedent as stress/cooldowns) ‚Äî the day-advance gate mitigates but doesn't eliminate this. (4) The two overlays are independent and can rarely show simultaneously (a gritty choice and a succession choice landing the same day) ‚Äî no z-order/queueing built. (5) An avatar event-choice can appear as an overlay while an attended game is already in flight, since the dispatcher polls independently of which screen is active ‚Äî the underlying at-bat keeps running on its own background task underneath. (6) Neither new screen's visuals/copy have been playtested ‚Äî first-pass thin slices, matching every prior UI phase's precedent.

**Next steps (model assignments, same cost logic):**

1. **`RivalryEffects` ¬±8 retune after playtesting** (unchanged, calibrated-core data behind the suite-8 band check): **Fable 5.**
2. **Stress persistence** (additive schema v6 ‚Äî bump the three DB-touching harnesses' hardcoded `user_version` checks, the known gotcha) and the **`ConceiveChild`/marriage consequence** (partner-target semantics need a design pass) ‚Äî both unchanged, deferred until prioritized: **Fable 5.**
3. Once there's real play feel to judge against: revisit the event-choice/succession screens' first-pass copy and layout, and consider whether players want an "autopilot this one" escape hatch on the event-choice screen: **Sonnet 5.**

Standing rule regardless of model: re-run `run_monte_carlo_batch` after anything that compiles into the sim assembly; escalate to Fable 5 if any band moves.

---

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî `RivalryEffects` Calibration Groundwork ‚úÖ (Fable 5 ‚Äî data pass, NO constant changed; retune decision staged for playtest)

The queued retune item is gated on play feel, which doesn't exist yet ‚Äî so this session produced the calibration data the decision needs, leaving the shipped ¬±8 untouched. **Working tree ends byte-identical to where it started (`RivalryModifiers.cs` clean vs git; MonteCarloHarness re-confirmed 126/126).** Method: a scratchpad sweep tool compiling the production `AtBatResolver.cs` directly (analytic 7-outcome distributions, no sampling noise), plus three temporary-edit-and-revert harness runs at boost 12/16/24 to probe the suite-8 season bands with the real 45-rivalry season.

**Finding 1 ‚Äî at organic intensities the shipped ¬±8 is imperceptible.** The content writers create rivalries at intensity 35‚Äì60 (`beanball_grudge` ‚àí35, `defy_them` ‚àí50, career-arc ‚àí60; intensity = ‚àíaffinity), deepening only on repeat fires. At boost 8/intensity 50 the flat-matchup shift is K +0.68pp, HR +0.06pp ‚Äî over a full season series vs one rival (~50 PA) that's **0.3 extra strikeouts and 0.03 extra home runs**. Even at intensity 100 it's 0.7 K / 0.06 HR per 50 PA. Nobody will ever feel the current tuning; it's mechanically real (harness-provable divergence) but perceptually zero.

**Finding 2 ‚Äî league calibration is NOT the binding constraint; the boost can go much higher than expected.** Rival-pair sparsity insulates the league line almost completely: the 45-max-intensity-rivalry season prints .247/.316/.411 at boost 8, .247/.316/.411 at 16, and still .247/.315/.411 at **24** (per-PA K% 22.5‚Üí26.8 at full intensity). The doc comment's "league line essentially unmoved" holds at 3√ó the shipped value.

**Finding 3 ‚Äî the suite-8 band check, not the calibration, is what breaks first, and it breaks as a seed artifact.** The check re-tests the *absolute* ¬ß8 bands on the divergent rivalry season, and this seed's control R/G sits at 4.20‚Äì4.21 against the 4.2 floor ‚Äî zero slack. Any constant change resamples the same-seed season and coin-flips R/G: boost 12 ‚Üí 4.19 (fail), 16 ‚Üí 4.195‚Äì4.199 (prints 4.20, fails), 24 ‚Üí 4.20 (fails). Non-monotonic, pure sampling noise around the floor. **When the retune lands, suite 8 should switch from absolute bands to a rivalry-vs-control delta bound (e.g. |ŒîR/G| ‚â§ 0.05, |ŒîAVG| ‚â§ .003) ‚Äî the property it actually wants ("rivalries don't move the league") ‚Äî plus the hardcoded `50‚Üí54 at intensity 50` fixture updated for the new constant.**

**Finding 4 ‚Äî symmetric boosts are net pitcher-favored; asymmetry is the second retune lever.** Batter-only +8 is OPS +.027, pitcher-only +8 is OPS ‚àí.037; both together net **‚àí.011** (‚àí.023 at ¬±16) because stuff hits K% harder than power lifts HR/XBH through the ¬ß4.1 weights. If playtest verdict is "rivalries should feel dangerous" the symmetric shape is right; if it's "the player should rise to the moment," retune shape (e.g. +12 power/+6 stuff) matters more than magnitude. Cap note: full effect holds up to rating 92 at boost 8, 84 at 16 (clamp-at-100 compresses star-vs-star rivalries above that).

**Staged recommendation (pending play feel):** raise to ¬±16 (full-intensity K 22.5‚Üí25.3%, HR 3.20‚Üí3.45%, 1B 14.3‚Üí13.0% ‚Äî a shift a player can actually notice across an attended season series) and convert the suite-8 season check to delta-vs-control in the same commit. Keep symmetry unless playtest says otherwise.

**Also observed (needs a look, pre-existing):** suite 7's "scripted UI drives a full interactive game over the bridge" check flaked once on unchanged code (4 PA/20 pitches/19 snapshots ‚Äî a dropped snapshot, then green on re-run), and its passing pitch counts vary run-to-run (27, 25) ‚Äî the scripted-UI thread handshake is timing-sensitive. First spurious failure observed; if it recurs, the bridge check needs a determinism pass. **Sonnet 5** to investigate if it bites again (harness-side, low blast radius) ‚Äî escalate to Fable 5 only if the fix touches `PlayerIntentBridge` itself.

**Next steps (model assignments, same cost logic):**

1. **Playtest verdict on rivalry feel** (user) ‚Üí apply the staged ¬±16 + suite-8 delta-check retune above: **Fable 5** (one constant pair + one harness check rewrite; the sweep data in this entry is the justification trail).
2. **Stress persistence v6** + **`ConceiveChild`/marriage consequence** ‚Äî unchanged, deferred until prioritized: **Fable 5.**
3. Event-choice/succession screens' copy/layout pass once there's play feel: **Sonnet 5.**

Standing rule regardless of model: re-run `run_monte_carlo_batch` after anything that compiles into the sim assembly; escalate to Fable 5 if any band moves.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Marriage & Conception DESIGN DOC done (Opus 4.8, design only ‚Äî NO code): `docs/design/marriage_and_conception.md`

The deferred `ConceiveChild`/marriage consequence from `gritty_event_framework.md` ¬ß4/¬ß9 + `heir_mechanics.md` ¬ß11.1/¬ß11.2 ‚Äî the writers that drive the already-built heir seam from live play. Design only, per the Opus architecture lane; no code this pass. **No schema change.**

**The load-bearing constraint that forced the shape (¬ß2):** `GrittyEventsHarness.csproj` compiles Narrative against Data+Core+Life+`RngState.cs` ONLY ‚Äî never the Baseball assembly (verified). `ConceiveChild` is in `CareerManager` (Baseball). So the applier physically **cannot** call it ‚Äî a direct call drags the whole Baseball graph into that harness's compile surface and breaks it. **Conception must route Narrative ‚Üí Core `EventBus` event ‚Üí Baseball `CareerManager` subscriber**, the exact sanctioned pattern of `StressImpulseEvent` (Narrative‚Üíbus‚ÜíLife) and `RivalryChangedEvent` (Life‚Üíbus‚ÜíBaseball). Bonus: same clean test split as the rivalry writer ‚Äî `GrittyEventsHarness` proves the request is *published* (no Baseball compiled); `MonteCarloHarness` proves `CareerManager` *services* it.

**Two engine capabilities, orthogonal:**

1. **Marriage = reuse the existing `relationship` consequence** with `kind: partner`, `target: league` (first pass ‚Äî every entity is a ballplayer, so `league` is the only sane spouse pool; a partner with a `Player_Ratings` row IS the two-parent bloodline path `heir_mechanics.md` ¬ß2.3 designed but couldn't reach), **+ a `Partner`-kind exclusivity guard** in `ApplyRelationship` (~6 lines: skip if the subject already has any `Partner` edge, so `FindPartnerId` stays unambiguous and repeat/scope-any fires can't accrete spouses). No new enum, no schema.
2. **Conception = new closed-enum `ConsequenceKind.ConceiveChild`**, JSON `{ "type": "conceive_child" }`, payload-free. **Load-time gate: valid only on `scope: avatar`** (only the avatar has a tracked bloodline) ‚Äî rejected loudly at parse time otherwise, so the apply path is total.

**The apply-time hop + the ordering hazard it closes (¬ß4.2):** the applier resolves the avatar's co-parent from the **live in-memory `RelationshipGraph`** (the same object that authored the marriage this session) and publishes `ChildConceptionRequestedEvent(avatarId, partnerId?, day)`. Resolving from the graph ‚Äî NOT the DB ‚Äî sidesteps a real hazard: `ConceiveChild.FindPartnerId` reads the *database*, but a `Partner` edge authored this session only persists on GameManager's day-cadence flush, so a same-session marry-then-baby could miss it. Passing the id IN the request makes conception flush-order-independent. Deferred publish drains on a later pump, outside the applier's committed batch ‚Üí no shared/nested transaction with the Baseball write.

**Baseball consumer (¬ß4.3):** `CareerManager` (already bus-subscribed for DayAdvanced/SeasonRolledOver) adds a `ChildConceptionRequestedEvent` handler ‚Äî no-op unless the request's avatar is still current (drops stale requests for a since-retired avatar), generates names (surname = avatar's bloodline surname, first name from a new `LeagueGenerator.GenerateName(ref rng)` using `_rng`), calls `ConceiveChild` with a NEW explicit `string? partnerId` param (non-null ‚Üí skip `FindPartnerId`; null ‚Üí unchanged DB path for harness/direct callers), then publishes `ChildBornEvent(childId, avatarId, partnerId, day)` as the feed/notification seam (shipped-before-consumer, mirrors `GrittyEventResolvedEvent`/`LastSuccession`). Conception has NO exclusivity ‚Äî multiple kids are the wanted `NoWillingHeir` hedge (`heir_mechanics.md` ¬ß6); pacing is content's job.

**The arc is content, not engine (¬ß5):** no hard-coded marriage‚Üíbaby sequence. Content composes it via the existing flag cascade (`min_days_since`), same as bribe‚Üísyndicate: `met_someone` (writes partner + `married` flag) ‚Üí `starting_a_family` at +365 (`expecting`) ‚Üí `child_is_born` at +270 (`conceive_child` + clear `expecting` so it repeats for a 2nd child). Flags round-trip through `Entity_Flags` and survive saves; `cooldown_days` alone wouldn't.

**¬ß8 MODEL SPLIT:** **Fable 5** = engine plumbing (2 Core events, the consequence type + parse + avatar-scope rejection, applier partner-resolution/publish + `Partner` exclusivity guard, `CareerManager` subscriber + `GenerateName` + `ConceiveChild` partnerId overload + `ChildBornEvent`, harness checks 1‚Äì9 incl. the "no ¬ß8 band moved" reconfirm ‚Äî career-wiring/calibration-adjacent, same reason succession was Fable's). **Sonnet 5** = the ¬ß5 event-arc JSON + prompt/label copy + `check_event_graph_integrity`, and later the birth-feed UI once `ChildBornEvent` has a consumer. Deferred (¬ß9): civilian spouse pool / eligible-singles filter, divorce/re-marriage, partner‚Üíneeds/stress coupling, twins/birth-age payloads, naming UI.

**Next steps (model assignments):**

1. **Implement marriage & conception** from this doc ‚Äî **Fable 5** engine plumbing (checks 1‚Äì9), then **Sonnet 5** content arc. Genuinely unblocked, no playtest gate. ‚úÖ Fable half done same day (entry below); Sonnet content arc still open.
2. **Stress persistence v6** (additive schema ‚Äî bump the three harnesses' hardcoded `user_version` checks) ‚Äî **Fable 5**, when prioritized.
3. **Playtest verdict ‚Üí staged `RivalryEffects` ¬±16 + suite-8 delta-check retune** (data/justification in the prior entry) ‚Äî **Fable 5**.
4. Event-choice/succession screens' copy/layout pass once there's play feel ‚Äî **Sonnet 5.**

Standing rule regardless of model: re-run `run_monte_carlo_batch` after anything that compiles into the sim assembly; escalate to Fable 5 if any band moves.
