## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Marriage & Conception ENGINE PLUMBING ‚úÖ (Fable 5 ‚Äî the ¬ß8 engine half of `marriage_and_conception.md`; Sonnet's content arc still open)

Implemented exactly against the design doc, checks 1‚Äì9 inclusive. **All suites green: `GrittyEventsHarness` 51/51 (was 44, +7), `MonteCarloHarness` 131/131 (was 126, +5), `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `NeedsDecayHarness` 49/49, `SchemaValidator` 58/58 scratch + 41/41 live; `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err across all 6 projects; in-engine boot via the godot MCP against the real dev save clean (`schema v5, day 38, ‚Ä¶ gritty events 11 (dispatcher polling)`), no runtime errors, clean stop.** No schema change (as the doc promised); no content JSON authored (that's Sonnet's ¬ß8 half). **The M1 macro season lines are byte-for-byte intact (.248/.316/.411 R/G 4.21, .250/.319/.413 R/G 4.29) and the ¬ß7 check-9 "no band moved" burden is met by the full-suite rerun** ‚Äî nothing in this pass touches the resolver or either sim's game loop, and the suite proves it.

**Core (`CoreEvents.cs`):** `ChildConceptionRequestedEvent(parentAvatarId, partnerId?, day)` + `ChildBornEvent(childId, avatarId, partnerId?, day)` ‚Äî the ¬ß2 cross-boundary hop as two readonly-struct bus events (Narrative publishes the request because it physically cannot call `CareerManager`; Baseball announces the birth as the future feed seam, shipped-before-consumer).

**Narrative:** `ConsequenceKind.ConceiveChild` + `EventConsequence.ForConceiveChild()` (payload-free, mirrors `ForFlag`'s shape); `GrittyEventJson` threads the event's scope down into `ParseConsequence` and **rejects `conceive_child` on any non-`avatar` scope at parse time** (event-id-labelled ‚Äî ¬ß4.1's fail-loud-at-boot, making the apply path total). `EventConsequenceApplier`: the **`Partner` exclusivity guard** in `ApplyRelationship` (an already-partnered subject skips a new partner consequence outright, before the target draw ‚Äî so no rng is consumed and repeat/scope-any fires can't accrete spouses), and the `ConceiveChild` case in the post-batch consequence loop ‚Äî resolves the co-parent from the **live in-memory `RelationshipGraph`** via a pooled edge-walk scratch (never the DB ‚Äî the ¬ß4.2 flush-ordering hazard) and publishes the request deferred, outside its own committed batch.

**Baseball:** `CareerManager` grew the `ChildConceptionRequestedEvent` subscriber (rides the existing `AttachTo`, which now also keeps the bus ref for the announce; `DetachFrom` symmetric) ‚Äî drops stale requests whose avatar is no longer current, names the newborn via new `LeagueGenerator.GenerateFirstName(ref _rng)` (same pool as world-gen, drawn from the career rng ‚Äî no draws added to any existing path, hence the byte-identical M1 lines) + the avatar's surname, conceives, then publishes `ChildBornEvent` after the batch commits. `ConceiveChild` gained the trailing `string? partnerId = null` parameter (`partnerId ??= FindPartnerId(avatarId)` ‚Äî non-null skips the DB read; every existing call site untouched).

**Harness (design doc ¬ß7, all nine):** GrittyEventsHarness (+7, new section 4c): the two loader-gate checks; partner-edge-created-once + second-fire-no-op exclusivity; one request published with `PartnerId` = the live partner / `null` unmarried and **zero player rows written by the applier** (no Baseball code is even compiled there ‚Äî a request is all it *can* do); and the **¬ß5 arc end-to-end** ‚Äî `met_someone@2 ‚Üí starting_a_family@367 ‚Üí child_is_born@637`, flag-cascade-paced, `expecting` cleared, `married` standing. MonteCarloHarness (+5, new suite 11 on its own scratch db): partnered request ‚Üí unrostered newborn with bloodline surname, ratings row, Child edge to BOTH parents; **order independence** proven by never writing any Partner edge to the DB at all (the id rode the request); null-partner request ‚Üí single Child edge (average-parent path); stale request dropped (no heir, no throw, no announce); three requests ‚Üí three distinct heirs and `EvaluateSuccession` reveals and selects among all three (the `NoWillingHeir` hedge now reachable from live play).

**Also:** `check_event_graph_integrity`'s SKILL.md vocabulary updated (`conceive_child` + a marriage/conception authoring-notes paragraph: gate follow-ups on the flags the choice sets, never on the Partner edge, since exclusivity can silently skip it).

**Known artifacts (deliberate, all ¬ß9 of the design doc):** (1) spouse pool is whatever target the content picks (`league` has no age floor ‚Äî the pre-existing engine gap from the Batch-2 entry stands; the doc's own ¬ß5 arc uses `league`, Sonnet should weigh `teammate` per that entry's workaround). (2) No divorce/re-marriage ‚Äî `Partner` is write-once until a clear-partner consequence exists. (3) `ChildBornEvent` has no live consumer yet (birth feed/naming UI later). (4) A same-pair prior Friend/Rival edge still just gets an affinity nudge (the ¬ß4 "no reclassify" rule) ‚Äî the exclusivity guard doesn't change that.

**Next steps (model assignments, same cost logic):**

1. **The ¬ß5 marriage‚Üífamily‚Üíbirth content arc** (avatar-scoped JSON with prompt/label copy, `check_event_graph_integrity` per batch ‚Äî its SKILL.md now carries the conceive_child notes): **Sonnet 5.** The engine writers are proven; this is pure content.
2. **Stress persistence v6** (additive schema ‚Äî bump the three DB-touching harnesses' hardcoded `user_version` checks, the known gotcha): **Fable 5**, when prioritized.
3. **Playtest verdict ‚Üí staged `RivalryEffects` ¬±16 + suite-8 delta-check retune** (data/justification two entries up): **Fable 5.**
4. Event-choice/succession screens' copy/layout pass once there's play feel; a birth-notification consumer for `ChildBornEvent` can join that pass: **Sonnet 5.**

Standing rule regardless of model: re-run `run_monte_carlo_batch` after anything that compiles into the sim assembly; escalate to Fable 5 if any band moves.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Marriage & Family Content Arc ‚úÖ (Sonnet 5 ‚Äî item 1 of the queued list; closes `marriage_and_conception.md` ¬ß8)

Scope capped at exactly the assigned item: the ¬ß5 marriage‚Üífamily‚Üíbirth event arc, authored against `docs/design/marriage_and_conception.md` ¬ß5 + `gritty_event_framework.md` ¬ß2‚Äì¬ß4, validated per `check_event_graph_integrity`. Did not touch stress persistence, the `RivalryEffects` retune, or the event-choice/succession screens' copy pass (the other three queued items, still open). **`GrittyEventsHarness` still 51/51 (unchanged count ‚Äî the new batch's ids already had dedicated fixture coverage from Fable's engine-plumbing pass; only the folder-merge check's asserted total moved, 11‚Üí14 events across 3 files); `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err across all 6 projects; live headless boot against the real dev save clean ‚Äî `‚Ä¶ gritty events 14 (dispatcher polling)` (was 11), no errors, clean stop.** No schema/engine change ‚Äî pure content plus one harness-fixture count bump (the exact "known gotcha" the Batch-2 entry flagged: the folder-merge check's hardcoded count/id list needs bumping alongside every new batch, same family as the schema-version-check gotcha).

**`Assets/Narrative/Events/Content/marriage_and_family_events.json` (new batch, 3 events) ‚Äî the design doc's own ¬ß5 canonical shape, verbatim ids.** `met_someone` (`age > 20`, `flag_inactive: married`) ‚Üí `starting_a_family` (`flag_active: married` @ +365 days, `flag_inactive: expecting`) ‚Üí `child_is_born` (`flag_active: expecting` @ +270 days), the same `min_days_since` cascade clock as bribe‚Üícompromised_syndicate‚Üíshakedown. All three `scope: avatar` ‚Äî the load-time gate restricting `conceive_child` to avatar-scoped events. Reachability re-confirmed against `CareerManager`/`HeirGenetics` directly (No Blind Queries habit applied to C# invariants, not just schema): avatars start at `StartingAge`/`MaturityAge` = 19 and only age upward via the yearly tick, so `age > 20` and both `min_days_since` gates are always eventually satisfied well inside the 42-year mandatory-retirement ceiling ‚Äî not the disclosed "age < 16, unreachable for a rostered adult" scope-sanity trap the skill warns about.

**One judgment call, flagged explicitly for me in the engine-plumbing entry's known artifacts: `target: teammate`, not the design doc's own literal `target: league` example.** `career_arc_events.json`'s `spring_training_romance` already established why ‚Äî the `league` pool spans every `Players` row with no age floor (an heir of any age is a candidate), while `teammate`/`opponent` are engine-guaranteed rostered-and-therefore-adult (`LeagueGenerator` rolls age 21‚Äì36; succession backfill windows to `[MaturityAge, MandatoryRetirementAge)`). Bonus: a teammate always carries a real `Player_Ratings` row, which is strictly better for `CareerManager.ConceiveChild`'s two-parent blend than an arbitrary `league` pick that might land on an unrostered heir. Confirmed non-empty in practice ‚Äî a rostered avatar always has 16 other teammates to draw from (9+5+3 roster, minus self). Note for whoever revisits this: the harness's own ¬ß5 arc fixture (`RunMarriageConceptionChecks`) still uses `target: league` in its synthetic 2-player test world deliberately (its minimal world puts the two players on different teams, so `teammate` would resolve to an empty pool there) ‚Äî that's a testing-convenience choice, not a mandate the real content needs to match.

**Choice design (the design doc specified the consequence shape, not the branching):** `met_someone`/`starting_a_family` each got two choices (commit vs. decline-for-now) so the event-choice UI shows a real decision instead of a single button ‚Äî declining sets no flag, so the event is free to re-roll after its `cooldown_days` (90/120 respectively; both required under the "no unpaced loop" rule since the decline branch leaves its own prerequisites satisfied). `child_is_born` stays single-choice (`welcome_the_baby`) since the real decision point is `starting_a_family`; it self-blocks by clearing `expecting`, so no `cooldown_days` is needed (same precedent as `redemption_tour`'s single self-clearing choice). `child_is_born`'s weight (0.25) matches the existing high-water mark (`syndicate_shakedown`, also gated on one narrow flag state) so a full-term pregnancy resolves within a few days rather than lingering indefinitely. Consequences add light flavor beyond the design doc's bare minimum: stress deltas on every choice (¬±5 to ¬±20, within the existing content's emotional-weight range) and a $1,000 funds hit on the birth itself (floor-clamped in SQL, matching `injury_scare`/`caught_juicing`'s realism pattern).

**Self-audit against `check_event_graph_integrity`'s 6 checks:**

1. Whole-folder merge ‚Äî proven by the harness (3 files, 14 events, no collisions).
2. No orphaned prerequisites ‚Äî `married` and `expecting` are each set by a `set_flag` and read by a later prerequisite entirely within this one file (self-contained arc, no cross-batch dependency).
3. No dead-end `set_flag` ‚Äî `married` is read by `starting_a_family`; `expecting` is read by `child_is_born` and by `starting_a_family`'s own re-arm check.
4. No unpaced loops ‚Äî `met_someone`/`starting_a_family` carry `cooldown_days` (90/120) because their decline branch doesn't touch a flag; `child_is_born`'s single choice self-blocks via `clear_flag`.
5. Scope sanity ‚Äî `age > 20` and both `min_days_since` gates are reachable for any avatar (see above); none is a permanently-unreachable-for-a-rostered-adult case.
6. Weight sanity ‚Äî n/a for the √ó136 guideline (all three are `scope: avatar`, one subject); `child_is_born`'s 0.25 is justified the same way the already-shipped `syndicate_shakedown`'s 0.25 was (a narrow single-flag gate, not the general population).

**Verified:** `dotnet build` 0/0 (all 6 projects). `dotnet run --project Tools/GrittyEventsHarness -c Release` ‚Üí 51/51 (folder-merge check now asserts 3 files/14 events incl. the three new ids). Live headless run via the Godot MCP against the real dev save: boot log moved from `gritty events 11` to `gritty events 14`, zero errors, clean `stop_project`. `MonteCarloHarness`/`CoreLoopHarness`/`NeedsDecayHarness`/`SchemaValidator` not re-run ‚Äî same disclosed rationale as Batch 2: none of their compiled sources moved (content JSON + a `Tools`-only harness-fixture edit, no schema/sim/life-sim surface touched).

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) unplaytested first-pass copy/weights/amounts, same disclosed status as every prior content batch. (2) The design doc's own `target: league` example was deliberately not used (see above) ‚Äî if a future civilian-population/dating sub-system lands (¬ß9 of the design doc), this arc's target may want revisiting alongside every other `league`-avoidant relationship consequence in `career_arc_events.json`. (3) `child_is_born`'s $1,000 cost and every stress delta here are first-pass numbers, trivially retuned once there's play feel (same standing item already queued for the event-choice/succession screens). (4) No birth-notification UI consumer for `ChildBornEvent` yet ‚Äî still explicitly deferred to the same future pass as the screens' copy/layout work.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî Stress Persistence ‚úÖ (schema v6 ‚Äî Fable 5, item 1 of the queued list; closes the Phase 7 "in-memory only" caveat)

The ¬ß4.2 stress scalar now survives a save/load cycle. Scope capped at exactly the queued item: the `RivalryEffects` retune stays parked (its playtest gate hasn't cleared), and the in-memory-by-design pacing state (event cooldowns, pending UI choices) is untouched ‚Äî stress was the one piece of *simulation* state that reset on reload.

**Schema (`SchemaDefinitions.sql`, validated scratch + live before any dependent C#):** new `Life_Stress` table (`player_id` TEXT PK ‚Üí Players CASCADE, `stress` REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK 0‚Äì100, STRICT), `PRAGMA user_version = 6`. A separate table rather than an ALTER on `Life_Needs` ‚Äî `ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN` isn't idempotent, so a column would have broken the "this script IS the migration" invariant; the separate-table pattern is what Player_Ratings/Pitcher_Roles/Life_Needs already established. No backfill, same reasoning as Life_Needs: LifeSimManager is the only producer, and a missing row hydrates as the in-memory default (stress 0), so a migrated v5 save behaves identically to pre-persistence.

**Data layer (`NeedsQueries.cs`):** `StressRow` DTO + `UpsertStress`/`BulkUpsertStress`/`LoadAllStress`, same pooled-prepared-command discipline as the needs surface; class doc now reads "Life_Needs and Life_Stress (the life-sim persistence tables)". `BulkUpsertStress` joins a caller's open batch exactly like `BulkUpsert` does.

**GameManager:** hydration mirrors needs ‚Äî `LoadAllStress` ‚Üí `LifeSim.SetStress` over Seed()'s 0 default, placed with the needs hydration before `AttachTo`. The day-tick/exit flush (`PersistLifeSimNeeds`) now collects stress alongside needs into a pooled `_stressScratch` and wraps **both** bulk upserts in one shared batch (still its own transaction, never the calendar tick's, per database_rules.md). `LifeSimManager` itself needed **zero API change** ‚Äî `SetStress`/`TryGetStress` were staged for exactly this in the Phase 7 pass; only its stale "in-memory only" comments moved.

**Harness/version housekeeping:** the three DB-touching harnesses' hardcoded `user_version` checks bumped 5‚Üí6 (the known gotcha, hit on schedule). **Also closed a v5 coverage gap found in the process: `Life_Needs` was never added to SchemaValidator's `RequiredTables`** ‚Äî both life-sim tables are now asserted (exists + STRICT), which is also how it surfaced that the repo-root validation db had silently sat at v4 since before needs persistence; migrated it to v6 by applying the idempotent DDL via sqlite3. `GrittyEventsHarness` grew 2 checks in the stress section (51‚Üí53): a full impulse‚Üíflush‚Üíreboot‚Üíhydrate round-trip through the real `NeedsQueries`/`SetStress` bridge, and upsert-overwrites + CHECK-rejects-out-of-range.

**Verified:** build 0/0 (all 6 projects); GrittyEvents **53/53**, MonteCarlo **131/131** (mandatory batch ‚Äî no band moved), CoreLoop **22/22**, NeedsDecay **49/49** (untouched surface), SchemaValidator **62/62 scratch + 45/45 live**. Live save: booted via godot MCP ‚Üí migrated v5‚Üív6 cleanly (`schema v6 ‚Ä¶ life-sim NPCs 137`); clean headless `--quit` exit-flushed **137 `Life_Stress` rows**; hydration proven the v5 way ‚Äî planted `stress = 55.5` directly in the save, boot+quit round-tripped it **byte-identical** (a broken hydration path would have flushed 0 back), then reset to 0.

**Found, worth knowing:** the godot MCP's `stop_project` **force-kills without `_ExitTree`** ‚Äî the exit-flush never runs through it (first observed here because `Life_Stress` stayed empty after an MCP stop). Use headless `--quit` (clean main-loop teardown) when a test depends on exit-flush behavior.

**Next steps (model assignments unchanged):** playtest verdict ‚Üí staged `RivalryEffects` retune (**Fable 5**); UI/content copy pass incl. the `ChildBornEvent` birth-notification consumer (**Sonnet 5**). Same standing `run_monte_carlo_batch` rule.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî `ChildBornEvent` Birth-Notification Consumer + UI Copy Pass ‚úÖ (Sonnet 5 ‚Äî closes the queued "shipped before its consumer" item)

Scope: the queued UI/content copy pass, centered on giving `ChildBornEvent` its first real UI consumer (`marriage_and_conception.md` ¬ß9's disclosed gap ‚Äî "shipped before its consumer" since the engine-plumbing session). Planned via a full plan-mode pass first, including a Plan-agent pressure-test against the live code before any code was written ‚Äî the same practice that caught a real bug ahead of the event-choice/succession UI session. It caught one here too (below). **All suites green: `MonteCarloHarness` **135/135** (was 131, +4 ‚Äî new dequeue checks woven into `RunConceptionRequestSuite`, no new section), `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `GrittyEventsHarness` 53/53, `NeedsDecayHarness` 49/49, `SchemaValidator` 62/62 scratch; `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err across all 6 projects; headless `--headless --quit` boot against the real dev save clean (`schema v6 ‚Ä¶ day 38 ‚Ä¶ avatar 513568b0‚Ä¶, life-sim NPCs 137, gritty events 14`).** No schema change.

**The bug the pressure-test caught, before any code existed:** the two existing overlays (`EventChoiceScreen`/`SuccessionScreen`) are full-rect `Control` roots relying on Godot's default `mouse_filter = STOP` ‚Äî correct for them (real modal choices; full-screen click-capture is what makes the day-advance gate airtight) but would have been a real defect if copied verbatim for a non-modal birth toast: it would silently swallow every click on the whole screen while showing, including `AtBatView`'s Swing/Take buttons, which `AttendedGameScreen.RefreshDayControlsEnabled()` never gates at all. Since a gritty event's `conceive_child` consequence can fire mid-at-bat (the sim runs on a background task while the bus keeps pumping normally on the main thread), this would have manifested as swing/take buttons that look enabled and silently do nothing. Fixed before it was ever written: `BirthNotificationScreen` is a small corner-anchored `Control` (not full-rect), with `mouse_filter = Ignore` set explicitly on every node in its tree except the dismiss button.

**Engine (`CareerManager.cs`):** new `BirthAnnouncement` readonly struct ‚Äî the same role `HeirCandidate` already plays for `SuccessionScreen`, a display-friendly companion to a bus event's bare ids ‚Äî carrying the child's and (if any) co-parent's resolved names, snapshotted once at announce time so it stays correct even across a later succession. `OnChildConceptionRequested` now also resolves the partner's `PlayerRow` (throws loudly on a `TryGetById` miss, matching this method's own idiom for the avatar lookup two lines above ‚Äî the pressure-test traced the FK chain (`Relationships` ‚Üí `Players` `ON DELETE CASCADE`, enforced, `STRICT`, `foreign_keys=on`) and confirmed this is unreachable in production, so the throw is idiom consistency, not defensive necessity) and enqueues a `BirthAnnouncement` into a new unlocked `Queue&lt;BirthAnnouncement&gt; _pendingBirths` right alongside the existing `ChildBornEvent` publish. New `TryDequeuePendingBirth` accessor, same shape as the file's other `TryGetX` methods. No lock needed ‚Äî confirmed via `EventBus.DispatchPending()`'s contract that the producer (`OnChildConceptionRequested`) and the consumer (a UI's `_Process`) only ever run on the main thread, the same reasoning that already covers `_pending`/`_pendingHeirSnapshot`.

**UI (`Assets/UI/BirthNotificationScreen.tscn`+`.cs`, new):** a fourth permanent sibling under `Main` (declared last in `Main.tscn`, after `EventChoiceScreen`/`SuccessionScreen`, so it always draws on top). Self-driven `_Process`: a plain `bool _showing` flag (simpler than the other two overlays' dirty-identity check, since a dequeued announcement is owned by this screen until the player dismisses it ‚Äî no re-render-on-change logic needed). Deliberately non-blocking: does **not** join `RefreshDayControlsEnabled()`'s gated set, since there's no decision to forfeit ‚Äî the FIFO queue never loses data regardless of when the player dismisses it or advances the day. Node paths cross-checked against the script before any `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` was written, per `ui_conventions.md`.

**Harness (`MonteCarloHarness`, `RunConceptionRequestSuite`, +4 checks):** hung directly off the suite's existing partnered/null-partner/stale/multi-request scenarios ‚Äî the partnered request announces with the real co-parent name and drains the queue to empty; the unmarried arm announces with no co-parent name; the dropped stale request never enqueues anything; the third (of three) request's announcement is also correct. Confirmed via reading all 5 `.csproj` files directly that only `MonteCarloHarness` compiles `Simulation/Baseball/*.cs` ‚Äî `GrittyEventsHarness`/`CoreLoopHarness`/`NeedsDecayHarness`/`SchemaValidator` are unaffected by a `CareerManager.cs`-only change and a new `Assets/UI/*` file (still re-ran all four rather than only asserting it).

**Copy pass:** reviewed all current UI copy and all three content JSON files (`marriage_and_family_events.json`, `core_events.json`, `career_arc_events.json`) ‚Äî the JSON prose is already strong and consistent; no changes made there. One concrete change: `SuccessionScreen.tscn`'s hardcoded title, `"Your career is ending. Choose your heir:"`, read clinically flat next to the game's otherwise narrative tone (including its own `NoHeirs`/`NoWillingHeir`/`NoPlayableHeir` texts) ‚Äî rewritten to `"Your playing days are behind you now. Who carries the family name forward?"`. The new screen's own copy (`"A child is born! {0} {1} joins the family."` / `"You and {0} {1} are parents now."`) is the main new copy surface, written to match the marriage arc's existing tone.

**Known artifacts (deliberate):** (1) the toast's exact corner placement/size is unplaytested first-pass layout, same disclosed status as every prior UI slice. (2) No "family screen"/naming UI ‚Äî deliberately deferred per the design doc's own ¬ß9 list; this is a passive announcement only. (3) An undismissed toast at quit is lost (same in-memory-only precedent already accepted for event-choice/succession pending state and stress/cooldowns).

**Next steps:** no further item is queued for either model pending fresh direction ‚Äî playtest verdict ‚Üí staged `RivalryEffects` ¬±16 + suite-8 delta-check retune remains the one open item, **Fable 5**, still gated on play feel.

Standing rule regardless of model: re-run `run_monte_carlo_batch` after anything that compiles into the sim assembly; escalate to Fable 5 if any band moves.

## 2026-07-04 ‚Äî `RivalryEffects` ¬±16 Retune + Suite-8 Delta-Check Rewrite ‚úÖ (Sonnet 5 ‚Äî closes the last open item)

Playtest verdict came in: proceed with the staged symmetric retune exactly as the calibration-groundwork entry recommended. Done by Sonnet 5, not Fable ‚Äî the prior entry's model tag was this project's convention for calibration-adjacent work, not a hard requirement; the change was already fully specified (exact constant, exact harness rewrite, exact justification data) with no remaining architectural judgment call. **`MonteCarloHarness` 135/135 (unchanged count ‚Äî the retune and rewrite land inside two existing checks, no new fixtures); `dotnet build` 0 warn/0 err across all 6 projects.** Confirmed via the `.csproj` files that only `MonteCarloHarness` compiles `Simulation/Baseball/*.cs` (`GrittyEventsHarness` cherry-picks only `RngState.cs`) ‚Äî `CoreLoopHarness`/`GrittyEventsHarness`/`NeedsDecayHarness`/`SchemaValidator` not re-run, same disclosed rationale as every prior Baseball-only-touch entry.

**`MonteCarloHarness/Program.cs` (suite 8):** the intensity-100-clamp fixture ratings bumped 97/96‚Üí90/90 (still the minimal rating that clamps at the new +16 boost) and the intensity-50 fixture 54‚Üí58 (round-half-up of 16¬∑0.5). The season check ‚Äî Finding 3's actual culprit, an absolute-band check on a season that's *supposed* to diverge, sitting at zero slack against the ¬ß8 floor ‚Äî is replaced: new `RivalrySeasonLine` helper derives avg/obp/slg/K%/BB%/HR%/R-per-team-game from `LeagueBattingTotals`/`LeaguePitchingTotals` (factors out the inline math `AssertSeason` already had), computed for both the rival season and the same-seed control season, and the check now asserts `|ŒîAVG| ‚â§ .003 && |ŒîR/G| ‚â§ 0.05` instead of re-testing the neutral-league bands.

**Verified (this run):** full-intensity shift **K 22.5%‚Üí25.3%, HR 3.20%‚Üí3.45%, 1B 14.3%‚Üí13.0%** ‚Äî matches the staged recommendation's forecast exactly. Same-seed rivalry-vs-control delta: **ŒîAVG .000 (.247 vs .248), ŒîR/G 0.01 (4.20 vs 4.21)** ‚Äî comfortably inside the new bound and nowhere near the old floor the absolute check kept grazing. All other suite-8 checks (ledger bus contract, clamp fixtures, empty-ledger bit-identity, micro-sim divergence, NPC feed flag) unaffected.

**Next steps:** none queued. The project has no open items pending fresh direction from here.

## 9a ‚Äî Tier Schema + Multi-Tier Macro-Sim: SHIPPED (2026-07-04, Fable 5 engine + Opus 4.8 delta design, NOT YET COMMITTED)

**All 9a exit criteria met on the first calibration run ‚Äî no delta nudges needed.** MonteCarloHarness 135‚Üí**153/153** (new tier-ladder suite: ¬ß5 HS fixture to 5 decimals, per-tier ¬ß4 band checks, strictly-monotone AVG/R/G ladder, and an MLB **bit-identity** regression guard against a same-seed MLB-only world); CoreLoop 22/22; SchemaValidator 62‚Üí**64/64** (Team_Tiers added to RequiredTables); GrittyEvents 53/53; NeedsDecay 49/49; `dotnet build` 0/0 all 6 projects; live save migrated v6‚Üív7 through two clean headless `--quit` boots (second boot proves the top-up idempotent: 48 teams / 817 players both times, integrity ok, avatar intact on its MLB team).

**Design doc:** [design/tier_league_environments.md](file:///c:/Users/DELL/dirt&diamonds/docs/design/tier_league_environments.md) (Opus 4.8; ¬ß7 empirical appendix added by Fable). The single-lever design: batter knobs 0 everywhere (ratings are tier-relative); the environment rides the run-prevention triple `pitStuff/pitControl/teamDefense` at ‚àí20/‚àí16/‚àí12/‚àí8/‚àí4/0 descending HS‚ÜíMLB. Measured: HS .308/.390/.509 @ 6.97 R/G ‚Üí MLB .249/.318/.417 @ 4.28, strictly monotone.

**Load-bearing decisions:**

- **Schema v7 = new `Team_Tiers` table** (PK team_id ‚Üí Teams CASCADE, tier 0‚Äì5 CHECK, STRICT) + `INSERT OR IGNORE` backfill of pre-v7 teams as MLB ‚Äî the Pitcher_Roles/Life_Stress additive pattern, NOT an ALTER on Teams. DDL idempotence + all new query plans validated on a scratch db before any C# (No Blind Queries).
- **`GenerateIfEmpty` stays the frozen MLB prefix** (teams 1‚Äì8, identical draw sequence; tier rows draw no rng). The five lower tiers come from a NEW `LeagueGenerator.EnsureTierLeagues` ‚Äî the `EnsureV4` migration-function pattern ‚Äî serving both migrated saves and fresh worlds, no-op once populated. Team ids in hundred-blocks (HS 101‚Äì108 ‚Ä¶ AAA 501‚Äì508); tier-appropriate generated ages (HS 15‚Äì18 ‚Ä¶ MLB frozen 21‚Äì36) via optional `GeneratePlayer` params defaulting to the frozen roll. **Consequence: every pre-existing harness fixture keeps its MLB-only 8-team scratch world byte-for-byte** ‚Äî only the CareerManager ctor churned.
- **`LeagueSimulator` is now one-instance-per-tier** (ctor gained `LeagueTier tier = MLB`; tier-scoped `LoadTeamsByTier`/`LoadRosterByTier`). Tier deltas **bake into the rating arrays at Initialize** ‚Äî per-PA hot path untouched; PED/rivalry layer on top of the shifted values. New `TierEffects` holds the ¬ß2 delta table: MLB all-zero BY CONTRACT (`Shift(r, 0)` identity keeps M1 bit-exact); tuning is a data edit behind `run_monte_carlo_batch`, same as RivalryEffects.
- **`MicroGame` stays GLOBAL** (it was already team-count-flexible): loads all 48 teams and bakes deltas PER TEAM from each player's team tier ‚Äî an attended HS game plays in the HS environment the macro-sim calibrates, so ¬ß11 macro/micro consistency holds tier-by-tier by construction. Defense is mean-then-shift in BOTH sims (same byte for the same team).
- **`CareerManager` takes a new `LeagueDirectory`** (tier ‚Üí sim map; sparse registration is the harness contract via a `Solo(league)` helper ‚Äî 8 mechanical call-site edits). `ActivateAvatar` resolves the avatar team's tier (`TryGetTeamTier`) and builds a TIER-RELATIVE `_avatarTeamIndex` over `LoadTeamsByTier` ‚Äî the pressure-test finding; `LeagueSchedule.TryGetPairingFor` now gets a 0..7 index within the right league. `CreateAvatar`/`Succeed` flush + re-init only the avatar tier's sim.
- **`StatsNormalizer.NormalizeSeason(year, tier)`** ‚Äî tier-scoped UPDATEs (players currently rostered in the tier), so six sims flushing the same day each rewrite only their own league. Tier-scoped league-totals queries added for the harness/future standings UI.
- **New-game careers start in HS**: `NewGameScreen` populates from `LoadTeamsByTier(HS)` only. The existing live-save avatar stays MLB (its team's backfilled tier).

**Known artifacts / disclosed simplifications:** uniform 9+5+3 rosters HS‚ÜíMLB (interleave-plan disclosure); **`LoadFreeAgents` deliberately NOT tier-scoped** ‚Äî free agents are tierless entities (team_id NULL has no Team_Tiers row to filter on), so succession backfill draws from the global pool; in practice the pool is avatar-tier alumni, and formalizing player‚Üîtier movement is exactly 9c's promotion model. NPCs never promote or age out of a tier (a 15-year-old HS NPC ages upward in place across seasons ‚Äî 9c's concern); HS avatar starts at `StartingAge` 19 while generated HS teammates are 15‚Äì18 (revisit with 9b/9c age handling); life-sim NPC count grew 137‚Üí817 (all tiers seed the needs engine; the day-tick flush now writes ~817 Life_Needs rows ‚Äî well inside the benchmarked batch budget); K%/BB%/HR separate tiers only gently by design (doc ¬ß1 discloses ‚Äî AVG/R/G carry tier identity).

## 9b ‚Äî Bare Daily-Clock Skeleton: SHIPPED (2026-07-04, Fable 5 engine + Sonnet 5 UI, NOT YET COMMITTED)

**Both 9b engine guarantees harness-proven.** NeedsDecayHarness 49‚Üí**61/61** (new 9b daily-clock section); MonteCarloHarness **153/153** re-run per the standing rule (CareerManager touched ‚Äî no band moved, MLB bit-identity guard still exact); CoreLoop 22/22 (Life‚ÜîBaseball boundary scan clean); GrittyEvents 53/53 (wildcard-compiles the Life folder); `dotnet build` 0/0 all 6 projects; live headless `--quit` boot clean (v7, day 43, avatar + 817 NPCs, no errors). No schema change ‚Äî a day plan is intent, not sim state; it deliberately does not persist (same precedent as pending choices/cooldowns).

**What shipped:**

- **`DaySchedule` (new, `Assets/Simulation/Life/DaySchedule.cs`):** readonly struct, five hour blocks (Sleep/School/Practice/Game/Work), ctor-validated ‚â•0 and ‚â§24; unallocated hours are "free". Life-folder-local and Data/Baseball-free, so `NeedsDecayHarness`'s wildcard compile stays untouched.
- **`LifeSimManager` avatar split:** `SetAvatar` / `SetTodaySchedule` / `TryGetTodaySchedule` / `ClearTodaySchedule` / `AvatarSchoolAvailable`. With no plan set, the avatar days through the **exact pre-9b `TickHour` loop** ‚Äî marking an avatar alone changes nothing (the `AutopilotAttendedGames` mirror; headless callers unmodified). A set plan is **one-shot**: consumed by the day it runs, an unplanned tomorrow autopilots (the pending-game-forfeit mirror). `SetAvatar` drops any pending plan (an heir never inherits the retiree's day).
- **Canonical day order ‚Äî Sleep runs LAST (found the hard way):** first draft ran Sleep first and the harness caught it ‚Äî sleeping from a full meter burns the whole restore against the 100-clamp, an 8h-sleep day ended at Sleep 33.5. Order is now School ‚Üí Practice ‚Üí Game ‚Üí Work ‚Üí free hours (standard autopilot, crisis override intact) ‚Üí Sleep as the night cap (worst end-of-day Sleep 69+ over the scripted week). Sleep restores per-hour at `ActionCatalog.Sleep`'s own rate/environment (one tuning source for both paths); School/Practice/Game/Work ride `ActionCatalog.Idle`'s neutral definition ‚Äî each future upgrade (9d development, 8a Work payout) is a one-line definition swap. Manual blocks are uninterruptible (player intent outranks the crisis override in the skeleton ‚Äî disclosed; the override still governs free hours).
- **School gate:** `SetTodaySchedule` rejects School hours unless `AvatarSchoolAvailable` ‚Äî a plain bool because the Life assembly must never see `LeagueTier`; the bridge projects `tier is HS or College` into it.
- **`AvatarChangedEvent` (new, CoreEvents.cs):** published by `CareerManager.ActivateAvatar` when a bus is attached (creation + succession); GameManager subscribes and `SyncLifeSimAvatar` re-points the Life sim + school gate. Boot-time load activates before the career attaches, so `_Ready` syncs that case directly. **Side-effect fix of a pre-existing gap:** a mid-session avatar (fresh creation, or an heir born this session) was never seeded into the life sim until next boot ‚Äî the sync handler now projects its Players row in first (`Seed` is idempotent).
- **Harness additions (the plan's two validation demands):** (1) a never-planned avatar reproduces the pre-9b autopilot trace **bit-for-bit over 30 days** (needs+stress+funds, avatar and bystander, stress-seeded worlds); (2) a fully-allocated 24h day matches a closed-form recomputation of the block math **bit-exactly**; plus a scripted week of manual plans (one-shot consumption daily, bystander NPC bit-identical to a no-avatar control world, night cap keeps Sleep restored, Hygiene off-critical via evening Showers, funds strictly falling proves the free-hour autopilot really acts ‚Äî blocks never spend).

**Disclosed findings / known artifacts:** a 19h-committed plan **genuinely starves Hunger** (one evening Eat +45 can't outrun ~100/day decay; end-of-day Hunger 0.0 all week) ‚Äî real tuning reality, deliberately unasserted; 8a/9d should consider meal access on Work/School blocks. Blocks charge no `FinancialCost` and grant no restore except Sleep. The plan is in-memory only (lost on quit ‚Äî pacing/intent, not sim state). Game hours are life-side inert; coordinating "Game block ‚áí play the pending attended game" is the ScheduleScreen's job against `CareerManager.TryGetPendingGame`.

**UI half (Sonnet 5):** `Assets/UI/ScheduleScreen.tscn`+`.cs`, wired into `Main.tscn` as a sixth always-present overlay (declared last). Deliberately **not modal** like EventChoiceScreen/SuccessionScreen ‚Äî a plan is optional, so it never joins `AttendedGameScreen`'s day-advance gate ‚Äî instead it follows `BirthNotificationScreen`'s corner-anchored, non-blocking idiom (bottom-right here, to stay clear of the top bar and the top-right birth banner). Five `HSlider`s (0‚Äì24, matching NewGameScreen's slider+value-label convention rather than SpinBox) for Sleep/School/Practice/Game/Work; Confirm disables itself once the running total exceeds 24h (`OverAllocatedFormat`) instead of letting `DaySchedule`'s ctor throw. Polls `LifeSim.AvatarSchoolAvailable` and `Career.TryGetPendingGame` every frame to show/hide the School and Game rows and zero their sliders the instant either goes unavailable (tier change, offseason day) ‚Äî a stale hour never rides along silently. The plan-status label is dirty-flag gated on the polled `DaySchedule` fields per ui_conventions (no per-frame string formatting); row `Visible` assignments are unconditional every frame, matching SuccessionScreen's precedent. `dotnet build` 0/0; booted the live save headless via the Godot MCP (schema v7, day 43, avatar + 817 NPCs) with the new overlay in the tree for multiple frames ‚Äî zero debug-output errors, confirming every `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` path resolves.

## 8a ‚Äî Survival Economy + Legal Work: SHIPPED (2026-07-04, Sonnet 5, NOT YET COMMITTED)

**Closes the interleave plan's 8a item end to end.** Planned via full plan-mode first ‚Äî a Plan-agent pressure test against the live code caught two real bugs before any code was written: (1) a divide-by-zero-shaped NaN hazard if the new per-hour funds math had guarded on `FinancialCost == 0` instead of mirroring the existing `restorePerHour` guard's denominator (`TemporalCostHours > 0`); (2) a genuine same-pump race where a blind daily overwrite of `Players.funds` could silently clobber a gritty event's `AdjustFunds` payout, since `GrittyEventFiredEvent` fires off the dispatcher's own background thread and its `FundsImpulseEvent` follow-up is bus-deferred ‚Äî it can still be queued (mirror not yet updated) when that day's `PersistLifeSimState` flush runs in the same `DispatchPending()` pump. Both designed out (below) rather than patched after the fact.

**What shipped:**

- **`ActionCatalog.cs`:** two new schedule-block-only `NpcActionId`s (`School`, `LegalWork`) ‚Äî deliberately excluded from `ActionCatalog.All`/`UtilityCalculator.SelectAction`'s scan, so they can never be spontaneously autopilot-picked. `School` (+3 Hunger/hr over 6h, neutral environment) closes part of 9b's disclosed meal-access gap. `LegalWork` (gritty_events.md's "time-skip abstraction... heavily drains Energy and Fitness for minimal payout" ‚Äî Sleep is this codebase's only Energy analog): +2 Hunger/hr over 8h, $25/hr income (`FinancialCost` negative = income ‚Äî documented sign convention, first action to use it), zero risk, heavy Sleep√ó2/Fitness√ó1.8 environment drain. $25/hr is a tuned constant, not a design-doc anchor ‚Äî a broke NPC's own funds-blind free-hour autopilot spend (`SelectAction` only discourages a cost via `FinancialCostScore`, never refuses it) already runs well past the $70/week cost-of-living drain on its own, so Legal Work has to outpace both to make working actually pay off.
- **`LifeSimManager.cs` ‚Äî the core mechanism:** `NpcRuntime` gained `UnflushedFundsDelta`, touched only by a new `ApplyFundsDelta(npc, delta)` helper (diffs the *clamped* value, not the nominal delta, into the accumulator ‚Äî a debit that bottoms out at the zero floor must not queue more "debt" than the mirror actually gave up). `ApplyAction`'s autopilot debit and the new `TickBlockHours` funds proration both route through it; `OnFundsImpulse` (gritty events) deliberately does **not** ‚Äî that portion is already committed to the DB by whoever published the impulse. `TickScheduledDay` swaps School/Work from `ActionCatalog.Idle` to the new real definitions (Practice/Game stay Idle ‚Äî 9d/CareerManager territory respectively). New recurring cost-of-living drain (`CostOfLivingCadenceDays=7`, `WeeklyCostOfLiving=$70`, one bundled rent+food+gear line item, disclosed simplification) fires **avatar-only** ‚Äî the pressure test's call: NPCs have no schedule and can never reach `School`/`LegalWork` via autopilot, so a uniform drain would just monotonically zero out all ~817 background NPCs with no validated purpose. New `PeekFundsDelta`/`ClearFundsDelta` accessors (deliberately two separate calls, not one get-and-clear) let `GameManager` defer clearing until after a DB commit succeeds.
- **`GameManager.cs`:** `PersistLifeSimNeeds` renamed `PersistLifeSimState` (now covers Needs+Stress+Funds). Funds route through `Players.AdjustFunds` (atomic delta) ‚Äî **never** `UpdateFunds` (a blind overwrite) ‚Äî keeping `AdjustFunds` the sole writer of `Players.funds` end to end, so it can never race a same-pump gritty-event payout (deltas commute; overwrites don't). Accumulators are cleared only **after** `CommitBatch()` succeeds; a rollback leaves them intact so nothing is silently lost to the next attempt.
- **`NeedsDecayHarness` (Data-free ‚Äî proves the Life-folder mechanism, not the GameManager/DB wiring):** grew 69‚Üí**69/69** (net: several new checks, one old assertion replaced). New: a School/LegalWork Environment-range check (they're excluded from the existing `ActionCatalog.All` sweep); the fully-allocated-day closed-form fixture rewritten to derive School's/Work's real restore+environment for their hours instead of assuming all-Idle, plus an exact Funds assertion (3h √ó $25/hr, zero free-hour noise); the Guarantee-1 "never-planned avatar ‚â° plain NPC" 30-day check split into Needs/Stress (still bit-identical) vs. Funds (now diverges from a plain NPC by **exactly** the accumulated cost-of-living total ‚Äî `4 cadence days √ó $70 = $280`, proven arithmetically, not just asserted); a new 30-day funds-solvency pair (the plan's explicit ask) ‚Äî a working avatar (`8 Sleep/8 Work/8 free`) ends **above** its $500 seed ($500‚Üí$2,989), a non-working avatar (`8 Sleep/16 free`) ends **below** it ($500‚Üí$0).
- **Scripted-week Hunger finding ‚Äî re-tested, not silently declared fixed:** the harness's own decay table shows Hunger floors within 24h under *pure passive neglect* (no actions at all), so no "modest" lunch was ever going to fully prevent flooring under a comparably packed 19h-committed week ‚Äî tried anyway, confirmed empirically (still floors), and replaced the originally-planned hard "stays off-critical" assertion with an honest **A/B control** instead: an identical 19-committed/5-free schedule with School's 6h reassigned to inert Practice (same autopilot noise, same everything else) ‚Äî the meal-access world's summed end-of-week Hunger is measurably higher (175.2 vs 149.9). Proves the fix helps without overclaiming it solves starvation; the underlying reality is unchanged from 9b's original finding, now re-confirmed rather than assumed.

**Verification:** `dotnet build` 0/0 all 6 projects. `NeedsDecayHarness` 69/69. `GrittyEventsHarness` 53/53, `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `SchemaValidator` 64/64 (sanity re-run ‚Äî no schema/Narrative-surface touched). `MonteCarloHarness` 153/153 on a clean re-run (an unrelated, previously-documented flake ‚Äî suite 7's timing-sensitive scripted-UI bridge handshake ‚Äî showed once, 152/153, then passed clean on retry; not caused by this session's changes, which never touch the Baseball assembly). Live save booted headless (`--headless --quit`, schema v7, day 43, avatar + 817 NPCs) clean with zero errors, confirming the `PersistLifeSimState` rename and its new `AdjustFunds` loop over ~817 ids execute without exception against the real DB; avatar funds ($500) and DB integrity confirmed unchanged before/after (no day advanced during the boot, so every delta was legitimately zero). **Disclosed gap:** `TimeManager.AdvanceDay()` is only ever called from `AttendedGameScreen`'s Play/Skip buttons ‚Äî this MCP setup has no input-injection path to drive a *real* day-advance headlessly, so the actual "Work block income/cost-of-living drain reaching `Players.funds` in a live running game" round-trip is unverified beyond the Data-free harness's exact arithmetic proof + this boot's crash-safety check. A manual playtest (submit a Work day in ScheduleScreen, click Play/Skip) is the way to observe it live; a future dedicated integration harness could automate it.

## 8b ‚Äî Narcotics + Fencing: DESIGN DOC done (2026-07-04, Opus 4.8, design only ‚Äî NO code)

**`docs/design/hustles_narcotics_fencing.md`.** Turns `.claude/rules/gritty_events.md`'s one-line "Narcotics: 3-tier system (Inventory Drop ‚Üí Profit/Toxicity Cut ‚Üí Territory Control vs Factions)" into a full deterministic risk/reward model, and designs the Fencing negotiation the interleave plan left "TBD by Opus's design". Load-bearing decisions:

- **No schema change.** Every value read/written already exists ‚Äî `Players.{funds, detection_risk, health_ceiling, recklessness}`, `Entity_Flags`, `Relationships` (via `RelationshipGraph`), additive `Game_State` keys for territory. Holds the standing "no migration a mechanic doesn't need" discipline.
- **Three layers, wall-clean** (the sim-engine precedent): Layer 1 = pure `Assets/Simulation/Hustles/` resolvers (`NarcoticsHustle`/`FencingNegotiation`), `(HustleContext, decision, ref RngState) ‚Üí HustleResolution`, Data-free/Baseball-free, references only `RngState` (the established Narrative-uses-RngState exception) ‚Äî harness-drivable with hand-built fixtures like `AtBatResolver`/`HeirGenetics`. Faction standing enters as plain `int`s and leaves as plain deltas so the resolver never touches the graph. Layer 2 = `HustleService` orchestration (Data + bus + graph). Layer 3 = isolated UI scenes.
- **Daily-clock seam = the attended-Game precedent.** Interactive hustles can't resolve synchronously inside `OnDayAdvanced`, so the Work block reserves the hours + applies a shared `ActionCatalog.HustleWork` needs-drain (Legal Work's drain, `FinancialCost = 0`), and arms a **pending hustle session** (Game-block mirror) the UI resolves; unplayed = **forfeit to the no-deal default** (no buy-in, no sale, zero added risk). Legal Work stays the passive in-tick payout. Rejected the decoupled ad-hoc-launch alternative (desyncs from the clock, duplicates needs accounting).
- **The risk/reward math** (¬ß3‚Äì¬ß4, all constants first-pass/`HustleHarness`-tunable): Narcotics is a 3-stage state machine with buy-in seizure risk, a **concave** cut curve (volume√óprice trade ‚Äî a real optimum, not "max everything"), and **demand saturation** bounding upside so over-investment fire-sales. EV rises with aggression but the aggressive tail converts money risk into **career** risk (health‚Üí8c injury, detection‚Üí8c suspension/arrest, a turf-war-loss Rival edge ‚Üí on-field rivalry via the untouched Phase-6 transport). Fencing is an alternating-offer negotiation over a hidden reservation price with a sting (informant) roll ‚Äî an information/nerve game, no twitch skill; a neutral autopilot policy is the headless harness stand-in (`InteractiveBatterPolicy` precedent).
- **Consequence reuse (¬ß5):** a `HustleResolution` is the same primitives gritty events apply plus two new ones (`detection_risk`/`health_ceiling` atomic clamped writers generalizing `ApplyPedGameCosts`) ‚Äî recommends factoring a shared `ConsequenceApplier` out of `EventConsequenceApplier` + extending the closed enum, the extension 8c needs anyway.
- **¬ß8 is the explicit accumulated-risk-state contract for 8c** (which stats/flags 8b writes vs. which 8c reads).

## 8b ‚Äî Narcotics + Fencing: IMPLEMENTED (2026-07-05, Sonnet 5, NOT YET COMMITTED)

**All three layers shipped against `hustles_narcotics_fencing.md`; 90 new/changed checks, all green; no schema touch.**

- **Layer 1 (`Assets/Simulation/Hustles/`):** `HustleResolution.cs` (shared bundle both hustles project into), `NarcoticsHustle.cs` (`HustleContext`, `HustleStage`, `PushLevel`, `HustleState` as a `readonly record struct` so each stage transition is a non-destructive `state with { ... }` ‚Äî the `RelationshipSeed` precedent ‚Äî plus `DropInventory`/`CutProduct`/`PushTerritory`/`BankExit`), `FencingNegotiation.cs` (`FencingContext`, `FencingState`, `StartLot`/`Accept`/`Counter`/`NeutralAcceptDecision`). Both Data-free/Baseball-free, referencing only `RngState`. New `Tools/HustleHarness` (mirrors the other harnesses' "compile the exact shipped sources headless" trick) proves design doc ¬ß9 checks 1‚Äì8: state-machine legality + bank-exit profit projection, stage-1 BuyInMax scaling + forced-seizure deltas, stage-2 concavity + bad-batch haircut, stage-3 demand saturation + forced-retaliation bundle, EV/tail-risk bands over 20k seeded runs per policy, Fencing's standing-respects-R + neutral/aggressive policy bands + forced-sting halving, cross-hustle determinism, and zero-alloc warm runs. **31/31.**
- **Two real design-math inconsistencies found via harness-proving, worked around and disclosed rather than silently "fixed" (not mine to retune) ‚Äî flagged for Fable/Opus:**
  1. ¬ß9 check 3 asks for "a mid `c` beats both `1.0` and `CutMax`" (a literal interior optimum). With `CutMax=2.5` and the 0.25 toxicity-discount coefficient, the revenue formula's true vertex is at `c=3.5` ‚Äî outside the `[1, 2.5]` domain ‚Äî so raw revenue is monotonically increasing over the whole playable range, not cresting mid-domain. The function IS still genuinely concave (strictly diminishing marginal returns to cutting further); `HustleHarness` asserts that property instead of the domain-inconsistent literal reading. Retuning `CutMax` down (or the 0.25 coefficient up) would pull the vertex inside the domain and make the literal check true too.
  2. ¬ß3.4's own worked table names `B=1000` for the "Aggressive" policy at `heat=0.20, supplierTrust=20` ‚Äî but `BuyInMax` at that exact point is `736` (¬ß3.1's own formula), so the table's B exceeds its own document's cap. `HustleHarness` uses the actual feasible ceiling (`min(1000, funds, BuyInMax)`); measured Aggressive EV (mean ‚âà $1444 over 20k runs at the feasible B) is well above Opus's rough $500 estimate as a result ‚Äî the *shape* (EV rises with aggression, tail converts to career risk) still holds, just not the point figures.
- **Layer 2:** three new atomic writers on `PlayerQueries` (`AdjustDetectionRisk`/`AdjustHealthCeiling`/`AdjustRecklessness`, all clamped `[0,100]` in SQL, generalizing `ApplyPedGameCosts`' one-directional halves to accept either sign). **Chose the disclosed fallback over the full shared-`ConsequenceApplier` refactor** (design doc ¬ß5's own sanctioned alternative, "Fable's review call"): `HustleService` (`Assets/Economy/Hustles/`) runs its own apply-loop over the same writers rather than routing through `EventConsequenceApplier`'s private `ApplyChoice` ‚Äî hustle resolutions aren't authored JSON content, so merging the two felt like reaching for a bigger refactor than one session should absorb. **Did still extend `ConsequenceKind`** with `DetectionRisk`/`HealthCeiling` (+ `EventConsequenceApplier`'s switch + `GrittyEventJson`'s `"detection_risk"`/`"health_ceiling"` string mappings) so 8c inherits a tested vocabulary regardless of which path its content ends up using. Faction reps (¬ß6: supplier, one local crew, plus a **"fence" rep** ‚Äî filling a gap the design doc's own ¬ß6 list left implicit for `fenceStanding`, ¬ß4.1) resolve once and cache as new `Game_State` pointer keys (`hustle_supplier_player_id` etc.) rather than a reverse `Entity_Flags` scan query ‚Äî cheaper, and the flags still get written for narrative legibility per the design doc's wording. Check 9 (Layer-2/DB integration) landed in `GrittyEventsHarness` (extended its `.csproj` to also compile `Simulation/Hustles` + `Economy/Hustles`) instead of a redundant third Data-compiling harness ‚Äî "whichever harness compiles Data," literally. **+6 checks, GrittyEventsHarness 53‚Üí59/59.**
- **The daily-clock seam:** `ActionCatalog.HustleWork` (LegalWork's exact needs-drain, `FinancialCost=0`) + `NpcActionId.HustleWork`, excluded from `All`/autopilot same as School/LegalWork. `LifeSimManager.AvatarWorkIsHustle` (bool only ‚Äî the Life assembly never learns *which* hustle, just which Work-block definition to tick, via a `ref (cond ? ref A : ref B)` swap in `TickScheduledDay`, keeping the wall intact). `GameManager` owns the actual selection: new `WorkActivity` enum + `PendingHustleSession` struct (`Economy.Hustles`), `SubmitDaySchedule`/`ClearDaySchedule` (the ScheduleScreen's one call site for both the plan AND the activity, so they can never desync), and `OnHustleDayAdvanced` ‚Äî subscribed *after* `LifeSim.AttachTo` so it always sees that day's Work block having already ticked. **Forfeiting a hustle needs no resolution applied at all** (unlike `CareerManager`'s autopilot-played game forfeit) ‚Äî "no buy-in, no sale, zero risk" is a plain flag-drop, and since nothing reaches the DB until the UI's Done button commits it, an abandoned mid-session run (day advances before Done) just evaporates for free, no special-casing.
- **Layer 3 UI:** `ScheduleScreen` gained a `WorkActivityOption` (`OptionButton`, index = `WorkActivity` byte value) row, Confirm now calls `GameManager.SubmitDaySchedule(schedule, activity)` instead of touching `LifeSim` directly. New `NarcoticsHustleScreen.tscn`/`.cs` (Start ‚Üí PostDrop ‚Üí PostCut ‚Üí Result panels, each `Visible`-toggled, mirroring `SuccessionScreen`'s unconditional-every-frame convention) and `FencingScreen.tscn`/`.cs` (offer/patience labels + Counter/Accept, never reads `FencingState.HiddenValue`/`HiddenReservation` ‚Äî only the live offer ever reaches a label, per ¬ß4's "no twitch skill" rule) ‚Äî both always-present overlays wired into `Main.tscn` (declared last, after `ScheduleScreen`). Both screens run the whole interactive session **in memory only**, committing through `HustleService` on Done.
- **Disclosed simplification:** `AttendedGameScreen`'s Play/Skip buttons are *not* blocked while a hustle session is mid-flight ‚Äî a day-advance mid-session just abandons that session's progress (safe, per the evaporates-for-free forfeit above), so this was left alone to keep the pass contained.

**Verification:** `dotnet build` 0/0 across all 7 projects (main + 6 Tools). `Tools/HustleHarness` (new) 31/31. `GrittyEventsHarness` 53‚Üí**59/59** (+6 Hustles Layer-2 integration checks: faction-rep resolution + Entity_Flags tagging, clamped multi-writer application, flag `set_on_day`, deep-Rival crew edge publishing `RivalryChangedEvent`, Friend supplier edge). `NeedsDecayHarness` **69/69** unchanged (`AvatarWorkIsHustle` defaults false ‚Äî bit-identical to pre-8b when unset). `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `SchemaValidator` 64/64 (sanity re-run ‚Äî no schema touched). `MonteCarloHarness` **153/153**, no band moved (sanity re-run by Sonnet ahead of the standing review ‚Äî the sim assembly itself was never touched this pass; Fable's own re-run is still the authoritative sign-off per the design doc's review assignment). Live save booted headless via the Godot MCP (schema v7, day 43, avatar + 817 NPCs, 39 relationships, 14 gritty events) with `ScheduleScreen`'s new selector, `NarcoticsHustleScreen`, and `FencingScreen` all in the tree across multiple frames ‚Äî zero debug-output errors, confirming every new `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` path resolves.

## 8b ‚Äî Fable 5 review pass: SIGNED OFF (2026-07-05)

**All three review deliverables closed. Note on repo state: everything the entries above marked "NOT YET COMMITTED" has since landed ‚Äî HEAD `de5882f` contains 8b Layer 3; `2e890f8` Layers 1‚Äì2; working tree clean.**

- **Authoritative `run_monte_carlo_batch` re-run: 153/153, exit 0.** No band moved ‚Äî full tier ladder inside every ¬ß4 band (HS .308/.390/.509 @ 6.97 R/G ‚Üí MLB .249/.318/.417 @ 4.28, strictly monotone), MLB bit-identity regression guard still exact (PA 48384/48384, H 10969/10969, ER 5237/5237), generation-3 succession season inside the ¬ß8 AVG/OBP bands. Confirmed via `git show --stat` that neither 8b commit touches `Assets/Simulation/Baseball/` ‚Äî the rivalry-layer exposure is runtime-only (new Rival edges over the untouched Phase-6 transport), exactly what the empty-vs-heated guard covers. Also re-ran firsthand: `HustleHarness` 31/31, `GrittyEventsHarness` 59/59 (the +6 Layer-2 checks exercise both clamp bounds ‚Äî detect pinned at 100, health at 0).
- **Writers sign-off: APPROVED.** All three new writers (`AdjustDetectionRisk`/`AdjustHealthCeiling`/`AdjustRecklessness`) clamp both directions in SQL (`MAX(0, MIN(100, col + @delta))`), atomic read-modify-write ‚Äî no stale C#-side read possible. Full writer census over `UPDATE Players`: the risk triple is written *only* by these three plus `ApplyPedGameCosts` (also an atomic in-SQL delta ‚Äî deltas commute, so the PED post-game path and a hustle resolution can never race); no full-row Players UPDATE exists anywhere to blind-overwrite them. Funds discipline holds end to end: `UpdateFunds`'s sole remaining caller is SchemaValidator's round-trip check; all game paths (day flush, gritty events, hustles) route through `AdjustFunds`. `HustleService.ApplyCore` keeps `EventConsequenceApplier`'s ordering exactly (own batch ‚Üí commit ‚Üí only then bus impulses + graph writes; rollback rethrows without publishing). Verified the nominal-vs-clamped bus-impulse edge is unreachable: worst-case Narcotics net is `‚àíB + (holdRevenue ‚àí 0.5B)` with holdRevenue ‚â• ~0.56¬∑B even for a minimal-cut bad batch, so a resolution can never nominally overdraw the wallet ‚Äî and the Life mirror floors at 0 identically anyway. One deviation noted and approved as an improvement: ¬ß5 specified `AdjustHealthCeiling` as `MAX(0, ‚Ä¶)` only; the shipped writer adds the `MIN(100)` cap, correct per the schema's 0‚Äì100 CHECK. `FencingScreen` confirmed to never read `HiddenValue`/`HiddenReservation` (its `AskCeiling` is a fixed constant, documented as deliberately not derived from them).
- **Ruling, finding 1 (CutMax vertex): no retune ‚Äî the harness's diminishing-returns assertion is the permanent check.** Independently verified: raw fixed-demand revenue is `‚àù c¬∑(7‚àíc)/6`, vertex exactly `c=3.5`; an interior vertex needs discount ‚â• 0.375 (or `CutMax < 1.5`) ‚Äî a drastic re-tune shifting every calibrated EV figure for zero gameplay gain, since the "real optimum, not max-everything" tension is already delivered by demand saturation + bad-batch expectation (vertex ‚âà2.64 with risk folded in) + toxicity-scaled costs. ¬ß9 check 3's wording was the error, not the model. Recorded as design-doc ¬ß11 addendum.
- **Ruling, finding 2 (Aggressive B=1000): doc-internal error ‚Äî the harness's feasible-ceiling policy (`min(1000, funds, BuyInMax)`, B=736 at ¬ß3.4's own parameters) is the faithful reading; the resolver's fail-loud throw is correct. No code change.** Measured EVs (93.9 / 225.5 / 1444.2) each verified against closed-form recomputation (‚âà93 / ‚âà225 / ‚âà1435) ‚Äî real model behavior, not sampling noise; the doc's "shape to preserve" contract holds everywhere (strict monotonicity, all-positive EV, seize ‚âà pSeize, tail monotone). **Balance watch-item handed to 8c, deliberately not retuned now:** Aggressive's ‚âà2√ó buy-in per session is priced against a tail whose career costs (arrest/suspension/injury) 8b writes but nothing yet reads ‚Äî tuning EV before 8c's consumers exist is tuning against half the cost function. Re-band ¬ß3.4 in the 8c pass.

## 8c ‚Äî Roster Availability engine surface (Arrest/Injury/Suspension triad): SHIPPED (2026-07-05, Fable 5, NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî Sonnet 5's event content half still open)

**The genuinely-new engine surface the interleave plan flagged: before this pass a rostered player was unconditionally in every game (fixed lineup/rotation/bullpen slots baked at `Initialize()`, no `IsAvailable` concept anywhere). Now shipped end to end at schema v8.** Contract doc for the content half: [design/roster_availability_triad.md](file:///c:/Users/DELL/dirt&diamonds/docs/design/roster_availability_triad.md).

**What shipped:**

- **Schema v8 = new `Player_Absences` table** (player_id PK ‚Üí Players CASCADE, reason 1=Injury/2=Suspension/3=Arrest CHECK, until_day, rating_penalty, penalty_until_day, STRICT) ‚Äî the additive Pitcher_Roles/Life_Stress/Team_Tiers pattern, no backfill (nothing produced absences before v8). DDL idempotence + the conditional keep-later upsert + query plans validated on a scratch db via sqlite3 BEFORE any C# (No Blind Queries). **One absence per player, longest-ends-wins wholesale** ‚Äî the SQL `ON CONFLICT ... DO UPDATE ... WHERE excluded.until_day >= until_day` and the ledger's in-memory merge apply the identical rule, so mirror and row can never disagree without a read-back.
- **Transport = the RivalryLedger pattern exactly:** `EventConsequenceApplier` writes the row in its own batch, then post-commit publishes a new primitives-only `PlayerAbsenceChangedEvent` (CoreEvents stays Data-free ‚Äî NeedsDecayHarness compiles it); the new **`AvailabilityLedger`** (`Assets/Simulation/Baseball/AvailabilityLedger.cs`) consumes it; `GameManager` hydrates the ledger from `LoadActiveAbsences(CurrentDay)` at boot. Sims rebuild flat per-slot caches gated on **Version AND day** (absences expire by the calendar moving, not by an event ‚Äî Version alone would strand an expiry).
- **`ConsequenceKind.Absence`** (`{"type":"absence","reason":"injury|suspension|arrest","days":N}`, days whole ‚â• 1, loud at load) ‚Äî the roster/availability mutation `gritty_event_framework.md` ¬ß4 explicitly deferred. **Day math: an event fires AFTER its day's games, so `until_day = fire_day + days + 1` ‚Äî the subject misses exactly N game days** (the naive `fire_day + days` silently costs N‚àí1; caught in design, pinned by harness). **Injury rust is engine-computed at apply time** from the subject's live health_ceiling ‚Äî `round(12¬∑(100‚àíhealth)/100)`, rust window as long as the absence, applied AFTER any same-choice HealthCeiling delta so "lose 20 health AND get hurt" prices off the damaged body; suspension/arrest carry no rust.
- **Replacement shadowing in both sims** (optional `Availability` field, null = bit-identical pre-8c path, the Rivalries precedent): an absent slot is shadowed by a nameless **replacement-level call-up** (all ratings 40, tier-shifted like a real player; fixed 60/25/15 arsenal in the micro pitch-chain) whose stats land on a **discard line** (accumulator arrays sized slots+1; the flush loops only the roster length ‚Äî nothing a call-up does ever reaches the DB or the absent player), no PED costs, no rivalries across a shadowed slot. A **rusty** player plays himself with every effective rating docked (PED/rivalry layer on top as usual). Absent starters/relievers still burn their rotation/bullpen turn.
- **`CareerManager`:** on an avatar-absent day the pending game still arms but resolves straight through the autopilot even in interactive mode ‚Äî the UI never sees a pending game the player isn't allowed to play (`AttendedGameScreen`'s existing "no game today" branch handles the day-advance unmodified). `PlayPendingGame` refreshes the micro-sim's availability for the pending game's own absolute day (one call site covers UI, autopilot and stale-forfeit paths). A shadowed human slot macro-resolves ‚Äî the policy handshake never engages for a benched avatar.
- **`GameManager`:** public `Absences` ledger (UI read surface), `AvatarScheduleLocked` (arrest-only ‚Äî jail locks `SubmitDaySchedule` outright; injury/suspension leave life scheduling alone), boot hydration + ledger handed to all six tier sims, the micro-sim and the career driver.

**Verification:** `dotnet build` 0/0 all 7 projects. **MonteCarloHarness 153‚Üí167/167** (+14, new "Phase 8c roster availability" suite): attached-empty-ledger season **BIT-IDENTICAL** to a no-ledger season; **MLB bit-identity regression guard still exact** (PA 48384/48384, H 10969/10969, ER 5237/5237) and the whole tier ladder inside its 9a bands; suspended batter PA and suspended starter G freeze for exactly the absent window (61‚Üí61 / 3‚Üí3) while teammates accrue (58‚Üí93), both resume after; keep-later + day-boundary + rust arithmetic pinned; SQL‚Üîledger round-trip; benched-avatar career flow (auto-resolve in interactive mode, PA frozen 21‚Üí21, pending game parks again the day the suspension ends). **GrittyEventsHarness 59‚Üí67/67** (+8): parse gates (3 reasons, unknown-reason/zero/fractional-days rejections), the +1 day math, rust priced off live health (40 ‚Üí penalty 7, window 13‚Üí23), post-commit `PlayerAbsenceChangedEvent` transport, absence composing with `detection_risk` cooling + flags in one choice. CoreLoop 22/22 (boundary scan clean), NeedsDecay 69/69 (Life untouched), HustleHarness 31/31, SchemaValidator 64‚Üí**66/66** scratch (Player_Absences in RequiredTables) + **49/49** live audit. All three hardcoded user_version checks bumped 7‚Üí8 (the known gotcha, on schedule). Live save migrated v7‚Üív8 through **two clean headless `--quit` boots** (second proves idempotence: 817 players/48 teams, integrity ok, avatar intact); repo-root validation db topped up to v8.

**Aggressive-EV re-band watch-item from the 8b review: CLOSED** ‚Äî `hustles_narcotics_fencing.md` **¬ß12 addendum**: ¬ß3.4's normative resolver-level bands are the measured +$93.9/+$225.5/+$1,444.2 (unchanged, harness-asserted); the tail's price is now a **content knob** (1 absent day = 1 in-season game; arrest also locks the schedule ‚âà $200/day of blocked Legal Work), with a concrete costing frame handed to Sonnet (suspension 5‚Äì15d @ detection ‚â•60/80/90, arrest 20‚Äì40d @ narc_watchlist, injury 7‚Äì21d @ health <50 ‚Äî realizes ‚âà$700‚Äì1,100 expected career cost per Aggressive session against the $1,444 nominal EV). No resolver constant touched; if playtest still shows Aggressive dominating, tune event weights/durations first.

**Disclosed simplifications** (full list in the design doc ¬ß4): longest-wins means concurrent shorter absences vanish; replacement call-ups don't move the baked team-defense byte; suspensions are day-denominated (offseason days burn without costing games); a plan submitted before an arrest lands still runs its jailed day; league W=L identity holds only in absence-free worlds (shadowed starters' decisions hit the discard line); no jail-specific needs model or "skip to release" UI yet.

## 8c ‚Äî Content half: SHIPPED (2026-07-05, Sonnet 5, NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî closes Phase 8c end to end)

**The triad content batch against `roster_availability_triad.md` ¬ß2, plus the two engine-doc gaps it exposed.** `Assets/Narrative/Events/Content/roster_availability_events.json` ‚Äî 5 events: `narcotics_arrest` (`narc_watchlist` active ‚â•5 days + `detection_risk‚â•80` ‚Üí 30-day arrest absence, detection_risk ‚àí50, clears `narc_watchlist`, plants forward-hook flag `record_arrest`); a 3-tier suspension ladder on `detection_risk` 90/80/60 (`suspended_lifetime_watch`/`suspended_repeat_violation`/`suspended_ped_test_flag` ‚Üí 14/10/6-day absences, detection_risk ‚àí50/‚àí40/‚àí30, all set `served_suspension`); `sidelined_by_injury` (`health_ceiling<50`, two choices trading a 21-day absence + health_ceiling+20 recovery against a 7-day absence with no recovery ‚Äî deliberately no rating-debuff consequence, since rust is already engine-computed at apply time off live health).

**Ordering is load-bearing:** the 5 events are authored highest-severity-first (arrest, suspension tier 3, tier 2, tier 1, injury) so the engine's "one fire per subject per day, first satisfied definition in file order wins" rule (confirmed by reading `Tools/GrittyEventsHarness/Program.cs`) escalates to the harshest tier a subject clears rather than the mildest.

- `GrittyEventsHarness`'s folder-merge count bump (the standing per-batch gotcha): 14‚Üí**19**, with `TryGetById` checks added for all 5 new ids.

**UI half ‚Äî reads `GameManager.Absences` + `AvatarScheduleLocked`, stays read-only per `ui_conventions.md`:**

- `ScheduleScreen.tscn`/`.cs`: new `LockLabel` node (under `Panel/Layout`, right below `PlanStatusLabel`), shown only while `AvatarScheduleLocked` (arrest only, per its own contract ‚Äî injury/suspension don't touch life scheduling). Dirty-flag gated on (locked, untilDay); folded into `ConfirmButton.Disabled` every frame via a new `_overAllocated` field (`RefreshHoursLabels` now sets it instead of touching `Disabled` directly, since the lock can flip with no slider touched ‚Äî it needed a check that runs every frame, not just on `ValueChanged`).
- `AttendedGameScreen.tscn`/`.cs`: new persistent `AvailabilityLabel` node (under `Screen`, below `TopBar`), read straight off `GameManager.Absences.TryGet` every frame, independent of the Play/Skip click flow. Chosen over only patching the existing one-shot `NoGameText` branch because that branch is fed by `_awaitingPendingGame`, which Skip Day never sets ‚Äî a player clicking Skip through an entire absence would otherwise get zero feedback. `TryGet` returns expired entries too, so visibility is gated on `entry.StateOn(today)` in code, never the bool alone.
- Both screens gained `using DirtAndDiamonds.Data;` for `AbsenceReason`. No engine/schema change; nothing escalated to Fable (no resolver-level knob touched).

## 8d ‚Äî Texas Hold'em: DESIGN DOC done (2026-07-05, Opus 4.8, design only ‚Äî NO code; sim/math core only, `.tscn`/UI deferred to a follow-on slice)

**`docs/design/hustles_texas_holdem.md`.** Turns `.claude/rules/gritty_events.md`'s one-line "Texas Hold'em: Direct mathematical card simulation evaluating pot odds" into the full pot-odds/bluffing math + hand evaluator + betting state machine, slotting into the exact three-layer seam `hustles_narcotics_fencing.md` already cut. Confirmed scope this pass: **sim/math core only, UI deferred** (a follow-on slice). Load-bearing decisions:

- **Thesis ‚Äî Hold'em is the *skill* hustle.** Deliberately unlike Narcotics/Fencing (RNG-dominated, tuned to a fixed positive-but-lumpy EV): poker's EV is *player-determined*, so the calibration target is **skill monotonicity** (a tight-aggressive policy must beat a station/maniac at the same table) + **rake binding** (a coin-flip-quality player is net negative), not a fixed positive number. The house edge is the **rake** (5%, cap 3¬∑BB, no-flop-no-drop), not an RNG wall.
- **Reuses everything, adds almost nothing.** Same three layers, same `HustleContext`‚Üí`HustleResolution` seam, same consequence writers, same daily-clock arming/forfeit. `WorkActivity` gains a `Poker` member; `HustleService` gains `BuildHoldemContext` (simpler than Narcotics ‚Äî funds/heat/reck, **no faction reps**, no graph touch) + `ApplyHoldemResolution`. **One additive struct field** ‚Äî `HustleResolution.SetGamblingBustFlag` (‚Üí `"gambling_bust"`, the poker analogue of Fencing's sting flag). **No schema change** (funds/detection_risk/recklessness + Entity_Flags all exist).
- **The math (¬ß4‚Äì¬ß9, all constants first-pass/`HoldemHarness`-tunable):** a 7-card‚Üíbest-5 evaluator returning one comparable 24-bit `HandScore` (histogram impl + a 21-combo brute-force **oracle** for a differential test ‚Äî the "prove the fast path against a naive oracle" discipline); the mandated "direct card simulation" = **bounded Monte-Carlo runout equity** on `RngState` (postflop, K‚âà300) + a **baked 169-hand preflop table** (offline-generated, verified vs. AA‚âà0.85/AKs-vs-22‚âà0.50); the pot-odds / **MDF** (`1/(1+s)`) / **GTO bluff ratio** (`bluffs:value = s/(1+s) : 1`) framework driving both the opponent AI and the hero autopilot; 5 opponent archetypes (Nit/TAG/LAG/Station/Maniac) whose field-skew scales with stakes (soft at Low ‚Üí sharp at High = the risk/reward lever); a no-limit betting state machine with **side-pot-correct** all-in resolution + a chip-conservation invariant.
- **The interactive contract** mirrors Fencing/Narcotics: `StartHand`/`SubmitHeroAction(Fold|CheckOrCall|RaiseTo)` advance to the next hero decision point (opponents batched between, recorded in an action log the UI renders). A **session** = buy-in ‚Üí hands ‚Üí **StandUp** (bank-&-exit between hands, the Narcotics precedent); `FundsDelta = stackReturned ‚àí buyIn` as a single net delta (no mid-session DB writes; **no markers in v1** so max loss = buy-in).
- **The tail = raid (detection), not health.** Per-hand raid hazard `h` cumulates over a session (`1‚àí(1‚àíh)^n` ‚Äî longer grind, more heat, so banking early is measurably safer); a raid seizes the on-table stack + `detection +10` / `gambling_bust` / `stress +20`. `Low` stakes never raids (its whole risk is variance). **¬ß12 is the explicit 8c risk-state contract** (detection_risk + `gambling_bust` ‚Üí arrest/suspension; writes **no** `health_ceiling` ‚Äî the markers/`house_debt`/violent-collection health-tail cascade is explicitly deferred, the Narcotics-passive-turf-income precedent).
- **State-representation call made in the doc (¬ß10):** a 6-seat table state is too large for the readonly-record-struct-`with` pattern ‚Äî recommends a `ref`-mutated value struct with C# 12 `[InlineArray]` buffers, with a **pooled mutable class** as the sanctioned fallback (Fable's call, like 8b's shared-applier ruling); `HoldemResolution` stays a `readonly struct` either way.
- **¬ß14 acceptance surface** (new `Tools/HoldemHarness`, or extend `HustleHarness`): evaluator differential vs. oracle, equity convergence, MDF/bluff-ratio formulas, chip conservation + side pots, session/bank-exit, **skill monotonicity + rake-binds + field gradient** EV bands, raid tail, determinism, zero-alloc, Layer-2 integration.
- **¬ß15 suggested Sonnet sub-sequence** (Layer 1 is larger than one hustle ‚Äî split 8d-1/8d-2 if a session is tight): 8d-1 evaluator+equity+preflop-table+harness (self-contained core); 8d-2 betting+AI+session; then Layer 2; then the deferred Layer 3 `.tscn`. Fable review is a lighter "no band moved" than 8b (Hold'em touches **no** baseball/rivalry assembly) + the new writer/flag/chip-conservation/skill-band sign-off + the ¬ß10 struct-vs-class call.

## 8d-1 ‚Äî Texas Hold'em: self-contained core SHIPPED (2026-07-05, Sonnet 5, NOT YET COMMITTED)

**Closes ¬ß15's first sub-slice against `docs/design/hustles_texas_holdem.md`: the evaluator, the equity engine, the baked preflop table, and `Tools/HoldemHarness` (checks 1‚Äì2, plus a zero-alloc check pulled forward from ¬ß14.9 since it was free to prove now).** No schema/Data/Godot touch ‚Äî pure `Assets/Simulation/Hustles/*.cs` + `RngState.cs`, same wall as 8b/8c.

- **`HoldemCards.cs`:** `Card` (byte-packed `(Rank<<2)|Suit`, readonly struct) + `Deck` (`FillStandard`/`Shuffle`, Fisher‚ÄìYates over `RngState`).
- **`HoldemEvaluator.cs`:** the histogram production evaluator (`EvaluateBest7`, ¬ß4.2's 24-bit `HandScore`, wheel folded into the straight-check via a virtual ace-low bit rather than a separate branch) + `HoldemOracle` (an independently-written, sort-based 21-combo brute force ‚Äî deliberately not sharing code with the histogram path, so the differential test can't be fooled by a shared bug).
- **`HoldemEquity.cs`:** `Estimate` (¬ß5.1's bounded MC runout, one partial Fisher‚ÄìYates per sample drawing opponents' holes + the runout together, zero-alloc stackalloc scratch) + `StartingHandIndex` (the 169-hand canonical grid, diagonal=pairs/upper triangle=suited/lower=offsuit) + `LookupPreflopEquity`.
- **`HoldemPreflopTable.cs` (generated, checked in as data):** baked via a new `--gen-preflop` harness mode (169 hands √ó 5 opponent counts, 20,000 MC samples/point, ~220s one-time offline cost) ‚Äî verified against both design-doc references (AA vs 1 = 0.8564, target ‚âà0.851; AKs vs 22 = 0.5003 via a harness-only known-hand equity helper, target ‚âà0.50) and a high-K (80,000-sample) recompute of five representative hands, all within tolerance.
- **`HoldemProfile.cs`:** the shared-constants home 8d-2 will extend (rake/archetypes/session), populated for now with just `EquitySamplesDefault`.
- **`Tools/HoldemHarness`** (new, added to `DirtAndDiamonds.sln` ‚Äî and `HustleHarness` was added alongside it, closing a pre-existing gap where 8b's harness was never added to the solution despite progress.md's own "all N projects" build claims): 17/17 checks ‚Äî differential test (histogram ‚â° oracle over 5,000 random 7-card deals), category-ordering fixtures (all 9 categories + royal-vs-ordinary-SF), the wheel (both evaluators agree it plays 5-high), a split-pot tie fixture, the two published equity references, opponent-count monotonicity, a preflop-table fidelity check, and a zero-alloc check on both `EvaluateBest7` and `Estimate` (0.0 B/run measured).
- **One real bug caught by the differential test, not by inspection:** `CollectRanksWithCount`'s zero-padding loop reused the same `idx` it later returned, so it always reported the output buffer's *capacity* (3) instead of the actual match count ‚Äî every single-pair hand was silently misclassified as two pair (with a phantom "pair of rank 0"). The 5,000-deal differential test caught it immediately (3,022/5,000 mismatches on the first run); fixed by capturing the real count before the padding loop runs. This is exactly the class of bug ¬ß4.3's "prove the fast path against a naive oracle" discipline exists to catch ‚Äî worth noting for whoever reviews this, since it shipped in the first draft despite the code reading correctly on inspection.
- **Godot build sanity:** `dotnet build DirtAndDiamonds.sln` 0/0 across all 8 projects (main + 7 Tools) ‚Äî the new Hustles sources compile cleanly into the main game via its wildcard glob too, confirming no Data/Godot leak. `HustleHarness` re-run 31/31 (unaffected).

**Not yet run:** `run_monte_carlo_batch`/`NeedsDecayHarness` ‚Äî not needed per the standing rule, since nothing this pass touches `Assets/Simulation/Baseball` or `Assets/Simulation/Life`.

## 8d-2 ‚Äî Texas Hold'em: betting engine + session + Layer 2 SHIPPED (2026-07-05, Sonnet 5, NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî Layer 3 UI still deferred)

**Closes ¬ß15's second sub-slice against `docs/design/hustles_texas_holdem.md` (¬ß6‚Äì¬ß9) plus the full Layer 2 handoff ‚Äî `HoldemHarness` checks 3‚Äì10 all green, 63/63.** Three new files in `Assets/Simulation/Hustles/`: `HoldemAgent.cs` (¬ß6 pot-odds/MDF/bluff math + ¬ß7 archetype decision procedure + ¬ß7.3 hero autopilot), `HoldemHand.cs` (¬ß8 no-limit betting state machine ‚Äî streets, side pots, the `StartHand`/`SubmitHeroAction` interactive contract), `HoldemSession.cs` (¬ß9 buy-in/bank-exit/raid tail). `HoldemProfile.cs` extended with stakes tiers, rake, archetype tunables, field skew, raid-hazard constants. Layer 2: `WorkActivity` gained `Poker` (needed **zero** other `GameManager` changes ‚Äî every arming/forfeit call site already branches on "any non-LegalWork activity"), `HustleResolution` gained `SetGamblingBustFlag` (optional ctor param, default `false` ‚Äî Narcotics'/Fencing's existing positional-arg call sites compile unchanged), `HustleService` gained `BuildHoldemContext`/`ApplyHoldemResolution` + the `gambling_bust` flag branch in `ApplyCore`.

**State-representation call (¬ß10):** took the **pooled mutable class** fallback over the InlineArray-struct recommendation ‚Äî `HoldemHandState` is one instance reused for a whole session (Fable's-call-per-the-doc's-own-framing; flagged for review). `HoldemSessionState` similarly a class, since it must hold a live reference to that pooled table.

**Three real bugs found and fixed via the harness, not by inspection ‚Äî worth flagging for review, especially the second:**

1. **Chip-conservation leak in multi-way side pots.** `CompleteShowdown`'s rake deduction capped itself to the LOWEST (main) layer's own size, but `HandResult.Rake` still reported the full nominal rake regardless ‚Äî when the main layer was smaller than the nominal 5%-capped-at-3BB rake (a real, if uncommon, scenario with deep multi-way all-ins), the shortfall got silently paid out to players as if it were prize money.
