Caught by a differential-style sweep (3,000 random hands, varied seat counts 2‚Äì6, some forced to very short stacks to guarantee frequent all-ins/side pots) asserting `Œ£stacks_after + rake == Œ£stacks_before` exactly ‚Äî 40/3000 failures on the first run. Fixed by draining the nominal rake progressively across ascending layers (spilling into the next if the main layer alone can't cover it) and reporting the amount ACTUALLY deducted, not the nominal target.
2. **Preflop entry-equity gate compared against the wrong reference.** The ¬ß7.1 archetype table's "preflop entry equity" (Nit 0.62 ‚Ä¶ Maniac 0.40) was being checked against equity vs. the table's ACTUAL live-opponent count (5, at a full 6-max table) ‚Äî but even pocket Aces are only ‚âà49% against 5 random hands, so almost nothing could clear even Maniac's loosest 0.40 threshold. VPIP collapsed toward 0‚Äì2% for every archetype, and the EV-band ordering came out wildly non-monotone as a result. Real preflop hand-selection charts rank hands by intrinsic strength (effectively heads-up equity), independent of table size ‚Äî fixed by always looking the entry-gate equity up against 1 opponent (`HoldemAgent.PreflopEntryEquity`), while the rest of the decision procedure (pot-odds/value/bluff) still uses equity vs. the real live-opponent count.
3. **¬ß6.1's pot-odds formula didn't match what ¬ß6.3's bluff-ratio calibration assumes.** The design doc's ¬ß6.1 prose is internally inconsistent about what "P" means (once "including the bet," once "before the bet," in adjacent sentences) ‚Äî the standard textbook reading (`c/(pot+c)`, ‚âà33%/25% for pot/half-pot bets) was implemented first, since it's the common convention. This silently broke the whole aggression model: ¬ß6.3's bluff-ratio is calibrated so a caller defending at exactly `s/(1+s)` (¬ß6.1's OWN worked 50%/33% examples, and algebraically identical to ¬ß6.2's MDF) is indifferent between calling and folding against a mixed bluff/value range ‚Äî using the looser, more-callable textbook threshold instead made every archetype's bluffs get picked off more often than the ratio assumes, so ALL aggression became a structural leak and the least-bluffy archetypes (Nit, Station) won regardless of overall decision quality. Diagnosed via a new `--debug-archetypes` harness mode (isolates one archetype against a homogeneous field, with VPIP/showdown stats) after the EV bands came back with Station beating TAG by 100+ bb/100. Fixed by implementing ¬ß6.1 as literally `c/P` (P = the running pot, which already includes the bet being faced) ‚Äî algebraically exactly `s/(1+s)`, matching the doc's own examples and restoring the MDF/bluff-ratio equivalence it explicitly claims. After the fix: `TAG=214.60 > LAG=128.41 > Nit=75.61 ‚âà Station=70.39 ‚â´ Maniac=-500.94 ‚â´ Random=-1523.95` bb/100 (Low, 60k hands/policy, common random numbers) ‚Äî matches ¬ß13's target shape.

**Disclosed, not chased further:** the doc's literal skill-monotonicity claim assumes real poker's opponent-adaptive dynamics; this model's archetypes are static thresholds with zero opponent-specific exploitation. Against a *homogeneous all-TAG field* specifically (probed while debugging finding 3, via `--debug-archetypes`, at 2/3/6-max), Nit and Station consistently **outearn** TAG ‚Äî plausible given rake scales with pot size/frequency and nothing here punishes tightness the way an adaptive opponent would. The harness asserts the doc's shape against the tier's REAL field skew (where it holds cleanly, per the numbers above), not against a homogeneous field; flagged for Fable/Opus, same as 8b's disclosed EV-figure findings.

**Methodology note:** the EV-band harness checks measure bb/100 with a **fresh, independently-seeded hand per hand-index** (not one continuously-evolving session RNG) so that comparing two different subject policies at the same seed deals hand #i identical cards against identical opponent archetypes both times ‚Äî common random numbers, needed because naive independent-stream sampling was dominated by field-composition/card-luck noise at 30‚Äì60k hands (real poker's variance needs far more hands than that to converge on its own). This is a harness-only measurement convention; `HoldemSession` itself still uses one continuously-threaded `RngState` per real session, proven bit-identical under the same seed (check 8).

**Verification:** `dotnet build DirtAndDiamonds.sln` 0/0 across all 8 projects. `HoldemHarness` **63/63** (17 from 8d-1 + 46 new: pot-odds/MDF/bluff-ratio formulas + hero-autopilot interpolation, blinds/button/illegal-action fixtures, the chip-conservation sweep, session buy-in/bank-exit/bust/double-stand-up fixtures, the 6 skill-monotonicity/rake-binds/field-gradient EV-band checks, 6 raid-tail checks incl. a measured-rate-vs-formula check, determinism, 2 more zero-alloc checks for a warm hand and a warm session's per-hand play). `GrittyEventsHarness` **67/67** unchanged (compiles the new Hold'em resolvers + the `HustleService`/`HustleResolution` edits wholesale; no regression). `HustleHarness` **31/31** unchanged (the `SetGamblingBustFlag` optional param didn't disturb Narcotics'/Fencing's positional-arg `HustleResolution` construction). `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `SchemaValidator` 49/49 live audit (sanity ‚Äî no schema/DB code touched). `MonteCarloHarness`/`NeedsDecayHarness` not re-run per the standing rule (nothing this pass touches `Simulation/Baseball` or `Simulation/Life`).

**Still open:** Layer 3 (`Assets/UI/TexasHoldemTable.tscn`/`.cs`) remains the explicitly deferred follow-on slice ‚Äî `ScheduleScreen`'s Work-activity dropdown is deliberately left at its current 3 hardcoded items (LegalWork/Narcotics/Fencing) rather than exposing a selectable Poker option with no table screen behind it yet. Fable 5's review: the ¬ß10 struct-vs-pooled-class call, the writer/flag/chip-conservation/skill-band sign-off, and a lighter "no band moved" `run_monte_carlo_batch` pass (Hold'em touches no baseball/rivalry assembly, so this is a sanity re-run rather than a real risk).

**Repo-state note (2026-07-05, this session, start-of-session check):** `git log`/`git status` showed 8d-1 (`b2994bb`) and 8d-2 (`f40b09e`) already committed on `main` with a clean tree ‚Äî the two entries above are stale on "NOT YET COMMITTED"; this file wasn't updated to match at the time. Always re-check `git status`/`git log` before trusting this file's commit-status claims ‚Äî the repo is authoritative, not the log.

## 8d Layer 3 ‚Äî Texas Hold'em table UI SHIPPED (2026-07-05, Sonnet 5, NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî closes Phase 8d end to end pending Fable's 8d-2 review)

**Closes the explicitly-deferred Layer 3 slice against `docs/design/hustles_texas_holdem.md`'s own ¬ß15 handoff.** `Assets/UI/TexasHoldemTable.tscn`+`.cs`, wired as a seventh permanent `Main.tscn` overlay sibling (declared last, after `FencingScreen`, so it draws on top like the other hustle screens); `ScheduleScreen.tscn`'s `WorkActivityOption` grew a 4th item (`"Poker"`, id 3 ‚Äî matches `WorkActivity.Poker`'s enum value exactly, so `ScheduleScreen.cs`'s existing `(WorkActivity)_workActivityOption.Selected` cast needed no code change at all).

Follows the `NarcoticsHustleScreen`/`FencingScreen` always-present-overlay convention exactly: `_Process` polls `GameManager.TryGetPendingHustleSession(out session) && session.Activity == WorkActivity.Poker`; nothing reaches the database until `OnDonePressed` applies the session's one net `HustleResolution` ‚Äî same abandon-evaporates-cleanly forfeit discipline (a session left mid-hand when the day advances never touches real funds, per ¬ß9's "no mid-session DB writes").

**Flow, three panels:**

1. **Start panel** ‚Äî Stakes `OptionButton` (Low/Mid/High) + opponent-count `HSlider` (1‚Äì5) + buy-in `HSlider`, whose bounds are recomputed live off `HoldemProfile.GetTier` every time the stakes selection changes (mirrors `NarcoticsHustleScreen`'s buy-in-bounds-vs-affordability pattern).
2. **Table panel** ‚Äî board/hero cards rendered via `Card.ToString()` (`"Ah Kd"`-style, the same debug-readable format the resolver already ships), pot/current-bet, a full per-hand action log built from `HoldemHandState.ActionLog`, and either the hero action controls (Fold / Check-or-Call / Raise-to) or a between-hands sub-panel (Next Hand / Stand Up), toggled off `HoldemHandState.HandComplete`.
3. **Result panel** ‚Äî bust/raid/stood-up summary (net funds/detection/recklessness/stress deltas) once `HoldemSessionState.IsOver`.

**One sequencing decision not spelled out in the design doc:** `HoldemSession.CompleteHand` (the bust/raid roll + opponent rebuy + button rotation) is invoked automatically by the screen the instant `HoldemHandState.HandComplete` goes true ‚Äî before the player sees anything or presses a button. The doc's ¬ß8.2 interactive contract only covers the hand itself; treating "resolve the between-hands session bookkeeping immediately, non-optionally" as UI-owned sequencing (rather than a button press) was this session's call. Same reasoning extends to **Stand Up being offered only in the between-hands panel, never mid-hand** ‚Äî the resolver's own `StandUp` doesn't actually check `HandComplete` before running, so the screen itself is the enforcement point here, not the sim.

**Two smaller judgment calls:**

- The raise slider's bounds come directly from the resolver's own legality math (`minLegalTotal = min(CurrentBet + MinRaiseIncrement, available)`, `max = available`) ‚Äî when a full min-raise isn't affordable, `min` collapses to equal `max` (a single forced-all-in point) rather than needing a separate disabled state, since the resolver already treats `total == available` as always-legal regardless of the min-raise rule.
- Opponent archetypes (Nit/TAG/LAG/Station/Maniac) are never surfaced to the player ‚Äî seats render as `"Seat N"` only. The resolver tracks them internally for its own decision-making, but nothing in the design doc calls for exposing AI style, and doing so would hand the player a read the pot-odds/bluff-ratio game is supposed to be about inferring.

**One build error, one class of gotcha already on file:** bare `Environment.TickCount64` is ambiguous between `Godot.Environment`/`System.Environment` in any script with `using Godot;` ‚Äî fully qualified it, the same fix `NarcoticsHustleScreen` already carries.

**Verification:** `dotnet build DirtAndDiamonds.sln` 0/0 across all 8 projects. Booted the live save via the `godot` MCP with the new overlay instanced in `Main.tscn` ‚Äî two `get_debug_output` polls showed zero errors, confirming every `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` path in `_Ready()` resolves against the actual scene tree; `godot_scene_mapper` was run against the new `.tscn` before the `.cs` was written, per the mandatory `ui_conventions.md`/CLAUDE.md workflow. Harnesses not re-run ‚Äî pure UI, no compiled `Simulation/Baseball`/`Simulation/Hustles` surface touched (this session added zero lines to any resolver); `HoldemHarness` remains 63/63 from 8d-2.

**Known gap, same class as every prior UI-copy entry:** no input-injection path exists to drive a real Poker `WorkActivity` day-advance headlessly, so the actual hand-by-hand interactive flow (raise-slider legality at the table, action-log rendering across streets, the between-hands/session-end panels) is verified by code inspection + a clean boot only ‚Äî not by watching a real session play out. A manual playtest (submit a Poker work day in `ScheduleScreen`, click Play/Skip, sit down and play a few hands) is how to see it live.

## 8d-2 ‚Äî Fable 5 review pass: SIGNED OFF (2026-07-05)

**All four review deliverables closed (full verdict text in the design doc's new ¬ß16 addendum). Reviewed at HEAD `f40b09e` (8d-2 committed) with the uncommitted Layer 3 UI in the tree ‚Äî the UI adds no sim/math surface, so the review target is exactly the committed resolver code.**

- **¬ß10 state-representation call: pooled mutable class UPHELD.** Three reasons, the first decisive: (1) the ¬ß8.2 interactive contract has the UI *retain* `session.Table` across frames between hero decisions ‚Äî a by-value struct would either copy on every read or end up housed in a class anyway, so the InlineArray-struct recommendation dissolves at the seam the state actually crosses; (2) allocation is once per session (a dozen small arrays at `StartSession`), never per hand ‚Äî `ResetHand` reuses everything and the harness pins a warm hand and warm session-hand at ~0 B, which is the zero-GC mandate's actual substance (CLAUDE.md explicitly endorses pooling); (3) `[InlineArray]` would add ~6 buffer types and ref-plumbing for zero measurable gain on a turn-based path. `HustleResolution` remains a readonly struct as ¬ß10 requires.
- **Writers: APPROVED.** Hold'em introduces **no new SQL writer** ‚Äî `HoldemSessionState` accumulates plain deltas and `ApplyHoldemResolution` routes through the shared `ApplyCore`: `AdjustFunds` (floor-clamp never load-bearing ‚Äî buy-in ‚â§ funds validated at `StartSession`, max session loss = buy-in, no markers), 8b's atomic in-SQL clamps for detection/reck, `gambling_bust` via `SetFlag` with `set_on_day = day` (the 8c cascade clock), stress as a post-commit `StressImpulseEvent` ‚Äî commit-then-publish ordering intact. Census re-confirmed at review time: the risk-triple's writers are still exactly the three 8b writers + `ApplyPedGameCosts`; `UpdateFunds`'s only caller is still SchemaValidator. `ToResolution` hard-codes `healthCeilingDelta: 0` ‚Äî ¬ß11's deferred markers/health-tail correctly not smuggled in.
- **Chip conservation: APPROVED, verified analytically, not just empirically.** The ¬ß8.3 layered algorithm's level sum Œ£(L‚Çñ‚àíL‚Çñ‚Çã‚ÇÅ)¬∑|{i: committed·µ¢ ‚â• L‚Çñ}| = Œ£CommittedTotal = Pot exactly (folded seats' dead money included), so the progressive rake drain always collects exactly the nominal rake and Œ£net = ‚àírake. Also proven structurally: the feared empty-eligible-layer division-by-zero can't occur ‚Äî at showdown the max-committed seat is never folded (every fold happens against a strictly larger live street-commit; the all-folded case exits via `CompleteByFold`). The 8d-2 rake-overpayment fix (drain across ascending layers, report the actual deduction) is correct; harness sweeps 3,000 random hands with forced all-ins.
- **Skill bands + the `c/P` pot-odds call: APPROVED ‚Äî and the `c/P` form is confirmed as the *correct* resolution, not a workaround.** `c/P` (P = running pot, already including the bet faced) equals `s/(1+s)` algebraically ‚Äî the doc's own worked examples (pot-sized ‚áí 50%, half-pot ‚áí 33%) and ¬ß6.2's "MDF and pot odds are two views of the same line" both demand it; ¬ß6.1's `c/(P+c)` formula line is the internally-inconsistent artifact. The deeper reason it's right for THIS model: agent equity is estimated vs *random* holdings (range-blind, so overestimated vs a real betting range), and the tighter `s/(1+s)` threshold is what keeps callers honest enough that ¬ß6.3's bluff-ratio calibration holds ‚Äî self-consistency between the call threshold and the bluff mix is the load-bearing property. `BluffFraction = s/(1+2s)` is the correct ratio‚Üífraction conversion (pot ‚áí 1/3, half-pot ‚áí 1/4). The warning comment on `RequiredEquity` is exactly the guard a future "fixer" needs ‚Äî leave it. Re-measured bands reproduce 8d-2's run: **TAG 214.60 > LAG 128.41 > Nit 75.61 ‚âà Station 70.39 ‚â´ Maniac ‚àí500.94 ‚â´ Random ‚àí1523.95 bb/100** (Low, 60k hands, common random numbers); TAG at High 116.56 < Low ‚úì. Two disclosed items ruled on: the homogeneous-all-TAG-field anomaly (Nit/Station outearn TAG there) is **accepted, no retune** ‚Äî ¬ß13's ordering is a claim about the tier's real field mix, and without opponent adaptation nothing exploits a tight range's predictability; and ¬ß13's table row "calling-station hero: negative" **does not hold at Low** (Station +70) ‚Äî also accepted: a Station in a Maniac/LAG-heavy field is passively executing ¬ß6.3's own prescribed exploit against over-bluffers (call more), so its positive rate at Low is the model agreeing with its own theory. The binding ¬ß13 assertion list (TAG top by ‚â•5 bb/100 over every archetype, random hero negative, field gradient) all hold and are harness-pinned.
- **Authoritative `run_monte_carlo_batch` re-run: 167/167, exit 0.** No band moved ‚Äî MLB bit-identity regression guard still exact (PA 48,384; the full tier ladder monotone HS 6.97 R/G ‚Üí MLB 4.28), both macro seasons inside ¬ß8 (.248/.316/.411 @ 4.21, .250/.319/.413 @ 4.29), rivalry empty-ledger neutrality green. Also re-run firsthand: `HoldemHarness` **63/63**, `GrittyEventsHarness` **67/67** (carries the Layer-2 check-10 resolution‚Üíwriters proof), `dotnet build` 0/0 all 8 projects.
- **Minor observations, disclosed-not-actioned:** (1) rake is taken on the *uncalled* portion of a final bet (`CompleteByFold` rakes the whole pot; real rooms return the uncalled bet first) ‚Äî bounded by the 3¬∑BB cap, conservation unaffected; a v2 nicety. (2) A below-entry-threshold hand folds to any preflop raise regardless of price (never defends the BB on pot odds) ‚Äî a VPIP-chart simplification already priced into the measured bands. (3) `HoldemProfile.GetFieldSkew` hands out its shared mutable `double[]` ‚Äî internal-only today; returning `ReadOnlySpan&lt;double&gt;` would be free hardening whenever that file is next touched. (4) `Assets/Economy/Hustles/TexasHoldemLogic.cs` is an empty Phase-0 scaffold leftover (committed in `821d732`, predates the design), unrelated to 8d ‚Äî delete in a future cleanup commit.

**This closes Phase 8d end to end (design + 8d-1 + 8d-2 + Layer 2 + Layer 3 UI + review), pending only the user-driven live playtest.**

## 8e ‚Äî Equipment Quality: SHIPPED end to end (2026-07-05, Fable 5 design + engine + UI, NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî includes the still-uncommitted 8d Layer 3 files in the same tree)

**Closes the interleave plan's 8e item in one pass at schema v9: design doc, all three layers, harness suites, live-save migration.** Design doc: [design/equipment_quality.md](file:///c:/Users/DELL/dirt&diamonds/docs/design/equipment_quality.md) ‚Äî purchasable gear tiers as effective-ratings modifiers, the exact PED/fatigue/rivalry precedent (never a calibration-table edit), and the first mechanic where Life-sim money buys on-field performance.

**The design in one paragraph:** per-player gear quality 0‚Äì3 (no row = 0, standard issue), boosts +0/+2/+4/+6 to batter **Power+Contact** (never Discipline) and pitcher **Stuff+Control** (never Stamina), priced $750/$2,500/$7,500 at full sticker with no trade-in credit (laddering 1‚Üí2‚Üí3 costs $10,750 vs. $7,500 straight to 3 ‚Äî a real save-or-spend decision against the 8a/8b economy). **Upgrade-only, no durability** ‚Äî upkeep is already priced into 8a's weekly cost-of-living bundle, whose own line item reads "rent+food+gear"; the purchase is the capital expenditure. Heirs start at quality 0 (gear is per person, a fresh sink each generation). Avatar-driven in v1, engine-generic per player_id forever.

**What shipped:**

- **Schema v9 = new `Player_Equipment` table** (player_id PK ‚Üí Players CASCADE, quality 1‚Äì3 CHECK, purchased_day, STRICT) ‚Äî the additive Player_Absences pattern, no backfill. **Upgrade-only enforced in SQL**: `ON CONFLICT ... DO UPDATE ... WHERE excluded.quality > quality` (the keep-later absence trick, as keep-higher), so the ledger's in-memory merge applies the identical rule with no read-back. DDL idempotence + upsert semantics (fresh/upgrade/same-no-op/downgrade-no-op) + CHECKs + FK CASCADE + query plans all validated on a scratch db via sqlite3 BEFORE any C# (No Blind Queries).
- **Transport = the RivalryLedger/AvailabilityLedger pattern exactly:** `EquipmentService` writes in its own batch ‚Üí commit ‚Üí publishes primitives-only `PlayerEquipmentChangedEvent` (CoreEvents stays Data-free) + `FundsImpulseEvent` (Life funds mirror); new **`EquipmentLedger`** (`Assets/Simulation/Baseball/`) consumes; `GameManager` hydrates from `LoadAllEquipment` at boot and hands it to all six tier sims + the micro-sim (`GameManager.Gear`, the UI read surface). Sims rebuild flat per-slot `byte` boost caches gated on **Version only** ‚Äî gear never expires by calendar, so no day gating (unlike absences).
- **Order of operations pinned:** baked array value (tier) ‚Üí **gear boost UP** ‚Üí rust dock DOWN ‚Üí rivalry ‚Üí resolver's own PED 1.5√ó. Gear joins the macro PA fast-path conjunction (`rivalry==0 && !shadowed && rust==0 && gear==0` ‚Üí the exact pre-8e resolve call); pitcher gear lands in `EffectivePitcher`/`EffectivePitcherBase` beside rust ‚Äî in the micro-sim **before fatigue seeding**, so fatigue erodes geared ratings like rusty ones. The replacement call-up carries no gear (a stranger ‚Äî the no-rivalry-across-shadowed-slots rule). The human's interactive pitch-chain PAs flow through the same effective-ratings sites, so avatar gear shifts the anchor p* with zero extra plumbing.
- **Layer 2 (`Assets/Economy/Equipment/EquipmentService.cs`):** `GetShopState` snapshot + `TryPurchase(playerId, quality, day, out typed failure)` ‚Äî validates quality 1‚Äì3 / strictly-above-owned / funds ‚â• price against the authoritative Players row, then one batch (`AdjustFunds(-price)` ‚Äî the atomic writer, never `UpdateFunds` ‚Äî + `SetEquipment`), commit, then the two bus impulses (the HustleService/EventConsequenceApplier ordering kept exactly). Every refusal is a clean no-op with a typed reason. Prices live in Economy; rating boosts live in `EquipmentEffects` (Baseball) ‚Äî both first-pass tunable data behind `run_monte_carlo_batch`.
- **Layer 3 (`Assets/UI/EquipmentShopScreen.tscn`/`.cs`):** eighth permanent Main.tscn overlay (declared last), ScheduleScreen's corner-anchored non-blocking idiom at **bottom-left** (schedule owns bottom-right). Render path is fully in-memory per ui_conventions: funds off the Life sim's mirror (`TryGetFunds`), owned tier off the `Gear` ledger, labels dirty-flag gated on (funds, quality); the DB is touched only by an actual purchase click, which re-validates everything anyway. Buy-button prices formatted once at `_Ready` from the service's one price table ‚Äî the scene never hardcodes a dollar figure. `godot_scene_mapper` run against the new `.tscn` before the `.cs` was written.

**Verification:** `dotnet build` 0/0 all 8 projects. **MonteCarloHarness 167‚Üí181/181** (+14, new "Phase 8e equipment quality" suite): boost table + batter/pitcher applier arithmetic pins (identity at 0, clamp at 100), **gear-then-rust order pinned at the clamp** (97‚Üí100‚Üí92, not 95 ‚Äî the reversed order would differ), ledger keep-higher merge semantics, attached-empty-ledger season **BIT-IDENTICAL** to no-ledger (PA 49068/49068), micro attached-empty game bit-identical + geared-lineup same-seed divergence, SQL‚Üîledger hydration round-trip + quality-0 write rejection, **directional league proof** (all-batters-geared q3: AVG .248‚Üí.267, HR 1610‚Üí1772; all-pitchers-geared: AVG .248‚Üí.239, SO 11207‚Üí11504), warm geared game day **0 B**. **No band moved:** MLB bit-identity guard still exact (PA 48384/48384, H 10969/10969, ER 5237/5237), full tier ladder inside every ¬ß4 band and strictly monotone (HS .308/.390/.509 @ 6.97 ‚Üí MLB .249/.318/.417 @ 4.28). **GrittyEventsHarness 67‚Üí72/72** (+5 Layer-2 integration: snapshot, q1 happy path with exact funds/row/ledger/impulse, four typed rejections as true no-ops, 1‚Üí3 rung-skip at full sticker, batch/integrity). CoreLoop 22/22 (Life‚ÜîBaseball boundary scan clean), NeedsDecay 69/69, HustleHarness 31/31, HoldemHarness 63/63. SchemaValidator scratch green + live audit 49‚Üí**51/51** (Player_Equipment in RequiredTables; repo-root validation db topped up to v9). All three hardcoded user_version checks bumped 8‚Üí9 (the standing gotcha, on schedule). Live save migrated v8‚Üív9 through **two clean headless `--quit` boots** (second proves idempotence: 817 players/48 teams/avatar intact, integrity ok, Player_Equipment empty as expected) + an MCP-driven boot with the shop overlay live in the tree across multiple frames, zero errors ‚Äî every `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` resolves and the `_Process` render path runs against the real save.

**Disclosed simplifications (design doc ¬ß9):** no durability/wear (upkeep is the CoL bundle); no fielding/team-defense or stamina effect (defense is a baked mean ‚Äî the 8c call-up disclosure's sibling); one bundled gear scalar, no per-slot itemization; NPCs never shop (league lines move only through the harness's synthetic worlds until content says otherwise); tier-flat pricing (revisit with 9c's economy movement); mirror-vs-DB funds drift means the shop's Disabled predicate can lag the authoritative row by a day's unflushed spending ‚Äî same class as the hustle buy-in check, and `TryPurchase` re-validates server-side regardless. **Known gap, same class as every prior UI entry:** no input-injection path drives a real purchase click headlessly ‚Äî the buy flow end-to-end (click ‚Üí funds label drop ‚Üí button disable flip) is verified by the Layer-2 harness checks + code inspection + the clean live boot, not by a watched purchase; a manual playtest (open the shop bottom-left, buy Quality gear, check funds and the at-bat feel) is how to see it live.

## 9c ‚Äî Promotion / Advancement Gates: DESIGN DOC done (2026-07-05, Opus 4.8, design only ‚Äî NO code)

**`docs/design/promotion_advancement_gates.md`.** Turns the interleave plan's "a generated player climbs HS‚ÜíMLB across simulated seasons" into the offseason mechanism that moves players up/down the 9a tier ladder. Confirmed scope this pass: **the promotion model (Opus) + the avatar tier-transfer contract for Fable**; no C#. Load-bearing decisions:

- **No schema change** (a first for a 9x pass). Every move is `PlayerQueries.SetTeam` (existing), removal is `SetTeam(null)` (the succession-retiree precedent), intake is `LeagueGenerator.GeneratePlayer` (existing), and a player's tier is *derived* from their team's `Team_Tiers` row ‚Äî moving teams moves tiers for free. The advancement score is computed at evaluation time and thrown away, so nothing needs storing. `user_version` stays at **9**.
- **The roster invariant is a hard conservation law** (the chip-conservation / 9+5+3 sibling): after every offseason pass every tier is exactly 8 teams √ó (9 batters + 5 starters + 3 relievers), rostered population constant at 816, `#intake ‚â° #removals` per year. Proven by the ladder being **six equal 136-slot leagues** (not a pyramid ‚Äî the uniform 8√ó17 9a simplification) reconciled by a **single top-down per-role sweep**: merit swaps (net-0 matched exchange, with a `SwapMargin` for hysteresis), vacancy promotions (‚àí1 lower/+1 upper, the hole cascades down), removals (retire at 42/health‚â§40 reusing `HeirGeneticsProfile`; amateur age-out past `TierAgeCap`), terminating in HS intake generation. Each boundary√órole is an independent matched reconciliation ‚Üí conservation is trivially provable/harness-exact.
- **The advancement score `A = wP¬∑P + wS¬∑S`** (first-pass wP=wS=0.5, all constants in a new `PromotionProfile`): **P** = tier-relative, reliability-shrunk season line (batter OPS/tierOPS, pitcher tierERA/ERA, both `1 + w¬∑(raw‚àí1)` with `w = PA/(PA+PA_k)`) off the existing `LoadLeague*Totals(year, tier)` aggregates ‚Äî the "did you dominate your level" signal that auto-recalibrates by tier; **S** = role-summed `Player_Ratings` (the exact `FindDisplacedPlayer`/`EvaluateSuccession` metric, reused) + a modest age-upside bonus ‚Äî the "do your tools project up" signal. Tier-relative ratings (50=avg everywhere) + baked `TierEffects` environment are what make cross-tier comparison honest; a HS masher's P falls toward 100 as he climbs while S (raw tools) justified the climb.
- **Runs on `SeasonRolledOverEvent`**, a new `PromotionManager` (Baseball-only) attached **after** `CareerManager` so it sees post-`AgeAllPlayers`/post-succession state and final normalized season stats. Two precedented correctness reqs handed to Fable: **FlushPending on affected tier sims before re-init** (rollover fires after new-season day-1 games ‚Äî 1-game-stale roster disclosed, the succession-mid-season precedent) and **one batch + a forked `RngState`** for intake (no stream perturbation), then re-`Initialize()` all six tier sims + micro + re-activate the avatar (the `Succeed` tail generalized).
- **Avatar tier-transfer = Fable's contract (¬ß6):** ranked by the same `A`, promotes to a real upper-tier team+slot (the out-ranked incumbent relegates into the vacated slot), `Succeed`-sibling mutation ‚Äî `_avatarTeamIndex` re-resolves against the *new* tier (the 9a tier-relative-index discipline), `SetAttendedTeam` re-established, **`AvatarChangedEvent` republished** so the 9b school-gate flips across HS‚ÜíCollege‚ÜíMinorA for free. Skipped when a succession is pending (avatar on its way out); **v1 recommendation = avatar promotes but never auto-relegates** (kinder feel, one flag from symmetric ‚Äî flagged tunable, not a blocker; NPC relegation fully modeled).
- **9c sorts; 9d moves.** With static ratings the ladder reaches a talent-stratified equilibrium after a few seasons (itself a testable steady state ‚Äî acceptance check 9); the ¬ß2.2 age bonus is the seam 9d replaces with a real rating trajectory.
- **¬ß10 acceptance** (MonteCarloHarness): neutrality/bit-identity guard (inert until a rollover), the roster-invariant conservation law, cream-rises HS‚ÜíMLB (the BUILD_PLAN exit criterion as a hard assertion), retirement/intake balance, performance-shrinkage + scouting/age gates, the avatar cross-tier handoff, determinism/stream-isolation, talent equilibrium. SchemaValidator unchanged. **¬ß12 suggested split:** 9c-1 NPC churn engine + harness (checks 1‚Äì6,8,9), 9c-2 avatar handoff (check 7). Fable review is lighter than 8b (no `AtBatResolver` calibration touched ‚Äî only *which* players sit in which tier sim): neutrality "no band moved" + the conservation sign-off + the avatar-handoff roster-invariant sign-off.

## 9c ‚Äî Promotion / Advancement Gates: SHIPPED end to end (2026-07-05, Fable 5, 9c-1 + 9c-2 in one pass, NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî shares the tree with the uncommitted 8d L3 + 8e files)

**Implements `docs/design/promotion_advancement_gates.md` exactly: the offseason sorting mechanism (NPC churn engine, 9c-1) and the avatar tier-transfer handoff (9c-2). No schema change ‚Äî `user_version` stays 9, as designed (a first for a 9x pass); SchemaValidator untouched.**

**What shipped:**

- **`Assets/Simulation/Baseball/PromotionManager.cs`** ‚Äî three pieces in the HeirGenetics file shape: **`PromotionProfile`** (every ¬ß2/¬ß3 constant as data: `wP=wS=0.5`, `PA_k=200`/`IP_k=40`, `AgeBonusMax=10` tapering to 0 at `PeakAge=27`, `SwapMargin=5`, `SwapCap` 2/1/1 per role, `TierAgeCap` HS 19/College 23, intake ages 15‚Äì16; retirement 42/health 40 **reused** from `HeirGeneticsProfile`, never duplicated); **`PromotionScore`** (pure, DB-free, RNG-free ‚Äî the harness pins fixtures against it): batter P = OPS/tierOPS with OPS recomputed from counting stats via the exact `SqlNormalizeBattingRates` formula, pitcher P = tierERA/ERA, both shrunk `1+w¬∑(raw‚àí1)` and **ratio-capped at 3.0** (a new profile constant found during implementation: without it a 1-out 0.00-ERA scrap produces an unbounded ratio no shrinkage weight tames); **`PromotionManager`** (the ¬ß3 sweep + one-batch mutation + re-init tail). One deliberate deviation from ¬ß8's ctor list: `GlobalState` omitted (the rollover event already carries the season year) and `CareerManager` rides an optional `Career` attachment property (the sims' ledger-reference pattern) rather than a ctor arg, so NPC-only harness worlds skip the avatar path entirely.
- **The sweep is the ¬ß3 conservation model literally:** forced removals (retire/health) leave before ranking and can never promote *or* relegate; the top-down MLB‚ÜíHS per-role pass finalizes each tier's amateur age-outs at that tier's turn (after their boundary-above promotion chance has passed ‚Äî an aged-out player who earns promotion keeps it), fills each tier's need from the tier below's best-by-`A` (ties on player_id everywhere), then runs capped+margined merit swaps as **direct team exchanges** (the riser takes the incumbent's exact slot and vice versa ‚Äî trivially net-zero); HS terminates every cascade with generated 15‚Äì16-year-old intake at `DefaultRatingSpread` (+arsenals for pitchers). Vacancy arrivals assign best-score‚Üílowest-team_id against the tier's sorted vacated slots; the arrivals‚â°vacancies reconciliation is asserted loudly per tier√órole. **A pass that moves nobody is a complete no-op** ‚Äî no flush, no re-init, bit-identical world (the empty-ledger-neutrality bar, and what makes the stream-isolation check provable).
- **¬ß4 ordering honored:** subscribed after `CareerManager` in `GameManager` (sims flush ‚Üí world ages + succession ‚Üí promotion); `FlushPending()` on every registered tier sim before mutation (the new-season day-1 blip survives ‚Äî 1-game-stale roster disclosed, the succession precedent); ONE batch for every `SetTeam`/intake; the only RNG is intake generation from a dedicated forked stream; then re-`Initialize()` all registered sims + micro once and `Career?.ReactivateAvatar()`. New disclosure of implementation's own: **background relievers rank almost purely on scouting** ‚Äî the macro-sim's complete-game shape gives them no season line (self-healing if the macro sim ever grows bullpens).
- **9c-2 avatar handoff (¬ß6):** when eligible (career attached, no pending succession, lineage alive) the avatar **rides the same cohort ranking with an `IsAvatar` flag** ‚Äî pickable as a vacancy riser or merit-swap riser exactly like an NPC (the "clears the same bar" gate is literal, not a parallel scoring path), never a removal candidate or relegation target (v1 promotes-never-relegates), swap destination = the out-ranked incumbent's exact slot with the incumbent relegated into the avatar's vacated one. New **`CareerManager.ReactivateAvatar()`** (the `Succeed` tail generalized cross-tier): re-reads the avatar's team post-commit, **clears the attended-team claim on every registered tier sim** ‚Äî a cross-tier move must not leave the ORIGIN sim skipping its old team's games forever (implied but unspelled in ¬ß6; caught and pinned by the origin-release harness check) ‚Äî then the standard activation: tier-relative `_avatarTeamIndex` re-resolve, `_avatarSlot` re-find, `SetAttendedTeam` on the new tier's sim, `AvatarChangedEvent` republished (the 9b bridge re-points the Life-sim clock + school gate for free). New `LeagueDirectory.TryGet` for sparse-registration worlds.
- **Query layer (No Blind Queries honored):** two new bulk reads in `BaseballQueries` ‚Äî `LoadSeasonBattingLines`/`LoadSeasonPitchingLines(seasonYear)` + `SeasonBattingLine`/`SeasonPitchingLine` DTOs ‚Äî validated against the **live v9 save** via the sqlite MCP before writing (816 rostered confirmed; plans are deliberate full scans: the UNIQUE index leads on player_id and ¬ß7 forbids a new index ‚Äî a once-per-offseason cold read, documented on the SQL constants). Everything else reads existing surfaces (`LoadRoster`, `LoadAllTeams`, `LoadAll`, `LoadLeague*Totals(year, tier)`) and mutates through existing writers (`SetTeam`, `GeneratePlayer`).
- **`GameManager`:** new public `Promotions` property ‚Äî a future ladder/news UI reads `PromotionManager.LastRun` (a `PromotionSummary`: removals/promotions/relegations/intake/avatar destination ‚Äî the `LastSuccession` seam pattern).

**Verification ‚Äî the three ¬ß12 sign-offs, all green.** `dotnet build` 0/0 solution-wide; **MonteCarloHarness 181‚Üí203/203, exit 0** (+22 across three new suites):

- **Neutrality "no band moved":** every pre-9c check untouched ‚Äî MLB bit-identity guard exact (PA 48384/48384, H 10969/10969, ER 5237/5237), full tier ladder inside every band and strictly monotone (HS .308/.390/.509 @ 6.97 R/G ‚Üí MLB .249/.318/.417 @ 4.28), succession/availability/equipment suites all green. Plus the stream-isolation proof: two same-seed worlds, one with the pass attached **and firing but choosing no-op** (spread-0 ratings, ages pinned inside every tier's window) ‚Äî season 2 **BIT-IDENTICAL across all six tiers**, with `LastRun` proving the pass ran and evaluated (¬ß10.1 + ¬ß10.8's fork-isolation clause).
- **Conservation sign-off (¬ß10.2, the hard law):** a 12-offseason world (spread 25, gameless ‚Äî scouting-driven ranking; the removal machine runs hot: HS/College age-out waves from year 2, the MLB retirement wave from year 6) ‚Äî **every rollover: 48 teams √ó exactly 9+5+3, 816 rostered, intake ‚â° removals.** Removal triad (42-retiree with stats intact in FA, health-39 starter, HS age-out) exactly matched by 3 HS intakes. **¬ß10.3 cream rises:** a max-rated 15-year-old climbs exactly one rung per offseason, HS‚ÜíMLB in 5, then holds; symmetric: a zero-rated MLB bat relegates rung-per-year then washes out at the College age cap (MinorAAA‚ÜíAA‚ÜíA‚ÜíCollege‚ÜíFA). **¬ß10.8 determinism:** two same-seed 3-year worlds produce byte-identical rosters including generated intake ids (66 removals / 53 promotions each). **¬ß10.9 pre-9d equilibrium:** HS strictly weakest (142.5 mean batter talent), MLB strictly strongest (172.8, gap 30.3), College out-sorts HS; the middle minors hover at the generation mean **by construction** (no age caps, no retirements until the founding generation ages through ‚Äî movement there is only capped swaps + the retirement cascade), so strict middle-rung monotonicity is explicitly 9d's development-curve handoff, not a static-ratings property. ¬ß2 score fixtures: 3-PA 2.500-OPS fluke 103.0 vs full-season star 121.4; ERA‚àí ordering with the 1-out cup capped at 101.7; scouting age/ceiling gates + the ¬ß2.3 both-signals-bind fixture (blue-chip teen 120.4 > hot low-ceiling vet 101.0).
- **Avatar-handoff roster-invariant sign-off (¬ß10.7):** a real 2-season game world ‚Äî the dominating HS avatar promotes to a real College team+slot on its first offseason (via merit swap with need=0 ‚Äî the pure-swap path); **the out-ranked incumbent from the avatar's destination team relegates into the avatar's vacated HS slot** (¬ß6's destination, asserted precisely); roster invariant exact across the handoff; `AvatarChangedEvent` republished with the destination team; season-1 stats persist by player_id; the next pending game schedules in the **College** round-robin and plays clean through the re-initialized micro-sim; **origin released** ‚Äî the HS tier completes a full 1232-start season after the avatar leaves (a stale attended claim would skip a pairing per day); **succession precedence** ‚Äî a parked pending succession skips the (still-dominant) avatar's promotion while NPC churn runs (40 removals), then `ResolvePendingSuccession` hands the College franchise to the heir cleanly.

**Harness-fixture lessons (all three first-run failures were fixture bugs, not engine bugs):** pin ages per tier when forcing a no-op (a flat 25 sits over both amateur age caps and legitimately empties HS+College); assert the ¬ß6 counterpart precisely (other College players legally relegate onto the same team whenever their swap-riser was a teammate); read tier-joined aggregates BEFORE the next rollover's removals drop players out of the join (`Load*Totals(year, tier)` joins by CURRENT team).

**Disclosed simplifications ‚Äî the design's ¬ß11 set carries, plus implementation's own:** relievers score on S almost alone; a swap-relegated College player can land in HS above its age cap and washes out the following offseason (boundary yo-yo with a one-year lag); the 3.0 performance-ratio cap; the free-agent pool still grows unbounded (pre-existing). Economy stays tier-flat ‚Äî 8e's "revisit with 9c" pricing lever deliberately deferred to a follow-on.

## 9d ‚Äî Development & Decline Curves: DESIGN DOC done (2026-07-05, Opus 4.8, design only ‚Äî NO code)

**`docs/design/development_decline_curves.md`.** Turns the interleave plan's "peak-age growth / veteran decline curves; the Practice block finally produces a real stat effect" into the mechanism that makes a player's *ratings themselves* move over a career. Confirmed scope this pass: **the curve model + the potential concept + the Practice lever + the season-boundary pass + the `AgeBonus` seam evolution** (Opus); Sonnet owns the tuning harness (the ¬ß7 equilibrium calibration), Fable implements + reviews. Load-bearing decisions:

- **Schema change (the first of the 9x line): `Player_Potential` v10.** A per-player latent ceiling per rating, the additive `Player_Absences`/`Player_Equipment` table pattern; **pure-SQL backfill copies current ratings as potential** (the `Pitch_Arsenals`/`Team_Tiers` copy-from-`Player_Ratings` precedent) so the founding generation is frozen at current (decline-only) and only post-v10 intake gets the full growth arc ‚Äî a controlled, non-lurching rollout. Rejected the no-schema incremental model (collapses talent spread + mean-drift-fragile; ¬ß3.4); stored potential anchors spread and makes the steady state well-defined. `user_version` 9‚Üí10.
- **The curve (`DevelopmentCurve`/`DevelopmentProfile`, pure/DB-free/`bell`-injectable ‚Äî the `PromotionScore`/`HeirGenetics` precedent):** three phases pivoting on `PeakAge` **reused from `PromotionProfile.PeakAge` (27)**. Growth = exponential approach to potential (fraction of the remaining gap, `youthWeight` tapering to 0 at peak ‚Äî asymptotes at the ceiling, never overshoots = the stationarity property). Decline = accelerating erosion off current rating (`ageWeight` steepening toward 42), with a **physical/skill `kindWeight` split** (discipline/control hold up, power/stuff/stamina fade ‚Äî the crafty-veteran texture) and a **`healthScale` coupling** (low health declines faster, reusing the existing stat, feeding the health‚â§40 retirement floor). Bust/breakout jitter from a **forked `RngState`** (never perturbs sim/career streams).
- **Raw intake is the band-moving lever:** `LeagueGenerator.GeneratePlayer` (+ heir/avatar creation) rolls potential at the normal distribution and current at a `ProspectDiscount` *below* it, shrinking to 0 by peak ‚Äî a fresh 15-yo is raw-now/projectable-later. A max-built create-a-player avatar has zero headroom (decline only) = disclosed character-creation risk/reward.
- **The Practice lever (the "Practice finally does something" payoff):** the avatar's scheduled Practice hours accumulate into an additive `Game_State` key `avatar_practice_credit` via the **`GameManager` bridge** (Life‚ÜíBaseball through the sanctioned seam, no wall break), consumed + cleared by `DevelopmentManager` at rollover into an extra growth fraction (diminishing returns + seasonal cap). **Succession guard:** a freshly-succeeded heir gets none of the retiree's credit (`Career.LastSuccession.Kind != Succeeded`, not dispatch-timing-luck). Avatar-only (the 8a cost-of-living precedent).
- **Runs on `SeasonRolledOverEvent`**, new `DevelopmentManager` (Baseball-only) attached **between `CareerManager` and `PromotionManager`** so it sees post-`AgeAllPlayers` ages and the sweep sorts on the just-developed ratings ‚Äî **develop-before-sort is load-bearing** ("climbs because he developed"; `P` = what he did at old ratings, `S` = what he now is; 9c conservation math untouched). Flush-before-re-init + one-batch + forked-RNG, the 9c reqs; a no-rating-change pass is a complete no-op. Discloses the negligible double-re-init when both season-boundary managers fire.
- **The `AgeBonus` seam (¬ß13's named seam):** `PromotionScore.AgeBonus(age)` ‚Üí `ProjectionBonus(age, headroom)` where `headroom = Œ£(potential‚àícurrent)` ‚Äî scouting now projects *real remaining headroom* instead of the age-only fudge. Small, additive change; no touch to the ¬ß2.3 combine or conservation.
- **The band-move contract (¬ß7 ‚Äî the key framing):** 9d is the **first pass that legitimately MOVES the tier bands** (every prior pass signed off "no band moved"; 9d's whole purpose is to move the steady state). Acceptance is a **new stationary equilibrium** Sonnet calibrates the band checks to, with the 9c middle-minors flatness **perturbed into a monotone gradient**; the MLB bit-identity guard still holds (no-rollover world) and 9d is inert without a rollover. Structural guarantee: a steady state *exists* (bounded ratings, growth asymptotes at stationarily-drawn potential, decline feeds retirement) ‚Äî the numbers are Sonnet's tuning.
- **¬ß10 acceptance** (MonteCarloHarness): inert-without-rollover neutrality, deterministic curve fixtures, the growth arc (raw prospect climbs *because he develops* ‚Äî distinct from 9c's already-max cream-rises), decline‚Üírelegation‚Üíretirement (no new retirement logic), the Practice lever, the new stationary equilibrium, determinism/stream-isolation, conservation-still-holds, the scouting-seam, v9‚Üív10 migration. **¬ß12 split:** 9d-1 curve+schema+generation (engine core), 9d-2 Practice lever + `AgeBonus` seam, Sonnet's tuning-harness pass alongside. Fable review is heavier than 9c (9d *does* move the steady state): the band-move sign-off (first legitimate re-baseline), curve correctness, stream isolation, the Practice proof, conservation re-run.

## 9d-1 ‚Äî Development Engine Core SHIPPED (2026-07-05, Fable 5, NOT YET COMMITTED)

**The ¬ß12 first slice of `docs/design/development_decline_curves.md`: the curve + schema v10 + generation + the season-boundary pass.** No Practice bridge, no scouting seam (both 9d-2, per the doc's own split). Acceptance checks 1‚Äì4, 7, 8, 10 all green.

**What shipped:**

- **Schema v10 ‚Äî `Player_Potential` (the first 9x schema change), validate-first honored literally:** the DDL + backfill + all three query plans were proven on a sqlite3 scratch db *before any C# was written* (idempotent re-apply; backfill copies-then-never-clobbers ‚Äî potential stayed 61 while a developed current moved to 90; an intake-written row survives the backfill; CHECK bounds + FK + cascade all reject/fire correctly; bulk load and PK probe both ride the PK autoindex). Additive table + `INSERT OR IGNORE` copy-from-`Player_Ratings` backfill in `SchemaDefinitions.sql`; `user_version` 9‚Üí10 with **all three hardcoded harness checks bumped in the same edit** (the standing gotcha, not repeated); `SchemaValidator.RequiredTables` gains the table.
- **`Assets/Simulation/Baseball/DevelopmentManager.cs`** ‚Äî four pieces in the `PromotionManager.cs` file shape: **`RatingKind`** (the 7-rating enum for the kindWeight split); **`DevelopmentProfile`** (`GrowthRate=0.5` fraction-of-gap at full youth weight, `DeclineRate=6.0` pts/season at age-42 weight, `SkillKindWeight=0.5` for BatDiscipline/PitControl vs physical 1.0, `HealthDeclineCoefficient=1.0` ‚Üí healthScale 1.6 at the health-40 floor with 0 as the clean off-switch, `JitterSpread=2.0`, `ProspectDiscount=20` **first-pass mild by design**, `AvatarCreationHeadroom=15`, `PracticeFracCap=0.25`; peak 27 / youngest 15 / retirement 42 all **reused** from `PromotionProfile`/`HeirGeneticsProfile`, never re-declared); **`DevelopmentCurve`** (pure, DB-free, `bell`-injectable: `youthWeight` linear 1‚Üí0 over 15‚Üí27, `ageWeight` quadratic 0‚Üí1 over 27‚Üí42 ‚Äî **both phase weights AND the jitter scale are zero at the peak**, so the plateau falls out of the math and a peak-pinned roster is a provable no-op; growth clamps at potential = the never-overshoot stationarity anchor; `RawCurrent`/`HeadroomPotential` intake cores); **`DevelopmentSummary`** (`LastRun` seam for a future development UI card); **`DevelopmentManager`** (bulk-loads roster + ages/health + potentials up front, applies the curve per rostered player, one batch of changed-row upserts, flush‚Üícommit‚Üíre-init‚Üí`Career?.ReactivateAvatar()`; a no-change pass is a complete no-op ‚Äî no flush, no re-init).
- **Generation (¬ß3.3) with the frozen-prefix discipline:** in `GeneratePlayer` the rolled vector **IS the potential** ‚Äî deliberately consuming the exact draws the pre-v10 code spent on current ratings, so the M1 main-stream generation prefix never moves ‚Äî and current sits `ProspectDiscount¬∑youthWeight(age)¬∑gapRoll` below it, drawn from a **`Split()` fork** (the v4-reliever precedent; the parent stream is untouched). One caught-in-session hazard: extracting the age roll to a local initially *reordered* the main-stream draws (age would have consumed firstName's draw) ‚Äî fixed by extracting all three locals in the original draw order, now pinned by comment. Reliever stamina penalty caps the *ceiling* too (a reliever can't develop back into starter stamina); arsenals derive from current (what he throws now); spread-0 collapses the discount entirely (calibration rosters stay uniform). **Heirs:** the `HeirGenetics` blend is the potential; current sits the full deterministic birth-age discount below it (gap roll pinned 1.0 ‚Äî same-age heirs shift identically, so succession's best-by-rating ordering is never lottery-scrambled; development supplies the texture once rostered). **Avatar:** chosen build = current, ceiling = `HeadroomPotential` (deterministic +10 at age 19 on a modest 60; a max-built 100 gets zero headroom ‚Äî the disclosed creation risk/reward). Unrostered people (FA, child heirs) don't develop in v1 ‚Äî an heir starts developing when succession rosters him (disclosed).
- **Query surface (No Blind Queries):** `PlayerPotentialRow` DTO + `UpsertPotential`/`LoadAllPotential(dict)`/`TryGetPotential` on `BaseballQueries` ‚Äî plans validated on the scratch db before writing (bulk load is a deliberate once-per-offseason full scan, the 9c season-line precedent, documented on the SQL constant).
- **Wiring:** `GameManager` constructs `Development` with a forked `RngState` and attaches it **between** `Career.AttachTo` and `Promotions` (develop-before-sort); public `Development` property (the `Promotions` seam pattern). `DevelopmentManager` ctor deliberately omits `GameStateQueries` (9d-2 adds it with the practice consumer ‚Äî no dead deps).

**Verification ‚Äî build 0/0 all 8 projects; MonteCarloHarness 203‚Üí233/233, exit 0 (+30 across three new suites); every other suite green: SchemaValidator 53/53 (scratch v10 + live audit), CoreLoop 22/22, GrittyEvents 72/72, NeedsDecay 69/69, Hustle 31/31, Holdem 63/63.**

- **NO band moved (the ¬ß7 nuance, resolved for this slice):** the mild `ProspectDiscount=20` kept every pre-existing band check green ‚Äî HS/College currents drop on *both* sides of the ball, so the tier environments largely cancel (the 9c ¬ß10.9 equilibrium check now reads HS 110.2 ‚Üí MLB 163.6, gap 53.4 ‚Äî wider stratification, same inequalities). **The legitimate band re-baseline remains Sonnet's ¬ß7 deliverable**; the first-pass constants deliberately minimized disruption exactly as ¬ß3.3 prescribes.
- **Curve fixtures (¬ß10.2):** exact bell-injected arithmetic ‚Äî 40‚Üí55 at 15 / 40‚Üí48 at 21 / 40‚Üí40 at peak; a 25/90 prospect converges monotonically to 88 by the peak, never over; decline ‚àí1@33 accelerating to ‚àí4@39, skill half-rate (‚àí2), frail (health 40) ‚àí6; clamps at 0/100/potential; practice +6 at age 20, hard-capped (frac 5.0 ‚â° 0.25), decline relief ‚àí3 vs ‚àí4; `RawCurrent`/`HeadroomPotential` cores exact.
- **The growth arc (¬ß10.3 ‚Äî the BUILD_PLAN exit criterion, distinct-from-9c):** a 24-offseason world with aging‚Üídevelopment‚Üípromotion in live FIFO order: a raw 75-sum/270-ceiling HS 15-year-old is **still in HS after rollover 1** (below the bar ‚Äî 9c's cream promoted immediately; this one can't until he develops), first climbs at rollover 2 with bat sum 205 (+130 developed), peaks at 262/270 at age 27, **reaches MLB**, and declines to 222 by 39. World-gen shape: 816/816 ceiling rows, current ‚â§ potential on every rating, 136/136 HS players carrying real headroom.
- **Decline ‚Üí relegation ‚Üí retirement (¬ß10.4, zero new retirement logic):** a health-worn (60) 36-year-old MLB mid-roster bat declines EVERY rostered season and 9c's existing merit swaps walk him down MinorAAA:95‚ÜíAA:85‚ÜíA:73‚ÜíCollege:58, where the College age cap washes him out ‚Äî row preserved, never re-rostered (the "washes out / hits retirement" clause, wash-out branch).
- **Conservation (¬ß10.8) + invariants:** 24 developed offseasons, every rollover 48√ó9+5+3 / 816 / intake ‚â° removals; **current ‚â§ potential holds world-wide after 24 years** (never-overshoot is global, not per-fixture); the first rollover moved 598 players (+6701/‚àí548 points ‚Äî both directions live).
- **Determinism + stream isolation (¬ß10.7):** two same-seed 3-year developed worlds byte-identical (rosters + ratings + ceilings, 67k-char fingerprint); the peak-pinned no-op pair ‚Äî the pass **fired, bulk-read the world, drew its jitter bells from the dedicated fork, and provably changed nothing** ‚Äî season 2 BIT-IDENTICAL across all six tiers vs the bare world (strictly stronger than the inert-without-rollover clause, which holds structurally: the only subscription is the rollover event).
- **Migration (¬ß10.10):** live save v9‚Üív10 through **two clean headless `--quit` boots** (second proves idempotence) ‚Äî 817/817 potential rows bit-equal to current (no rating jump; founding generation frozen decline-only), 816 rostered / 48 teams / avatar intact, integrity + FK clean; the repo-root validation db migrated via the same idempotent DDL (the Phase-2 precedent), SchemaValidator live audit green.

**Disclosed (implementation's own, beyond the doc's ¬ß11 set):** unrostered heirs are frozen until rostered (the birth discount is their standing handicap until succession rosters them ‚Äî v1); the heir/avatar discounts are deterministic (no gap roll) to keep succession ordering stable, a deliberate narrowing of ¬ß3.3's roll; `LoadAllPotential` reads ALL potential rows (FA'd players included) once per offseason ‚Äî harmless, dictionary-keyed; the double re-init when 9d + 9c both fire stands as the doc discloses.

## 9d-2 ‚Äî Practice Lever + Scouting Seam: SHIPPED (2026-07-05, Fable 5, NOT YET COMMITTED)

**The ¬ß12 second slice of `docs/design/development_decline_curves.md`: the `avatar_practice_credit` accumulate/consume bridge (¬ß4, with the succession guard) and `PromotionScore.AgeBonus` ‚Üí `ProjectionBonus(age, headroom)` (¬ß6). Acceptance checks 5 and 9 green. No schema change ‚Äî the credit is a `Game_State` KV key, exactly as designed.**

**What shipped:**

- **The Game_State surface:** `GameStateKeys.AvatarPracticeCredit` + a new `GameStateQueries.AdjustInt64` (additive `ON CONFLICT ... value = value + excluded.value` counter upsert ‚Äî the AdjustFunds atomic-delta discipline; semantics validated on a sqlite3 scratch db BEFORE the C#, No Blind Queries: absent-key seeds at the delta, present-key accumulates, integers stay integers under the STRICT `ANY` column).
- **The accumulate half (`GameManager`, ¬ß4):** `SubmitDaySchedule` captures the plan's Practice hours beside the existing Work-activity intent (one-shot, dropped by `ClearDaySchedule`); a new `OnPracticeDayAdvanced` handler ‚Äî subscribed after LifeSim's like the hustle seam, so the credited day's block actually ticked ‚Äî banks them via `AdjustInt64`; `OnAvatarChanged` zeroes the pending capture AND the stored key (creation + succession), so a new bloodline always starts at zero. The boot path deliberately does NOT clear (an existing avatar's banked season is his).
- **The conversion (`DevelopmentCurve.PracticeFraction` + `DevelopmentProfile.PracticeFracPerHour=0.0005`):** exponential saturation `cap¬∑(1‚àíe^(‚àírate¬∑h/cap))` ‚Äî initial slope exactly the per-hour knob, strictly diminishing returns, asymptote at the existing `PracticeFracCap=0.25` ("you cannot grind a 40 to a 100 in one winter"). All three ¬ß4 knobs are `DevelopmentProfile` data on the tuning surface.
- **The consume half (`DevelopmentManager`):** gains its `GameStateQueries` ctor arg (as 9d-1 staged); reads the key once per pass, converts, applies the fraction to the avatar's seven ratings only, and **clears the key regardless ‚Äî inside the rating batch when there are writes, standalone when the pass is otherwise a no-op** (credit never banks across seasons; the cap can't be stockpiled around). **The succession guard is the doc's contract, not dispatch-timing luck:** practice applies only when `Career.LastSuccession.Kind != Succeeded` (+ `HasAvatar`/`!IsLineageOver`, the 9c eligibility triple). Note: a rollover that *parks* a pending succession choice also reads `Succeeded` (`EvaluateSuccession`'s outcome is stored on park), so the outgoing retiree's credit is discarded then too ‚Äî conservative in exactly the right direction, per ¬ß4's "the retiree's credit leaves with him".
- **The scouting seam (¬ß6, `PromotionScore`):** new `ProjectionBonus(age, headroom)` ‚Äî the age-tapered upside scaled by `saturate(headroom / HeadroomForFullProjection=30)`; an at-ceiling young player projects **flat**, past the peak the age-driven decline stands regardless of paper headroom. **`AgeBonus` is kept verbatim as the legacy fallback and equals `ProjectionBonus` at saturated headroom** ‚Äî the old fudge was an implicit full-headroom assumption, now stated. New `Scouting(sum, age, headroom)` overload; new `Headroom(in current, in potential, isPitcher)` helper (placed on `PromotionScore` beside its consumer rather than `DevelopmentCurve` as ¬ß8 sketched ‚Äî disclosed placement deviation). `PromotionManager` bulk-loads `Player_Potential` (the 9d-1 `LoadAllPotential` surface) and scores every candidate through the headroom overload; a missing ceiling row reads zero headroom (the v10 backfill semantics).
- **Doc-contradiction resolved in ¬ß6's favor:** the design's parenthetical "(headroom = 0 ‚Üí the current behavior)" is unsatisfiable alongside its own "a young player already at his ceiling projects flat-to-down" ‚Äî the two can't both hold. Resolution: the semantic sentence wins (at-ceiling young reads 0), and "current behavior" survives as the *unchanged `AgeBonus` overload* for callers with no potential in hand. The harness pins the identity `ProjectionBonus(age, h ‚â• 30) ‚â° AgeBonus(age)`.

**Verification ‚Äî build 0/0 all 8 projects; MonteCarloHarness 233‚Üí245/245, exit 0 (+12, new "9d-2 Practice lever + scouting seam" suite); every guard exact: MLB bit-identity (PA 48384/48384, H 10969/10969, ER 5237/5237), full tier ladder inside every ¬ß4 band and strictly monotone (HS .308/.390/.509 @ 6.97 ‚Üí MLB .249/.318/.417 @ 4.28) ‚Äî NO band moved (the legitimate re-baseline remains Sonnet's ¬ß7 deliverable). Sanity suites: CoreLoop 22/22 (boundary scan clean ‚Äî the bridge is a KV write, no wall break), SchemaValidator 70/70, GrittyEvents 72/72, NeedsDecay 69/69, Hustle 31/31, Holdem 63/63. Live save booted headless `--quit` clean (v10, day 48, 48 teams, avatar + 817 NPCs, zero errors).**

- **¬ß4 conversion fixtures:** zero/negative‚Üí0, monotone, exact at the e-fold (`f(500h) = cap¬∑(1‚àí1/e)`), strictly diminishing marginal slices (0.158‚Üí0.058‚Üí0.029 per 500h), first hour ‚â° `PracticeFracPerHour`, asymptote never exceeded.
- **¬ß6 projection fixtures:** at-ceiling young = 0, saturation ‚â° the old `AgeBonus` exactly, half headroom = half bonus, past-peak negative side headroom-blind, `Scouting` overload orders on headroom at equal current ratings.
- **¬ß10.9 the seam in the sweep:** two HS batters with IDENTICAL current line (54/54/54) and age (17) contest one forced College vacancy; only stored headroom separates them (90 vs 0) ‚Äî the high-headroom probe takes the vacated slot, the at-ceiling twin stays down, AND his A (104) now misses the swap bar (100+5) that the old age fudge would have cleared (106.8) ‚Äî the projection is provably no longer fakeable. Roster invariant + integrity hold.
- **¬ß10.5 the Practice lever, driven through the exact accumulate/consume path:** peak-pinned twin worlds (all NPC phase weights AND jitter exactly zero) ‚Äî 6h/day banks 60h by day 10, the rollover consumes AND clears; the practicing avatar (aged to hit the peak at the rollover, so his growth fraction IS the practice term, jitter-free) gains EXACTLY +2 per rating (frac 0.2469 of his 10-point creation headroom) while the idle twin gains zero; the practiced pass changed EXACTLY one player (+14 over 7 ratings), the idle pass was a complete no-op, every NPC bit-identical across the pair.
- **¬ß4 succession guard, deterministic single world:** a 41-year-old founder banks 2,190 hours; the rollover hands off to a peak-age heir seeded with 60-points-per-rating headroom (at 27 his development is EXACTLY the practice term ‚Äî phase weights and jitter zero) ‚Äî the heir develops by exactly zero and the key clears. A leaked credit would have moved him +15 per bat rating; unambiguous.

**Harness-fixture lesson (the 9c "fixture bugs, not engine bugs" successor):** avatar/heir ids are wall-clock GUIDs (in-game runs are deliberately not replay-deterministic), and the development pass draws jitter in roster order ‚Äî so an avatar's random id shifts every later NPC's bell assignment, and any cross-world NPC-bit-identity fixture inherits that nondeterminism (it would also flake run to run). The peak-pinning trick from the 9d-1 stream suite is the cure: at 27 the jitter SCALE is zero by construction, so draw order stops mattering and every number in the fixture is exact.

**Two calibrated checks updated for the seam (disclosed, not silently patched):** (1) 9c's ¬ß6 destination-counterpart check re-scoped to the avatar's batter cohort within `SwapCapBatters` ‚Äî the seam removed the College incumbents' age fudge (headroom 0 at spread-0) while HS risers keep real projection, so more boundary swaps land ex-destination players on the vacated team across roles (observed 3 vs the old exactly-1; the avatar's batter counterpart is still asserted present). (2) 9d-1's ¬ß10.3 "still HS after rollover 1" replaced by "**the seed never climbs raw**": with the seam widening the amateur boundary, the prospect's +88 first develop legitimately clears the bar at rollover 1 ‚Äî which is the doc's own ¬ß5 mechanism ("a player's development this offseason is what pushes his S over the promotion bar"). The check now asserts the first move carries ‚â• +40 developed points AND statically proves the undeveloped 75-sum misses the bar (raw A 78.1 vs the 105 swap bar).

**Disclosed (implementation's own):** the new season's day-1 Practice hours bank into the *just-ended* season's credit (the rollover fires after the new-season day-1 `DayAdvancedEvent` ‚Äî the standing 1-day-stale class, worth at most one day's hours); the planned-hours capture is in-memory like the plan itself (a quit before the day ticks loses that day's capture ‚Äî pacing, not sim state); practice remains avatar-only (¬ß11); the live accumulate path end-to-end (ScheduleScreen submit ‚Üí day advance ‚Üí key) shares the standing `AdvanceDay()`-is-UI-button-only verification gap ‚Äî the harness drives the identical `AdjustInt64` call at the identical cadence, and a manual playtest (schedule Practice hours, play/skip a day, roll a season) is how to watch it live.

## 9d ¬ß7 ‚Äî Tuning harness / equilibrium calibration: SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Sonnet 5, NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî closes acceptance check 6, 9d's central deliverable)

**Found and fixed a real tier-equilibrium inversion the 9d-1 first-pass constants left in place, then baked the fix into a permanent regression suite.** Full detail + the calibrated numbers: [design/development_decline_curves.md ¬ß14 addendum](file:///c:/Users/DELL/dirt&diamonds/docs/design/development_decline_curves.md).

- **Method:** a throwaway (unshipped) multi-generation exploration tool reusing the exact `DevelopmentManager`/`PromotionManager` sources, run for 55‚Äì150 simulated offseasons per trial with time-averaged per-tier talent output (raw per-generation snapshots are too noisy to read by eye ‚Äî averaging over a post-warmup window is what exposes the real steady state).
- **Finding:** at the 9d-1 first-pass constants (`ProspectDiscount=20`, `GrowthRate=0.5`, `DeclineRate=6.0`), College's long-run mean batter talent settles *above* MinorA's ‚Äî a reproducible inversion (confirmed across 3 seeds, 60‚Äì150-year windows), not noise. Root cause: HS/College are the *only* tiers with a hard age cap (19/23), so their whole population is in the pure-growth phase; MinorA/AA/AAA/MLB have no cap short of 42, so each accumulates long-tenured residents who decline in place for a decade-plus before the capped merit-swap machinery (`PromotionProfile.SwapCap*`, deliberately left untouched) or forced retirement finally moves them. At `DeclineRate=6.0` that erosion pulled the pro tiers below College's pure-growth mean.
- **Fix:** halved `DeclineRate` 6.0‚Üí3.0 in `DevelopmentProfile` ‚Äî same accelerating shape, just gentler (first nonzero erosion at age 34 instead of 32, full-health physical rating). `GrowthRate` (tried 0.3‚Äì0.5) and `ProspectDiscount` (tried 20‚Äì45) were tested and do NOT fix the inversion alone ‚Äî the college/pro gap is set by *who declines*, not entry point or growth speed. `DeclineRate=4.0` also clears it but by a thin, seed-fragile ~0.5-point margin; `3.0` clears it by a comfortable, reproducible 2‚Äì3 points.
- **Calibrated equilibrium** (80 offseasons, generations 31‚Äì80 averaged): `HS 124.3 < College 145.1 < MinorA 147.1 < MinorAA 150.2 < MinorAAA 155.4 < MLB 166.0` ‚Äî strictly monotone across all six tiers (the 9c middle-minors flatness is gone), stationary (<3-point drift per tier across the measurement window).
- **New permanent suite:** `Tools/MonteCarloHarness`'s `RunDevelopmentEquilibriumSuite` ("Phase 9d ¬ß7 tuning harness") ‚Äî 80 offseasons, deliberately **no `LeagueSimulator`s attached** (the `RunPromotionSweepSuite`/`RunDevelopmentArcSuite` "no games" convention: with performance `P` shrunk to a constant 100, ranking is a monotone function of scouting `S` alone, so this is behaviorally identical to a real-games run ‚Äî verified empirically, ~2-point agreement ‚Äî but ~5x faster, 17s vs ~95s for 80 years). Asserts strict cross-tier monotonicity, a stationarity bound, and that the 9c roster-conservation law holds across all 80 developed offseasons.
- **No band re-baseline needed elsewhere:** the 9a ¬ß4 static single-season tier bands and the 9c ¬ß10.9 pre-9d equilibrium check both never run `DevelopmentManager` (one plays a single un-rolled-over season, the other never attaches development), so they're insensitive to the `DeclineRate` retune and re-ran green unchanged ‚Äî confirming the fix is scoped exactly to the long-run developed equilibrium it targets.
- **Existing fixtures updated to match the gentler curve:** `RunDevelopmentCurveSuite`'s four decline/kindWeight/healthScale/practice-relief fixtures re-pinned from ages 33/39 to 35/41 (recomputed exact values, since erosion now rounds to 0 at 33 with the halved rate); one 9d-1 growth-arc fixture's peak-to-age-39 decline margin loosened from 20 to 10 points (halved decline ‚áí roughly halved 12-year decline, ~20 points observed vs the old ~42).

**Verification:** `dotnet build DirtAndDiamonds.sln` 0/0 all 8 projects. `MonteCarloHarness` **249/249** (+4: the new ¬ß7 suite's four checks; the loosened threshold was re-pinned in place, not removed). Every other harness re-run clean per the standing "sim assembly touched" rule: `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `SchemaValidator` 70/70, `GrittyEventsHarness` 72/72, `HustleHarness` 31/31, `HoldemHarness` 63/63, `NeedsDecayHarness` 69/69. No schema change ‚Äî this pass is a one-constant `DevelopmentProfile` retune plus one new harness suite.

## 9d closing review ‚Äî SIGNED OFF (2026-07-06, Fable 5 ‚Äî 9d is CLOSED end to end)

**The ¬ß7 band move is signed off ‚Äî the first legitimate re-baseline in the project.** Full verdicts: [design/development_decline_curves.md ¬ß15](file:///c:/Users/DELL/dirt&diamonds/docs/design/development_decline_curves.md).

- **Band move:** `DeclineRate` 3.0 is the right lever (the inversion is a *who-declines* population dynamic, so growth/discount levers correctly failed) and the right magnitude (4.0's ~0.5-point margin is seed-fragile; 3.0's 2‚Äì3 points reproduce). Equilibrium re-ran exactly: HS 124.3 < College 145.1 < MinorA 147.1 < MinorAA 150.2 < MinorAAA 155.4 < MLB 166.0, max drift +2.6 vs the 10-point bound. Scope verified ‚Äî 9a static bands and the 9c pre-9d equilibrium unchanged, MLB bit-identity exact.
- **Re-pinned fixtures verified by independent hand computation** (35:1, 41:3, skill 1, frail 4, relieved 2 ‚Äî all exact); the 20‚Üí10 loosened growth-arc margin is sound (expected ~20-point peak‚Üí39 decline at the halved rate, observed 20).
- **Stream isolation, Practice lever, conservation** all re-ran green (byte-identical same-seed rosters; practice moved exactly one player; roster invariant across 12/24/80 rollovers). Full sweep re-run by Fable: build 0/0, MonteCarlo 249/249, all six other harnesses green at Sonnet's exact tallies.
- **Review corrections (docs only):** check-count arithmetic ("+1 net" ‚Üí +4) and the old-constant erosion onset ("~30" ‚Üí 32 exactly) in the ¬ß14 addendum, this file, and the fixture comment.

Load-bearing decisions:

- **No schema change, no sim touch.** Phase 10 is a pure read-model + chrome phase ‚Äî it never opens `Assets/Simulation/`, so the sim-band discipline is satisfied by *absence of change* (a `git show --stat` is the evidence), and `run_monte_carlo_batch` bands are inert by construction. - **The shell = a new career "home" primary screen, additively (¬ß2).** New `TwoPanelShell.tscn` (Baseball Dashboard | Burner Phone/Bank) replaces `AttendedGameScreen` as what `Main.ShowAppropriateScreen` swaps in when `HasAvatar`; the **entire existing overlay-sibling set is preserved verbatim** (ScheduleScreen/hustles/poker/shop/succession all still launch on top and inherit the theme for free). The dashboard **absorbs `AttendedGameScreen`'s day-advance + play-today role by reusing the exact `TimeManager.AdvanceDay`/`CareerManager.TryGetPendingGame`/`PlayPendingGame` seams** ‚Äî `AttendedGameScreen` retires; it's the one screen replaced, not reskinned. **The day-advance gate is the load-bearing correctness point** (¬ß2.3): the shell's advance control must honor the same "can't advance past a pending choice / parked succession / unplayed attended game" gates ‚Äî Fable's 10a to get right.
- **One theme resource, applied game-wide via `project.godot`'s `gui/theme/custom` (¬ß3)** ‚Äî there is NO theme anywhere today, so this single project-default setting reskins all eleven thin-slice scenes at once (the highest-leverage line in the phase); per-scene `theme_override_*` stays available for the two bespoke panels. Dark "gritty-polaroid" tokens: surfaces/ink/two accents (diamond=positive, dirt=risk)/type-scale/StyleBoxes incl. one reused progress-bar box for needs/season/risk/grade meters.
- **Narrative-as-messages ‚Äî the Opus seam (¬ß4).** The gap: `GrittyEventDefinition` has `Prompt`+`Choices[].Label` but **no sender/contact**. Chosen path (C): an **additive `"contact"` JSON field** + a content-authored `contacts.json` registry (id ‚Üí name/role/portrait_key/tone); untagged events default to a reserved `unknown` thread (never crash/drop). **Persistence read-model:** a sim-side `Game_Logs` write (`event_type="narrative_msg"`, payload `{contact,prompt,choice,choice_index}`) on `GrittyEventResolvedEvent` ‚Äî incl. auto-resolved/forfeited fires ‚Äî that the phone reads back as thread history (live fires still animate via `GrittyEventFiredEvent` for the unread badge). **The phone thread IS the choice surface: it reskins the `EventConsequenceApplier.TryGetPendingChoice`‚Üí`ResolveChoice(i)` seam verbatim (dirty-flag identity check carried over) and `EventChoiceScreen` retires** (one fewer overlay). Wall stays intact ‚Äî contacts are pure Narrative/UI; the sims never learn one exists.

Deliverable = an 8-band `Grade(rating)‚Üíletter` curve **centered so 50=C+ (average regular) and 40=C (the 8c replacement-level call-up floor)**, A+ at 90+, F below 30; deterministic, fixture-pinned at every boundary. Each tool shows **present `Grade(current)` vs future `Grade(potential)`** (the Player_Potential story), and a headline **OFP = `Grade(round(Scouting(sum,age,headroom)))`** ‚Äî the scout's projection and the promotion sweep's projection are the *same number* by construction. Development card reads `DevelopmentManager.LastRun` (the 9d-1 `DevelopmentSummary` seam built for exactly this).
