## 10b ‚Äî Burner Phone: messages: SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Sonnet 5, over Opus's ¬ß4 seam ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**The Burner Phone's Messages tab is live, `EventChoiceScreen` is retired, and every fired gritty event now posts to a threaded contact ‚Äî schema untouched, `Assets/Simulation/` untouched.**

- **The contact dimension (¬ß4.2), option C from the doc:** `GrittyEventDefinition` gains an additive `ContactId` (`GrittyEventModel.cs`/`GrittyEventJson.cs`, same optional-field-with-humanized-fallback pattern as `prompt`/`label`) ‚Äî an omitted `"contact"` resolves to the reserved `"unknown"` id, never a crash. New `Assets/Narrative/Contacts/contacts.json` + `ContactRegistry`/`ContactJson` (hand-walked `JsonDocument`, same discipline as `GrittyEventJson`): five contacts (`unknown`/"Unknown Number", `coach_reyes`, `agent_diaz`, `girlfriend_jess`, `family_mom`) with a strict `ContactRole` enum (Girlfriend/Coach/Agent/Dealer/Fixer/Family/Unknown ‚Äî Dealer/Fixer unused so far, reserved for later content). **`ContactRegistry.Resolve` never throws** ‚Äî it synthesizes the `unknown` fallback even if a future content edit drops that row, so a render call site can never crash on an unrecognized id. **All 19 existing events tagged**, content-driven grouping (not 1:1 with narrative continuity ‚Äî `spring_training_romance` and the `met_someone`‚Üí`starting_a_family`‚Üí`child_is_born` arc share `girlfriend_jess` as one thread): `unknown` √ó4 (the syndicate/arrest arc ‚Äî deliberately anonymous), `coach_reyes` √ó4, `agent_diaz` √ó5 (PED/suspension/injury correspondence), `girlfriend_jess` √ó4, `family_mom` √ó2.
- **Persistence ‚Äî the additive `Game_Logs` write (¬ß4.3), no schema change:** new `Assets/Data/Database/NarrativeLogQueries.cs` (`event_type = "narrative_msg"`, verified via the sqlite MCP against the LIVE save that no existing row uses that namespace ‚Äî only `"pa"`/`"final"` exist ‚Äî and that the read-back SELECT rides `idx_game_logs_player`, temp-B-tree sort acceptable at this row volume). **`EventConsequenceApplier.ApplyChoice` writes the row itself**, inside the same DB batch as the fire's other consequences, immediately after the consequence switch and before the `GrittyEventResolvedEvent` publish ‚Äî the single funnel every path shares (autopilot, `ResolveChoice`, and a forfeited stale pending choice all land here), so the thread reflects what actually happened including choices the player never saw. **Season year computed from the FIRE's day, not "now"** ‚Äî new `GlobalState.SeasonYearForDay(day)` (`SeasonYear` refactored to call it with `CurrentDay`) plus a symmetric static `DayOfSeasonForDay(day)` for the phone's timestamp ‚Äî because a forfeited choice logs with its ORIGINAL fire day, which can lag the live calendar by up to a cooldown window; reading "now" off `GlobalState` would have mis-dated exactly that case (harness-caught: the forfeit-narrative-log check pins day 2, not the day-3 bump). Payload is engine-generated wire format (`{contact,prompt,choice,choice_index}`), round-tripped through `System.Text.Json`'s reflection (de)serializer rather than `GrittyEventJson`'s hand-walked parser ‚Äî that discipline is for loud errors on untrusted authored content, not applicable to a payload only this code ever writes.
- **The phone IS the choice surface (¬ß4.4) ‚Äî `EventChoiceScreen` retired.** New `Assets/UI/BurnerPhone.cs` over the rewritten `BurnerPhone.tscn` (an `ItemList` contact sidebar + a thread `VBoxContainer` in a `ScrollContainer` + a reply-chip `VBoxContainer`). Carries `EventChoiceScreen`'s exact dirty-flag identity check (`TryGetPendingChoice`/`ResolveChoice`, rebuild only on a change of which fire is pending) verbatim ‚Äî reloads the DB-backed thread history only on that transition, never per-frame. When a choice is pending for the avatar, the phone force-switches to that contact's thread, renders the still-unanswered prompt as one more incoming bubble, and renders each choice as a reply-chip button calling `ResolveChoice(i)` ‚Äî identical seam, reskinned. Each persisted `NarrativeMessageRow` renders as an incoming bubble (prompt, with a `Season {y}, day {d}` caption off the theme's `CaptionLabel` variation) followed by an outgoing bubble (the chosen reply), using the theme's `MessageBubbleIncoming`/`MessageBubbleOutgoing` variations built in 10a specifically for this. Contacts sort most-recent-first (a live pending fire always wins the sort); an in-memory `_lastSeenCount` per contact (not persisted ‚Äî read-state is UI polish, not save state) drives an unread marker that clears the instant a thread opens, including a still-unanswered pending prompt. `EventChoiceScreen.cs/.tscn/.uid` deleted; five stale cross-references in `Main.cs`/`ScheduleScreen.cs`/`SuccessionScreen.cs`/`BirthNotificationScreen.cs` repointed to `SuccessionScreen`/`BurnerPhone` (the `AttendedGameScreen`-deletion precedent from 10a).
- **The wall holds:** contacts are pure Narrative/UI content: `GrittyEventJson`'s "contact" parse never references `ContactRegistry` (the two content files load independently ‚Äî cross-checking them is `check_event_graph_integrity`'s job, not a runtime dependency), and neither Baseball nor Life ever learns a contact exists.

**Verification:** `dotnet build DirtAndDiamonds.sln` 0/0 all 8 projects (one `.csproj` edit needed: `GrittyEventsHarness` compiles `Assets/Narrative/Events/*.cs` directly and needed the sibling `Assets/Narrative/Contacts/*.cs` glob added). `GrittyEventsHarness` 72‚Üí**82/82** (+10: 5 contact-registry checks ‚Äî parses/resolves `unknown`, synthesizes the fallback when a batch omits it, rejects an unrecognized role, rejects a duplicate id, the additive-field default; 5 narrative-log checks ‚Äî a resolved fire logs exactly one row with the right contact/prompt/choice/day/season, an untagged event defaults to `unknown`, a forfeited choice logs its ORIGINAL day not the bump day, resolving the still-open choice appends a second row). All other harnesses re-run per the standing "shared Core/Data files touched" rule, all green at their standing tallies: `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22, `SchemaValidator` 70/70, `NeedsDecayHarness` 69/69, `HustleHarness` 31/31, `HoldemHarness` 63/63, `MonteCarloHarness` 249/249 (no band moved). `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` empty ‚Äî confirmed no sim file touched, `run_monte_carlo_batch` inert by construction. `check_event_graph_integrity`'s content-graph checks (orphaned prerequisites, dead-end flags, unpaced loops, scope/weight sanity) are unaffected by this batch ‚Äî no prerequisite/consequence/cooldown changed, only the additive `contact` field; its new "every event's contact resolves in the registry or is `unknown`" rule is now a permanent harness check (0 unresolved of 19). Live headless boot via the Godot MCP against the real dev save: schema **v10 unchanged**, day 48, avatar + 817 NPCs, 19 gritty events, **zero debug-output errors across ~20 seconds of live frames** with the new `BurnerPhone.cs` in the tree (the shell already had an avatar so the Messages tab was live and polling every frame). sqlite MCP confirmed the read query plan (`SEARCH Game_Logs USING INDEX idx_game_logs_player`) and the live schema's exact column/nullability match against `NarrativeLogQueries`' INSERT ‚Äî no dummy row written to the live save (the harness's scratch-db checks are the write-path proof instead).

**Disclosed:** the live dev save predates this write, so its phone opens with genuinely empty threads (the standing pre-10b-saves-have-no-back-history nuance, unchanged from the design doc) ‚Äî seeing a real thread fill requires the standing manual playtest (create/advance an avatar, trigger a fire, answer it in the phone), same AdvanceDay-is-UI-button-only posture as every prior UI phase. Portraits (`portrait_key` parsed, stored, unused) and `tone` styling metadata wait for 10e. The ¬ß4.5 stretch (relationship/life-beat system-authored messages) was not attempted ‚Äî the required gritty-event thread was the full budget for one session.

## 10c ‚Äî Baseball Dashboard: scouting: SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Sonnet 5, over Opus's ¬ß5 grade-curve math ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**The scouting report card is live on `BaseballDashboard.tscn`: present/future grades per role tool, the OFP headline, tier standing, and the last-offseason development summary. Zero `Assets/Simulation/` touch (`git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` empty), per the phase's load-bearing invariant.**

- **The grade curve ‚Äî new `Assets/UI/Scouting/ScoutingGrade.cs`, deliberately outside `Assets/Simulation/`** (pure/Godot-free, mirroring `PromotionScore`'s style) so the phase's "no sim touch" claim holds by construction while still being harness-testable: `GradeLetter` (8 bands) + `Grade(int rating)` (the exact ¬ß5.2 switch, open-ended at both tails ‚Äî no clamp needed, `100`/`-10` both saturate correctly) + `Label()`. Tested by folding into **`Tools/MonteCarloHarness`** (one new `.csproj` compile-glob line for `Assets/UI/Scouting/*.cs`, the `GrittyEventsHarness`-Contacts-folder precedent from 10b) rather than a new Tools project ‚Äî "whichever harness already compiles the DTO layer" per the doc's own acceptance check 4, and the one that already compiles `PromotionScore` for the OFP fixture.
- **DISCLOSED FINDING, not silently patched (flagged for Fable/Opus, same class as the two 8b findings): ¬ß5.3's literal `Grade(round(Scouting(...)))` over-grades almost everyone.** `PromotionScore.Scouting` is deliberately **100-centred** (`Combine`'s own internal ranking convention ‚Äî an exactly-average, peak-age, zero-headroom role sum of 150 scores exactly `100.0`), not the 0-100/50-average domain `Grade()`'s bands are calibrated to; read literally, an average rostered player would project **A+**, and only a role-average rating under ~15 would clear the F floor. This is a doc/implementation scale mismatch, not a resolver bug ‚Äî `Scouting` is verbatim-correct for `Combine`'s own use. **Fix, disclosed in `ScoutingGrade.OfpRating`'s doc comment: halve it.** At peak age with zero headroom, `Scouting = 2¬∑roleAvgRating` exactly, so `Scouting/2` lands back on `Grade`'s 50-average domain precisely, with `ProjectionBonus` still nudging young/high-headroom prospects up the same way it does for the real sweep. `ScoutingGrade.OfpRating(roleRatingSum, age, headroom)` implements the recentered form; `OfpGrade` runs it through `Grade()`. Harness-pinned: an exactly-average peak-age player with no headroom projects exactly 50 (C+); a peak-age replacement-level player (3√ó40, the 8c call-up floor) projects exactly 40 (C); a 15-year-old with saturated headroom projects above his raw floor while an identical one with none doesn't.
- **`BaseballDashboard.tscn`/`.cs`:** new `ScoutingCard` (`Card` theme variation) holding the OFP headline (`DisplayLabel`), a tier-standing line, and four `ToolRow0..3` rows (`NameLabel` + a default-themed `ProgressBar` filled to the *current* rating + a `GradeLabel` rendering `"{presentGrade} {current} ‚Üí {futureGrade} {potential}"`) ‚Äî batters show Power/Contact/Discipline/Fielding, pitchers show Stuff/Control/Stamina/Fielding, role-switched at render time; plus a `DevCard` reading `GameManager.Development.LastRun` (season/players-changed/points-up/points-down, or a "no offseason yet" text before the first rollover). All player-facing strings are `[Export]` templates on the scene (the `OutcomeNamesCsv`/`AbsenceReasonText` precedent), including a `TierNamesCsv` (LeagueTier enum order) for tier display names ‚Äî nothing hardcoded in C#. **Inputs are all existing reads, no new query**: `PlayerQueries.TryGetById` (age/team), `BaseballQueries.TryGetRatings`/`TryGetPotential`/`TryGetTeamTier` (all already existed as single-row PK lookups); a local `RosterPlayerRow` is assembled in the dashboard from those three reads purely to call the *existing* `PromotionScore.Headroom(in RosterPlayerRow, in PlayerPotentialRow, bool)` overload unchanged ‚Äî avoided adding a `PlayerRatingsRow` overload to `PromotionManager.cs` specifically to keep the zero-Simulation-touch invariant literal, not just spiritual.
- **Refresh granularity:** recomputed at every point `RefreshDayLabel()` already is (boot, post-pending-game resolution, Skip Day, game-finish) ‚Äî day-advance is the only thing that can move ratings (PED costs, the offseason development pass), so per-day is the correct dirty-flag granularity per `ui_conventions.md`, not per-frame. Card+dev-card both hide when `!HasAvatar` (mirrors the `AvailabilityLabel` pattern).

**Verification:** `dotnet build DirtAndDiamonds.sln` 0/0 all 8 projects. **`MonteCarloHarness` 249‚Üí258/258** (+9: 4 boundary-fixture checks incl. the exact ¬ß5.2 pins + the open-tail saturation case, 1 present/future check, 4 OFP checks incl. the literal-formula equivalence with the disclosed `/2` recentering) ‚Äî **no band moved** (the standing 80-offseason equilibrium re-confirmed byte-for-byte: HS 124.3 < College 145.1 < MinorA 147.1 < MinorAA 150.2 < MinorAAA 155.4 < MLB 166.0). `CoreLoopHarness` 22/22 (wall scan clean ‚Äî `Assets/UI` was never in scope), `SchemaValidator` 70/70 (no schema touch, `PRAGMA user_version` still 10 ‚Äî asserted not assumed), `NeedsDecayHarness` 69/69, `GrittyEventsHarness` 82/82, `HustleHarness` 31/31, `HoldemHarness` 63/63, all unchanged (sanity re-run ‚Äî nothing they compile changed). `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` **empty** ‚Äî confirmed, not just claimed. Live headless boot via the Godot MCP against the real dev save: schema v10 unchanged, day 48, avatar + 817 NPCs, 72 relationships, 19 gritty events, **zero debug-output errors across ~14s of live frames** with the new `ScoutingCard`/`DevCard` nodes in the tree (proving every new `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` path resolves against the real save's data, incl. a real `Player_Potential` row for the live avatar).

The scouting card's actual on-screen *look* (bar proportions, grade-string legibility, tier-name copy) is verified by code + a clean headless boot only, not eyeballed ‚Äî same standing AdvanceDay-is-UI-button-only playtest gap as every prior UI entry. Per-pitch arsenal Velocity/Movement (¬ß5.4's stretch) was not attempted.

## 10d ‚Äî Bank / survival strip: SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Sonnet 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**The Burner Phone's Bank tab replaces its 10a placeholder with four `Card`-themed read-only sections (Funds, Gear, Needs, Side Work). Zero `Assets/Simulation/` touch, no schema change.**

- **Two design forks surfaced during research, both resolved with the user before writing code (not guessed):** (1) the three hustle overlays (`NarcoticsHustleScreen`/`FencingScreen`/`TexasHoldemTable`) only ever arm via `ScheduleScreen` ‚Üí confirm plan ‚Üí advance day ‚Üí `GameManager.OnHustleDayAdvanced`; there was no "open now" bypass to hook a launch button to. Resolved as **redirect-and-pre-fill**: the button never bypasses the day-plan gate, it only pre-selects the dropdown. (2) `EquipmentShopScreen` is already an always-visible corner overlay whenever an avatar exists ‚Äî it isn't "launched" by anything today, so a launch button has no analogue. Resolved as **summary-only, no button** ‚Äî converting it to toggle-visibility would have been a behavior change to a working screen, out of scope for adding a tab.
- **Funds card:** `LifeSim.TryGetFunds` (the in-memory mirror, `EquipmentShopScreen`'s own precedent for reading funds ‚Äî never `Players.TryGetById` directly) plus a computed "next bill in Nd" line. **No existing "days until next bill" accessor exists** ‚Äî `LifeSimManager.CostOfLivingCadenceDays`/`WeeklyCostOfLiving` (7 days / $70, a single bundled rent+food+gear line item, disclosed simplification from whenever they shipped) are public consts but the due-day math was inline-only inside `OnDayAdvanced`. The Bank tab computes it itself: `sinceBill = CurrentDay % CadenceDays; daysUntil = sinceBill == 0 ? CadenceDays : CadenceDays - sinceBill` ‚Äî matches the actual charge semantics (a bill lands ON the day `Day % 7 == 0`, so viewing state on that exact day correctly shows "7 days until the next one," not "0").
- **Gear card:** `GameManager.Gear.QualityFor` (the `EquipmentLedger` mirror) for the owned tier, `EquipmentService.PriceForQuality` for the next rung's sticker price. **No new DTO** ‚Äî `EquipmentShopState` and the tier-name array both already existed (this card's `TierNames` export is a verbatim copy of `EquipmentShopScreen`'s own array, same convention: tier copy lives on the scene, not in a shared class).
- **Needs card:** five default-themed `ProgressBar`s (green fill, 0‚Äì100 range matches `NeedsEngine.MaxNeed` exactly) bound directly to `LifeSim.TryGetNeeds`'s `NeedsState` struct ‚Äî no persistence-layer `NeedsQueries`/`Life_Needs` read, since that DTO is the write-path snapshot from last night, not the live current-hour value (same "read the live mirror, not the DB" discipline as Funds/Gear).
- **Side Work card:** three buttons emit a new `BurnerPhone.HustleLaunchRequestedEventHandler(int workActivity)` signal (Godot signals need Variant-friendly params, hence `int` not the `WorkActivity` enum directly). **`Main.cs` is the bridge**, not `BurnerPhone` or `ScheduleScreen` reaching into each other's tree ‚Äî `BurnerPhone` is nested three levels under `Main/ScreenContainer/TwoPanelShell/Panels`, `ScheduleScreen` is a direct `Main` sibling, so `Main` (already the common ancestor instantiating both) is the only node that can see both without a tree violation. `Main._Ready` now caches `_scheduleScreen` and, right after instantiating the shell, looks up `Panels/BurnerPhone` and subscribes ‚Äî the exact `newGameScreen.AvatarCreated += OnAvatarCreated` idiom already used one branch over. New `ScheduleScreen.SelectWorkActivity(WorkActivity)` just sets `_workActivityOption.Selected` ‚Äî no new `GameManager` surface, no bypass of the existing over-allocation/jail-lock confirm gate.
- All four cards are dirty-flag gated (`_bankInitialized` + per-section sentinel fields, a `NeedsEqual` struct comparison for the meters) ‚Äî no per-frame string formatting, the standing `ui_conventions.md` rule, same shape as `EquipmentShopScreen`'s `_shownFunds`/`_shownOwnedQuality`.

**Verification:** `dotnet build DirtAndDiamonds.sln` 0/0 all 8 projects. Node paths verified against the authored `BurnerPhone.tscn` tree before any `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` was written (`godot_scene_mapper`). `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` empty ‚Äî confirmed, not assumed; `run_monte_carlo_batch` inert by construction, no harness re-run needed (no harness compiles `Assets/UI`, same rationale as every prior UI-only entry). Live headless boot via the Godot MCP against the real dev save: schema v10 unchanged, day 48, avatar + 817 NPCs, 72 relationships, 19 gritty events, **zero debug-output errors across multiple live frames** with the new Bank tab and the `Main`‚Üî`ScheduleScreen` signal bridge both in the tree.

Pressing a hustle button was not exercised end-to-end in a live playtest (confirming the dropdown actually lands on the right index, then completing a day into a real hustle session) ‚Äî folds into the standing manual-playtest list below.

## 10e ‚Äî Portrait pipeline: SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Sonnet 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**The last item on Phase 10's ¬ß7 sub-plan. Avatar and contact portraits are wired into the shell; zero `Assets/Simulation/` touch, no schema change, no art assets authored ‚Äî every identity renders the deterministic procedural fallback today, exactly as ¬ß6's asset-budget disclosure anticipates.**

- **New `Assets/UI/Portraits/`, split on the same Godot-purity line as `Assets/UI/Scouting/ScoutingGrade.cs`:** `PortraitTile.cs` (pure, Godot-free ‚Äî the fallback math) + `PortraitLibrary.cs` (Godot `ResourceLoader`/`Texture2D` lazy-load + cache) + `PortraitView.cs`/`.tscn` (a reusable `PanelContainer` Control, the one place both paths meet). **`PortraitLibrary.TryLoad(key)`** checks `res://Assets/UI/Portraits/Art/{key}.png` via `ResourceLoader.Exists`, caches the hit-or-miss per key so a given identity is ever probed once per process ‚Äî satisfies ¬ß6's "loading discipline: object-pool/lazy-load pattern, never instantiated per-frame." The `Art/` folder is empty ‚Äî no assets exist yet ‚Äî so every lookup misses today; the pipeline is real, the art drop is a future, code-free task (just add `.png` files keyed by player_id/portrait_key).
- **The fallback ‚Äî ¬ß6's "themed initials-on-color tile ... seeded off player_id" ‚Äî is `PortraitTile`:** an 8-slot palette index from a custom **FNV-1a-32 hash** (offset basis `2166136261`, prime `16777619`) over the key's UTF-8 bytes, plus a 1‚Äì2 letter `Initials()` extraction off the display name. **Deliberately not `string.GetHashCode()`** ‚Äî .NET randomizes that per process for hash-flood protection, which would make "the same NPC always draws the same fallback" false across two boots of the same save. `PortraitView.SetIdentity(key, displayName)` is a no-op unless `key` changed since the last call (the dirty-flag/lazy-load discipline), and renders either the loaded `TextureRect` or, on a miss, hides it and paints an ink-on-palette `StyleBoxFlat` + initials `Label` instead ‚Äî "zero asset cost" per the doc, no procedural texture baking needed.
- **Wiring ‚Äî scoped to exactly ¬ß7's ask ("wire avatar + contact portraits into the phone/dashboard"):** `BaseballDashboard.tscn`'s `CalendarStrip` gained an `AvatarPortrait` `PortraitView` instance, fed `SetIdentity(avatarId, "{FirstName} {LastName}")` inside the existing `RefreshScoutingCard()` dirty-flag refresh (same-day-advance-granularity as every other scouting field, per `ui_conventions.md` ‚Äî no new per-frame call). `BurnerPhone.tscn`'s `ThreadHeaderLabel` was wrapped in a new `ThreadHeaderRow` alongside a `ThreadPortrait` instance, fed `SetIdentity(contact.PortraitKey, contact.DisplayName)` inside `RenderThread` ‚Äî keyed on `PortraitKey` (the design's authored art key, defaulting to `contactId` when omitted per 10b), not the raw contact id, so a future re-keyed asset doesn't need a code change. **Heirs are covered for free:** a succession handoff just repoints `CareerManager.AvatarPlayerId`, and `RefreshScoutingCard` already re-reads it every refresh ‚Äî the new avatar's own key (real art if ever authored, else its own distinct fallback tile) shows up with zero extra wiring, satisfying ¬ß6's "avatar, heirs" budget line without a heir-specific code path.
- **Disclosed scope calls (not gaps ‚Äî the doc's own wiring ask stops here):** the Messages tab's `ItemList` contact rows stay text-only, no per-row portrait swatch ‚Äî `ItemList` icons need a baked `Texture2D` per row, which the header portrait already renders once per open thread without that extra complexity. `SuccessionScreen`/`BirthNotificationScreen` were not touched ‚Äî ¬ß7 named "phone/dashboard" specifically, and neither of those screens was in scope.
- **Determinism harness, same discipline as `ScoutingGrade`:** `Tools/MonteCarloHarness/MonteCarloHarness.csproj` gained a `Assets/UI/Portraits/*.cs` compile glob **excluding** `PortraitLibrary.cs`/`PortraitView.cs` (the two Godot-facing files) ‚Äî mirrors the project's own `GameManager.cs` exclusion precedent. New `RunPortraitTileSuite()`: the FNV-1a palette index pinned exact (not just range-checked) for 6 known ids ‚Äî independently hand-computed, e.g. `"unknown"‚Üí1`, `"agent_diaz"‚Üí7`, `"avatar-player-guid-0001"‚Üí0` ‚Äî plus the empty-string edge case and a repeatability check; `Initials()` pinned across two-word ("Coach Reyes"‚Üí"CR"), a parenthetical third word ignored ("Alex Diaz (Agent)"‚Üí"AD"), single-word ("Jess"‚Üí"JE"), single-character ("A"‚Üí"A"), and empty/whitespace (‚Üí"?") cases.
- **Steam disclosure carry-forward (the other half of this step, per ¬ß7's table row):** ¬ß6 already records "the pre-generated AI portraits are a Steam content disclosure item ... so Phase 11's store-copy/questionnaire step inherits it. No action this phase beyond the note." Recording it here again, explicitly, so a future session loading only `progress.md` (not the design doc) still inherits it: **when Phase 11 authors real portrait art with an AI image generator, that art is a disclosed AI-generated content item for Steam's storefront questionnaire.** No code or doc action beyond this note is owed by 10e.

**Verification:** `dotnet build DirtAndDiamonds.sln` 0/0 all 8 projects. **`MonteCarloHarness` 258‚Üí266/266** (+8 portrait fixtures) ‚Äî **no band moved**, the standing 80-offseason equilibrium re-confirmed byte-for-byte (HS 124.3 < College 145.1 < MinorA 147.1 < MinorAA 150.2 < MinorAAA 155.4 < MLB 166.0). `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` **empty** ‚Äî confirmed, not assumed. Live headless boot via the Godot MCP against the real dev save: schema v10 unchanged, day 48, avatar + 817 NPCs, 72 relationships, 19 gritty events, **zero debug-output errors across ~22s of live frames** with both `AvatarPortrait` (dashboard) and `ThreadPortrait` (phone) in the tree ‚Äî the avatar branch genuinely executed (a real avatar exists in this save), confirming both new `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` paths resolve against live data, not just a no-avatar boot.

**Disclosed:** no portrait art has been authored ‚Äî every identity in the live game renders the procedural fallback today; that is the expected, correct state per ¬ß6's budget (art is a future, code-free asset drop), not a shortfall of this step. The tile's actual on-screen look (color contrast against the ink initials, corner radius, centering) is verified by code + a clean headless boot only, not eyeballed ‚Äî same standing `AdvanceDay`-is-UI-button-only playtest gap as every prior UI entry.

**This closes Phase 10's ¬ß7 sub-plan (10a‚Äì10e) end to end**, modulo the standing manual playtest and the one still-open design ruling (below).

## 10c OFP-scale ruling: CLOSED (2026-07-06, Fable 5 ‚Äî halving UPHELD as permanent)

**The disclosed 10c finding is ruled: Sonnet's `/2` in `ScoutingGrade.OfpRating` is the correct permanent recentering. `PromotionScore.Scouting`'s `/150` divisor must NOT be re-derived. The defect was in the design doc, which misstated `Scouting` as "returns a 0‚Äì100 overall"; the doc is now corrected.**

- **Why the divisor stands:** `Scouting`'s 100-centring is load-bearing, not accidental. `Combine(P, S) = wP¬∑P + wS¬∑S` mixes it against `BatterPerformance`/`PitcherPerformance`, which are explicitly 100-centred by construction (`100.0 * (1.0 + w¬∑(rawP ‚àí 1.0))`); the weights only mean their stated ratio if both operands share that scale. Re-deriving `/150` ‚Üí `/300` would silently halve the effective `ScoutingWeight`, re-ordering every promotion pool ‚Äî **a band move in closed 9c** (conservation-law harness + pinned fixtures) and a violation of Phase 10's no-`Simulation/`-touch construction guarantee. Compensating by doubling `ScoutingWeight` would churn a closed, fixture-pinned system for zero behavioral change while *creating* the scale mismatch inside `Combine` it purported to fix.
- **Why the halving is exact, not a fudge:** at peak age with zero headroom, `Scouting = 100¬∑sum/150 = 2 √ó role-average rating`, so `Scouting/2 = roleAvg + ProjectionBonus/3` ‚Äî precisely the 0‚Äì100/50-average `PlayerRatingsRow` scale `Grade`'s bands are calibrated to (150‚Üí50‚ÜíC+, 120‚Üí40‚ÜíC, both fixture-pinned), with `ProjectionBonus` correctly converted from role-sum units to per-rating units by the same factor.
- **Why `Grade`'s domain can't absorb it instead:** the bands also grade raw per-tool ratings (`Grade(current_i)`/`Grade(potential_i)` present/future), which are natively 0‚Äì100/50-average. OFP is the *only* consumer whose input arrives in Combine-units; unit conversion at that one boundary consumer is the right altitude.
- **Recorded in four places:** `ScoutingGrade.OfpRating`'s doc comment (flag ‚Üí ruling), the harness suite comment in `Tools/MonteCarloHarness/Program.cs`, the design doc (`¬ß5.1`'s scale claim corrected, `¬ß5.3`'s formula now `Grade(round(Scouting(...)/2))` with the ruling inline, acceptance check 4 updated), and this entry. No executable code changed ‚Äî comments/docs only.

**Verification:** `dotnet build` + `MonteCarloHarness` re-run green at the standing 266/266 (comment-only edits; no band moved, equilibrium byte-identical).

## Phase 11 ‚Äî Steam & Publishing ("Ship It"): DESIGN DOC done (2026-07-06, Opus 4.8, design only ‚Äî NO code)

**`docs/design/steam_publishing_ship_it.md`.** Turns BUILD_PLAN ¬ß11 (cloud saves, achievements‚Üídispatcher, rich presence, native-lib export, content compliance) into a full platform/packaging spec for **Fable 5** (who owns the whole implementation per CLAUDE.md's Steamworks directive). Grounded against the live composition root (`GameManager._Ready`/`_Process`/`_ExitTree`), `DatabaseManager` (WAL + the deliberate `Pooling = false` handle-release), the event bus/`CoreEvents`, `CareerManager`, and `GameStateQueries` ‚Äî plus the two **empty stub files** `Assets/Platform/Steam/{SteamIntegration,AchievementManager}.cs` Phase 0 reserved. Opus owns the two hard-to-reverse cores (¬ß4 achievement seam, ¬ß5 cloud-save WAL correctness); the rest is a precise Fable spec. Load-bearing decisions:

- **No schema change (user_version stays 10), no `Simulation/`/UI-logic touch** ‚Äî so `run_monte_carlo_batch` is inert by construction exactly like Phase 10 (asserted via `git show --stat`, target 266/266). The *only* Data-layer touch in the whole phase is one additive, engine-independent `DatabaseManager.CheckpointForSync()` method (¬ß5.3) ‚Äî changes no schema, no query, no-op when the WAL is empty.
- **The load-bearing robustness rule (the phase's Phase-10-"read-only"-analog): Steam is optional at runtime.** Every Steam call no-ops when the SDK failed to init (`SteamIntegration.IsAvailable`), so the game boots fully and all 8 harnesses stay green with **no Steam client present** ‚Äî which is the *normal* dev/headless/MCP state, not an error path. A build that throws because Steam isn't running is a review-blocking defect. `SteamIntegration` is the sole owner of the Facepunch `SteamClient` lifecycle (Init before the DB open; `RunCallbacks` next to the existing `Events.DispatchPending()` per-frame pump; `Shutdown` last in `_ExitTree`); it's also the only file that touches `Steamworks.*`. All Steam wiring lands in `GameManager` (Godot, outside every harness compile set) + `Assets/Platform/Steam/` (globbed by no harness), so harness inertness is structural.
- **Achievements = another bus consumer (¬ß4, Opus core).** `AchievementManager` is structurally identical to `RivalryLedger`/`AvailabilityLedger`/`EquipmentLedger` ‚Äî a pure `EventBus.Subscribe` reader whose side effect is `TrySetAchievement("ID")` instead of an in-memory cache. **Mapping discipline (normative):** every achievement traces to a signal the game *already* emits ‚Äî never a new tracking write. Decisive grounding finding: promotion routes `ReactivateAvatar` ‚Üí `ActivateAvatar` ‚Üí **publishes `AvatarChangedEvent` with the new team** (CareerManager.cs:607/873), so "reached the majors" is derivable via `Baseball.TryGetTeamTier(TeamId)==MLB` off the bus with zero new state. Starter roster (¬ß4.2) maps Went Pro/The Show (`AvatarChangedEvent`), Next of Kin (`ChildBornEvent`), Dynasty (`DynastyGeneration==3` ‚Äî the game's own 3-gen exit criterion), End of the Line (`LineageOverReason`), Rap Sheet (`PlayerAbsenceChangedEvent` reason 3), Moonlighting/Juiced (`GrittyEventResolvedEvent` by id), Journeyman (`SeasonRolledOverEvent` count via a server-side **Steam Stat**). **Steam is the durable store for unlock state ‚Üí the game persists nothing ‚Üí that's *why* there's no schema change.** `SetAchievement` is idempotent, so milestone conditions re-assert harmlessly on reload. Two deferred as stretch (Hold'em win + peak-A+ rating ‚Äî need an additive signal not on the bus today).
- **Cloud save = the WAL correctness problem (¬ß5, Opus core ‚Äî the one place a naive impl ships corruption).** The save is WAL-mode (mandatory for the gritty-event poller), so the `.db` alone is missing every un-checkpointed write and the `-wal`/`-shm` sidecars can't be carried cross-machine. Decision: `CheckpointForSync()` runs `PRAGMA wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE)` in `_ExitTree` *before* `_database.Dispose()`, leaving `dirt_and_diamonds.db` a complete self-contained snapshot; **Steam Auto-Cloud** (partner-site path pattern = `.db` only, not sidecars) syncs it with no `ISteamRemoteStorage` API code. `DatabaseManager` was *already designed for this* ‚Äî its `Pooling = false` comment literally says it releases the handle so "cloud sync never fights a lock." Boot path unchanged (Steam pre-places the newest `.db` at the `user://` path before launch). Disclosed limits: no in-game conflict UI (last-clean-exit-wins via Steam), crash-before-checkpoint recovers locally, checkpoint verified through the `--headless --quit` boot (which runs `_ExitTree`; MCP `stop_project` force-kills and doesn't).
- **Native/export (¬ß3, Fable):** Facepunch NuGet + `steam_api64.dll`/`libsteam_api.so` copy-to-output (the exact `validate_steamworks_native` gate); `NativeLibrary.SetDllImportResolver` (registered once in Init; `using System.Runtime.InteropServices;` already imported at GameManager.cs:1; `EnableDynamicLoading` already true). **First `export_presets.cfg` for the project** (none exists yet) ‚Äî Windows + Linux, and it MUST add `SchemaDefinitions.sql` + `Assets/Narrative/**/*.json` to the include filters or the exported `.pck` boots with no schema / no events (the exact hazard GameManager.cs:29-36's own NOTE comments flag). `steam_appid.txt` is a git-ignored dev-only artifact.
- **Content compliance (¬ß7, Fable):** the Phase-10e AI-portrait disclosure gets filed here (the one artifact 10e pre-generated for Phase 11); mature-content questionnaire for drug-dealing (Narcotics, 8b) + gambling (Hold'em, 8d).
- **¬ß8 sub-plan (one session each, all Fable):** 11a native+lifecycle+degradation (load-bearing, lands first) ‚Üí 11b achievements ‚Üí 11c cloud save ‚Üí 11d rich presence ‚Üí 11e export+compliance. ¬ß9 acceptance: the no-Steam boot IS the degradation proof (default in MCP); harness inertness asserted (no Facepunch in any `Tools/*.csproj`); `validate_steamworks_native` green; user_version stays 10; + manual Steam-client smoke tests for cloud round-trip and one achievement toast (idempotent re-assert on reload); Windows+Linux export builds launch.

## 11a ‚Äî Native + Steam lifecycle + graceful degradation: SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Fable 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**`Assets/Platform/Steam/SteamIntegration.cs` fills its Phase-0 stub as the sole Steam SDK owner; `GameManager` drives it at its three lifecycle seams; the load-bearing `IsAvailable` no-op contract is live and proven by the no-Steam headless boot.** `AchievementManager.cs` stays an empty stub (11b's deliverable).

- **The ¬ß10 open question is resolved ‚Äî and the answer overrode the doc's `&lt;PackageReference&gt;` line via its own escape hatch ("whichever Facepunch's distribution provides").** NuGet.org stalled at 2.3.3 (Feb 2020) and is **Win64-only**; even Facepunch's own current 2.5.2 nupkg declares itself "For Windows x64" (and its `content/steam_api64.dll` wouldn't flow to a PackageReference project anyway). The Posix managed build has *never* been packaged ‚Äî it ships only as a raw DLL in the GitHub release zip. So: **vendored Facepunch.Steamworks 2.5.2** (`Release/net6.0/`, MIT, release commit `5a22fa2`) committed under `Assets/Platform/Steam/lib/` (Win64 + Posix DLLs + IntelliSense XMLs, README with provenance/upgrade path, `.gdignore` so the importer never scans the binaries), consumed via **RID-conditional `&lt;Reference&gt;`** items: a `linux-x64` publish (the Godot Linux/Steam Deck export) ‚Üí Posix, everything else (editor/dev/win-x64) ‚Üí Win64. One version across both platforms, six years and one SDK era newer than the NuGet package.
- **Natives keep the standing Phase-0 `.gitignore` posture** ("copied at build time, not committed"): `steam_api64.dll` + `libsteam_api.so` are git-ignored drops in `Assets/Platform/Steam/native/` (sourced from the same release zip's `redistributable_bin`), copied to the output root by **`Exists`-guarded `<None ... CopyToOutputDirectory="PreserveNewest">`** items ‚Äî the exact shape `validate_steamworks_native` checks ‚Äî so a fresh clone with no drop still builds 0/0 and simply boots degraded. P/Invoke names verified against the shipped binaries, not assumed: the Win64 build imports `steam_api64`, Posix imports `libsteam_api`; the once-registered `NativeLibrary.SetDllImportResolver` maps both to the platform file beside the managed assemblies / the executable, returning Zero to default probing otherwise.
- **`SteamIntegration` (¬ß2.1/¬ß2.2 exactly):** `SteamClient.Init(480, asyncCallbacks: false)` ‚Äî Spacewar dev appid until 11e mints the real one; Facepunch exports the appid into the process environment, so dev against a live client needs no `steam_appid.txt`; callbacks pump manually once per frame. Wrappers `RunCallbacks` / `TrySetAchievement` (idempotent per ¬ß4.3, via `Achievement.Trigger`) / `SetRichPresence` / `Shutdown` all bare-guard on `IsAvailable` ‚Äî 11b/11d subscribers will run identically with Steam up or down (no divergent path to rot). Failure logs the doc's exact one-liner.
- **GameManager seams (¬ß2.1 table):** Init at the very top of `_Ready`, *before* the DB open (¬ß5.4 boot order ‚Äî Auto-Cloud pre-places the freshest `.db`, and `IsAvailable` is known before 11b's subscriber wires); `Steam.RunCallbacks()` beside `Events.DispatchPending()` in `_Process`; `Steam?.Shutdown()` **last** in `_ExitTree`, after `_database?.Dispose()` releases the handle (11c inserts the WAL checkpoint just ahead of that dispose). Public `GameManager.Steam` property in house style so no other class ever touches `Steamworks.*`.

**Verification:** build 0/0 (all 8 projects); all seven harnesses green at standing tallies ‚Äî SchemaValidator 70/70, CoreLoop 22/22, NeedsDecay 69/69, Hustle 31/31, Holdem 63/63, GrittyEvents 82/82, **MonteCarlo 266/266, no band moved** (inert by construction: `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` empty); zero Steam artifacts in any `Tools/*/bin` output and no Facepunch/Platform reference in any harness `.csproj` (¬ß9.2 asserted at source and artifact level); `validate_steamworks_native` **green** (both `&lt;None&gt;` items + both natives confirmed at the build output root); **the ¬ß9.1 degradation proof:** headless `--headless --quit` boot with no Steam process ‚Üí exactly one `[Steam] not available ‚Äî achievements/cloud disabled this session (SteamApi_Init failed with FailedGeneric - error: Could not determine Steam client install directory.)` line, then the normal clean boot (schema **v10** unchanged, journal=wal, fk=on, day 48, dispatcher polling). The error text itself proves the native **loaded and executed** ‚Äî resolver + copy targets work end-to-end and only the no-client stage failed ‚Äî so one boot evidences both ¬ß3's plumbing and ¬ß2's degradation. Live-client Init / achievement-toast smoke tests stay user-driven per ¬ß9.5/¬ß9.6.

## 11b ‚Äî Achievements as a bus consumer: SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Fable 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**`Assets/Platform/Steam/AchievementManager.cs` fills its Phase-0 stub as the ¬ß4 platform read-model over the event stream ‚Äî structurally another ledger (cached-delegate `AttachTo`/`DetachFrom`, the `AvailabilityLedger` house pattern), holding no sim authority and writing nothing to the database; its only side effect is a guarded `SteamIntegration` call. The full ¬ß4.2 starter roster is mapped; `PRAGMA user_version` stays 10 because Steam owns unlock state (¬ß4.3), not despite it.**

- **The eight unlocks + the counter, each traced to an already-emitted signal (the ¬ß4.2 normative rule ‚Äî zero new tracking writes):** *Went Pro* / *The Show* off `AvatarChangedEvent` via `Baseball.TryGetTeamTier` (‚â• `MinorA` / == `MLB` ‚Äî creation, succession, and the 9c promotion republish all land on the same channel); *Next of Kin* off `ChildBornEvent` (inherently avatar-scoped ‚Äî conception is bus-requested for the avatar only); *Dynasty* (`DynastyGeneration ‚â• 3`, the game's own exit criterion) + *End of the Line* (`LineageOverReason` present) re-evaluated from Game_State; *Rap Sheet* off `PlayerAbsenceChangedEvent` where `Reason == (byte)AbsenceReason.Arrest` and subject == avatar; *Moonlighting* / *Juiced* off `GrittyEventResolvedEvent` by content-id family; *Journeyman* as a `TryAddStat("STAT_SEASONS_PLAYED", 1)` **Steam Stat** on `SeasonRolledOverEvent` (server-side running total; the stat-vs-threshold rule lives on the partner site). Achievement API names (`ACH_WENT_PRO`, ‚Ä¶) are consts that 11e must mint verbatim on the partner site ‚Äî against the 11a dev appid (Spacewar) they don't exist, so live-client unlocks fail server-side silently, the expected dev state.
- **Two ordering facts make the milestone reads race-free, verified in source, not assumed:** (1) `CareerManager.Succeed` commits the `DynastyGeneration` bump **inside its batch, before** `ActivateAvatar` publishes `AvatarChangedEvent` (CareerManager.cs:826-840), so the generation read off that event is never stale ‚Äî including the interactive heir-choice path (`ResolvePendingSuccession`), which resolves outside any rollover; (2) game-over writes `LineageOverReason` immediately on **both** autopilot and interactive paths (`PersistGameOver` ‚Äî "there's no choice to make on a game-over"), inside Career's own `SeasonRolledOverEvent` handling ‚Äî and since per-channel handlers run in subscription order and `AchievementManager` attaches **last** in `_Ready`, its rollover read always observes that same rollover's succession/game-over writes within the same dispatch.
- **Subject discipline:** gritty events, absences, and season ticks fire for NPCs / an avatar-less world too, so every subject-carrying handler filters on the live avatar id ‚Äî tracked in-memory off `AvatarChangedEvent` plus a boot-time `SyncFromBoot(avatarId, teamId)` (the `SyncLifeSimAvatar` precedent: `LoadExistingAvatar` activates before the bus attaches and publishes nothing). `SyncFromBoot` also re-asserts the tier + Game_State milestones ‚Äî exactly ¬ß4.3's reload case, and it closes the gap for saves that earned a milestone before 11b existed or while Steam was down. *Journeyman* only ticks while an avatar exists (a pre-creation or post-game-over world ticking over is not a season "played").
- **The content-id families (finalized per ¬ß4.2's "Fable finalizes the exact ids"):** *Juiced* = the detection_risk arc ‚Äî `caught_juicing` + the three league-test suspensions (`suspended_ped_test_flag`/`suspended_repeat_violation`/`suspended_lifetime_watch`). *Moonlighting* = the underworld arc ‚Äî `back_alley_bribe`, `syndicate_shakedown`, `syndicate_enforcers`, `narcotics_arrest`. **One deliberate refinement:** walking away from the bribe must not moonlight, and `back_alley_bribe` is the only underworld event reachable *without* prior engagement (the other three key on `compromised_syndicate`/`syndicate_marked`/the hustle-written `narc_watchlist`) ‚Äî so that one event resolves its choice **id** (`take_the_envelope`) back through `GrittyEventLibrary`, never trusting the raw `ChoiceIndex` (authoring order, not contract). Disclosed coupling: these id sets mirror the shipped content batches, and `check_event_graph_integrity` doesn't know about the mapping ‚Äî a renamed content id must be renamed here too (noted in the source comment).
- **`SteamIntegration` gained the one missing wrapper, `TryAddStat`** (`SteamUserStats.AddStat` + `StoreStats` ‚Äî verified against the vendored 2.5.2 XML docs: `AddStat` only stages locally, unlike `SetStat` which auto-stores; `StoreStats`' minutes-order rate limit is far above the once-per-season caller cadence). Same bare `IsAvailable` guard as every other wrapper; `AchievementManager` itself never references `Steamworks.*` (¬ß2.1 held).
- **GameManager wiring:** private `_achievements` field (the `_rivalryLedger` precedent ‚Äî nothing reads it), constructed + attached at the very end of `_Ready` after every publisher, `SyncFromBoot` guarded on `avatarLoaded`. Subscriptions run whether Steam is up or not (¬ß2.2 ‚Äî no divergent path to rot).

**Verification:** build 0/0 (all 8 projects). All seven harnesses green at standing tallies ‚Äî SchemaValidator 70/70, CoreLoop 22/22, NeedsDecay 69/69, Hustle 31/31, GrittyEvents 82/82, Holdem 63/63, **MonteCarlo 266/266, no band moved** (inert by construction: the 11b diff is exactly `GameManager.cs` + the two `Assets/Platform/Steam/` files; `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation Assets/UI` empty, no `Tools/*.csproj` references `Assets/Platform` ‚Äî asserted, not assumed, per ¬ß9.2). **No schema change asserted:** the headless `--headless --quit` boot against the real dev save reports schema **v10** unchanged (journal=wal, fk=on, day 48) with the avatar loaded ‚Äî so `SyncFromBoot` + all five subscriptions + one full pump + `_ExitTree` genuinely executed with Steam down, one `[Steam] not available` line, zero exceptions (the ¬ß9.1 degradation proof re-run with the 11b wiring live). The ¬ß9.6 achievement-toast smoke test (real Steam client, real appid) stays user-driven at 11e ‚Äî no headless path exercises a Steam backend.

**Disclosed:** the two stretch achievements (Hold'em win, peak-A+ rating) stay deferred per ¬ß4.2 ‚Äî each needs a small additive bus signal that doesn't exist today; content decision, not platform. The *Moonlighting*/*Juiced* families are code-side consts, not content-side tags ‚Äî fine at 8 events, worth revisiting (a JSON `achievement` tag) only if the roster grows.

## 11c ‚Äî Cloud saves (the WAL-correctness deliverable): SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Fable 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**The ¬ß5 marquee decision lands: `DatabaseManager.CheckpointForSync()` folds the WAL into the single `.db` on clean exit, so the one file Steam Auto-Cloud uploads is the complete save. No schema change (`user_version` stays 10), no query change, no `Simulation/`/UI touch ‚Äî the checkpoint is a bare pragma, exactly as designed.**

- **`DatabaseManager.CheckpointForSync()` (¬ß5.3):** runs `PRAGMA wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE)` under the connection lock; throws on an active batch (the `ApplySchema`/`BeginBatch` design-error precedent ‚Äî a checkpoint inside a calendar tick is a bug, not a race to paper over); a no-op when the WAL is already empty. **One disclosed deviation from the doc's `void` sketch: it returns `bool`** ‚Äî the pragma's `busy` flag surfaces (0 = every frame folded + sidecar truncated), so the caller can *say* when the cloud snapshot would be incomplete instead of silently shipping it. DatabaseManager stays engine-independent; harnesses that construct their own manager never call it (additive, harmless).
- **`GameManager._ExitTree` insertion (¬ß2.1 table, third row):** after the Life/Relationship exit-flushes commit and after the gritty-event poll view ‚Äî the only other reader, whose open read txn could otherwise hold the truncate to `busy` ‚Äî has closed, just ahead of `_database.Dispose()`. An incomplete checkpoint logs one `[GameManager]` line and proceeds (the save stays consistent locally via WAL replay; only the cloud copy trails ‚Äî ¬ß5.5's disclosed posture). `Steam?.Shutdown()` stays last, and 11a's "11c inserts here" comment breadcrumb is retired.
- **Auto-Cloud path config recorded** in `Assets/Platform/Steam/README.md` for 11e to enter verbatim (the partner site can't be configured against the Spacewar dev appid): per-OS roots `WinAppDataRoaming` / `LinuxXdgDataHome`, subdirectories off `config/name="Dirt & Diamonds"`, **file mask = the exact literal filename `dirt_and_diamonds.db`**, 200 MB / 2-file quota. **The ¬ß10 open question is RESOLVED** (recorded in the design doc): Auto-Cloud masks take exact literal names, so the `-wal`/`-shm` sidecars are excluded by construction ‚Äî and the checkpoint leaves the `-wal` empty anyway, belt and braces.
- **Boot-order confirmation (¬ß5.4):** already held from 11a ‚Äî `Steam.Initialize()` runs before `new DatabaseManager(...)`, so Auto-Cloud's pre-launch download lands before the open; asserted, zero code change.

**Verification:** build 0/0 (all 8 projects); all seven harnesses green at standing tallies ‚Äî SchemaValidator 70/70, CoreLoop 22/22, NeedsDecay 69/69, Hustle 31/31, Holdem 63/63, GrittyEvents 82/82, **MonteCarlo 266/266, no band moved** (inert by construction: `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation Assets/UI Tools` empty; the 11c diff is exactly `DatabaseManager.cs` + `GameManager.cs` + the Steam README + the design-doc resolution note). **The ¬ß5.3 exit proof, on the real dev save:** headless `--headless --quit` boot clean (schema **v10**, journal=wal, fk=on, day 48, avatar + 817 NPCs, one `[Steam] not available` line, zero exceptions) with **no** "WAL checkpoint incomplete" warning ‚Äî and after exit the save directory holds **only `dirt_and_diamonds.db`** (no `-wal`, no `-shm`), its LastWriteTime stamped by the exit flush: the single file is the whole save. (Pre-exit the WAL held that boot's exit-flush frames ‚Äî ~817 Life_Needs rows ‚Äî so the checkpoint provably had real work to fold, not a vacuous pass.)

**Disclosed:** the ¬ß9.5 cloud round-trip smoke test (real Steam client, real appid, actual upload/download) stays user-driven at 11e with the partner-site entry; the godot-MCP `stop_project` force-kill path never runs `_ExitTree` and therefore never checkpoints ‚Äî ¬ß5.5's standard, disclosed crash-shaped behavior (local WAL replay recovers on next open).

## 11d ‚Äî Rich presence: SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Fable 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**New `Assets/Platform/Steam/RichPresenceWriter.cs` is the ¬ß6 presence writer ‚Äî the fourth ledger-shaped bus consumer (cached-delegate `AttachTo`/`DetachFrom`, subject tracked off `AvatarChangedEvent` + boot sync), whose only side effect is the guarded `SteamIntegration.SetRichPresence`. ¬ß6's "inside `SteamIntegration` or the `AchievementManager`, implementer's call" resolved to a separate class: 11a's `GameManager.Steam` doc comment had already reserved "11d's presence writer" as its own routing consumer, and folding presence into a class named `AchievementManager` would make the name lie.**

- **No display wording in C# (the Phase-10 localization posture, ¬ß1):** the game sets only stable tokens and raw values ‚Äî `steam_display` = `#Status_Career` / `#Status_BetweenCareers`, plus substitution keys `season` (invariant digits off `GlobalState.SeasonYear` ‚Äî a calendar-style year, e.g. 2026), `tier`, `player` (first + last from the avatar's row), `age`. The `tier` value is itself a sub-token (`#Tier_HS` ‚Ä¶ `#Tier_MLB`, pinned as consts so an enum rename can never silently change the wire contract ‚Äî Steam localizes values starting with `#`), so tier names localize on the partner site too. Full token table + suggested English set recorded in `Assets/Platform/Steam/README.md` for 11e to mint verbatim (the ACH_*/Auto-Cloud precedent); the English tier names mirror `BaseballDashboard.TierNamesCsv` so friends list and scouting card agree. Against Spacewar nothing renders ‚Äî expected until the real appid.
- **Update cadence is exactly ¬ß6's, event-driven only, never per-frame:** `AvatarChangedEvent` (creation, succession, the 9c promotion republish ‚Äî name/tier changes), `SeasonRolledOverEvent` (year tick; the avatar row is re-read because CareerManager's earlier-attached handler has already run the yearly aging tick, so the age refreshes too), plus the boot sync. Attach order (last in `_Ready`, after every publisher) makes the rollover reads observe that same rollover's succession/game-over writes ‚Äî the 11b ordering argument, reused.
- **The between-careers state covers all three no-career shapes:** an avatar-less boot (`SetBetweenCareers` from GameManager's `else` branch), a game-over rollover (`LineageOverReason` read flips presence live, then null subject ignores further ticks), and ‚Äî one nuance beyond the doc ‚Äî a **boot on a lineage-over save**: game-over parks the retiree with `avatar_player_id` still set (Phase 6: "avatar stays rostered, sim keeps running"), so `avatarLoaded` is true but the career isn't live; `SyncFromBoot` checks `LineageOverReason` first and publishes between-careers, not the parked retiree's career.
- **GameManager wiring:** private `_presence` field (the `_achievements` posture), constructed + attached beside it at the end of `_Ready`, `SyncFromBoot`/`SetBetweenCareers` split on `avatarLoaded`. Subscriptions run whether Steam is up or not (¬ß2.2). Presence reads DB/state only through the existing `BaseballQueries`/`PlayerQueries`/`GameStateQueries` surfaces + the `GlobalState` mirror ‚Äî no new query, no writes, rare events, so nothing hot.

**Verification:** build 0/0 (all 8 projects); all seven harnesses green at standing tallies ‚Äî SchemaValidator 70/70, CoreLoop 22/22, NeedsDecay 69/69, Hustle 31/31, Holdem 63/63, GrittyEvents 82/82, **MonteCarlo 266/266, no band moved** (inert by construction: `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation Assets/UI Tools` empty; the 11d diff is exactly the new `RichPresenceWriter.cs` + its `.uid` + `GameManager.cs` wiring + the Steam README section + this entry; no `Tools/*.csproj` references `Assets/Platform` or Facepunch ‚Äî re-asserted). **The ¬ß9.1 degradation proof re-run with 11d live:** headless `--headless --quit` boot against the real dev save, one `[Steam] not available` line, schema **v10** unchanged (journal=wal, fk=on, day 48, avatar + 817 NPCs), zero exceptions ‚Äî the boot has an avatar with lineage alive, so `SyncFromBoot` exercised the full career-presence path (tier + row reads, four guarded no-op presence calls) with Steam down. `.cs.uid` sidecar generated via the headless `--import` pass (the plain `--quit` boot doesn't scan).

**Disclosed:** the ¬ß6 example's position tag ("22 y/o **1B**") has no data source ‚Äî Players has no position column (is_pitcher/role live in ratings tables) ‚Äî so the substitution set is season/tier/player/age; 11e words the token around what exists. Rendering, and the real `steam_display` behavior, are only observable with the real appid at 11e (rich presence has no Spacewar-visible surface, unlike achievements' silent server-side failure). If a friends-list "view game info" legacy `status` key is wanted, that's an 11e wording decision on the partner site side of the wall, not new code.

## 11e ‚Äî Export + compliance: SHIPPED (2026-07-06, Fable 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî closes Phase 11 / Milestone M7 "Ship It")

**The project's first `export_presets.cfg` (Windows Desktop + Linux, ¬ß3.3), both release depots produced and byte-verified, the Windows depot launch-proven against the real save, `validate_steamworks_native` green at both the `.csproj` and real-publish level, and the ¬ß7 compliance items (AI-portrait disclosure, mature-content questionnaire, `ACH_*`/`STAT_*` minting) recorded verbatim in `Assets/Platform/Steam/README.md` ‚Äî the partner-site entry is now a transcription job. No game C# changed this step (only `.csproj` copy conditions), so the sims/UI are inert by construction.**

- **Toolchain first:** the 4.7 mono export templates weren't installed (no export had ever run) ‚Äî pulled the official `Godot_v4.7-stable_mono_export_templates.tpz` (1.12 GiB, GitHub release, matches the binary's `4.7.stable.mono.official.5b4e0cb0f`), installed only `version.txt` + the x86_64 Windows/Linux templates into `%APPDATA%\Godot\export_templates\4.7.stable.mono\` (a dev-machine artifact, not repo state). Platform names for 4.7: `"Windows Desktop"` and `"Linux"` (the 4.3+ rename; accepted first try).
- **`export_presets.cfg` is deliberately COMMITTED ‚Äî a `.gitignore` fix rode along:** the Phase-0 ignore list had `export_presets.cfg` (a Godot-3-era habit); in Godot 4 the secrets live in `export_credentials.cfg` (still ignored) and the presets carry load-bearing config, so the ignore line came out and `Build/` (the preset output paths) went in. Include filters are the ¬ß3.3 contract, path-scoped (`*Assets/Data/Database/SchemaDefinitions.sql, *Assets/Narrative/*.json`) because a bare `*.json` would sweep the `Tools/*` obj/ NuGet artifacts into the depot.
- **The real 11e finding ‚Äî Godot treats `.cs` and `.json` as resource types, so `all_resources` shipped the workshop:** the first export packed the entire `Tools/**` harness tree (sources + bin/obj artifacts ‚Äî the `sourcelink.json` files carry local absolute paths) and `.mcp.json` into the `.pck`. Fix: `exclude_filter="Tools/*, .mcp.json"` on both presets. Game `.cs` files keep their path entries (scene script resolution wants them) but ship **content-stripped** via `dotnet/include_scripts_content=false` ‚Äî byte-search of the final `.pck` shows `Assets/Core/GameManager.cs` present as a path and its source text absent, while the pck'd `SchemaDefinitions.sql` DDL and gritty-event JSON content read back verbatim. Probing gotcha for posterity: the three `dotnet/*` export options are registered by the C# plugin, so their names live in `GodotSharp/Tools/GodotTools.dll` (UTF-16), not the editor exe ‚Äî a string-probe of the exe alone false-negatives them.
- **`.csproj` tightening (the one code-adjacent touch):** the two native `&lt;None&gt;` copy items are now RID-scoped to mirror 11a's managed References (`steam_api64.dll` ‚Üî `!= linux-x64`, `libsteam_api.so` ‚Üî `== 'linux-x64'`) ‚Äî the unscoped items were putting the Linux `.so` into the Windows publish output (observed in the first export's data dir) and would have put the Windows `.dll` into the Linux depot. Each native now travels exactly with the managed assembly that P/Invokes it, so no export can ship Steamworks managed code without its native ‚Äî `validate_steamworks_native`'s instant-crash scenario is structurally excluded. Dev builds (no RID, Windows) still copy the Win64 pair; fresh clones still build via the Exists-guards. Solution build 0/0 (all 8 projects) after the edit; no `Tools/*.csproj` references `Assets/Platform`/Facepunch (re-asserted).
- **Windows depot verified + launch-proven (¬ß9.7 + ¬ß9.1 in one shot):** `Build/Windows/` = exe + console wrapper (`debug/export_console_wrapper=2` so the release depot carries a stdout surface) + `.pck` + `data_DirtAndDiamonds_windows_x86_64/` holding `DirtAndDiamonds.dll`, `Facepunch.Steamworks.Win64.dll`, `steam_api64.dll` and **no `.so`**. Launch: `DirtAndDiamonds.console.exe --headless --quit` against the real save boots clean ‚Äî schema **v10** applied from the pck'd `.sql`, `gritty events 19` + contact registry from the pck'd JSON, `48 teams, avatar + 817 NPCs, relationships 72`, exactly one `[Steam] not available` line whose error text (`Could not determine Steam client install directory`) proves the shipped native **loaded** and only client discovery failed, exit 0 ‚Äî and the post-exit save dir holds only the bare `.db` (no `-wal`/`-shm`), so the 11c checkpoint ran through the exported binary too.
- **Linux depot verified structurally:** export exit 0; `DirtAndDiamonds.x86_64` is the official ELF64 release template; `data_DirtAndDiamonds_linuxbsd_x86_64/` holds `Facepunch.Steamworks.Posix.dll` + `libsteam_api.so` + `libe_sqlite3.so` and **no Windows natives** ‚Äî the first real `-r linux-x64` publish, proving 11a's RID-conditional reference switch live, not just on paper. Same `.pck` byte checks pass (no `Tools/`, no `.mcp.json`, DDL + event JSON present, sources stripped).
- **Compliance recorded (¬ß7, README):** the full `ACH_*` minting table (8 code-fired ids verbatim from `AchievementManager.cs` + suggested display copy + hidden flags for the four spoilers), `STAT_SEASONS_PLAYED` as an increment-only INT, and the site-only `ACH_JOURNEYMAN` stat-linked at **min value 10** (the game never references that id ‚Äî the threshold is tunable on the site with no code change). AI-content disclosure is worded truthfully around the actual depot: **zero raster portraits ship today** (10e's procedural fallback everywhere), so the recorded text files the pre-generated-AI disclosure *if and when* portrait art lands, and "no AI content" otherwise ‚Äî no false disclosure either way. Mature-content answers: no sexual content, no frequent violence/gore, General Mature = yes with store free-text covering drug dealing, in-game-currency-only gambling, PEDs, organized crime/bribery/arrests, alcohol; no loot boxes/MTX/real-money wagering (IARC-relevant).

**Verification:** MonteCarloHarness **266/266, no band moved** (re-run this session); solution build 0/0 all 8 projects after the `.csproj` edit; `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation Assets/UI` empty (11e's tree touch = `export_presets.cfg` new, `.gitignore`, `DirtAndDiamonds.csproj` conditions, Steam README sections, design-doc ¬ß10 note, this entry); both exports exit 0; pck contents byte-verified on both depots; the exported-binary boot chain (schema DDL ‚Üí content JSON ‚Üí save open ‚Üí Main.tscn ‚Üí clean checkpoint exit) observed end to end on Windows.

**Disclosed:** the Linux depot has no local launch proof ‚Äî no Linux box or WSL distro on this machine; it queues on real Linux/Steam Deck hardware at submission (the binary is the untouched official template, and the platform-specific publish output is verified, so residual risk is low). Pre-existing repo dirt spotted, not fixed here: `Assets/Graphics/Covers/` and `Assets/Graphics/UI/` each hold an orphaned `cover_art.png.import` whose source `.png` was deleted ‚Äî they pack harmlessly but deserve a cleanup commit.

## 12a + 12b ‚Äî Render integrity + layout honesty: SHIPPED (2026-07-07, Fable 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî opens Phase 12 "Saleable")

**The user's first real playtest verdict ("looks like a DOS game, wouldn't download it for free") root-caused to the theme having NEVER LOADED on their machine ‚Äî plus three structural layout defects that hold even with the theme working. 12a makes the silent-fallback state unmissable and versions the import metadata; 12b removes every always-on overlap and the permanent dead scoreboard. The full Phase-12 sub-plan (12a render integrity ‚Üí 12b layout ‚Üí 12c surface-the-sim ‚Üí 12d at-bat presentation ‚Üí 12e sound ‚Üí 12f identity ‚Üí 12g juice/onboarding ‚Üí 12h store assets) was proposed in chat; 12c/12d owe an Opus design pass before implementation.**

- **The root cause (12a):** `*.import` was gitignored (a Phase-0 rule), so a `.godot/` cache predating the Fonts/ commit never imports the 7 Barlow TTFs ‚Üí `DirtAndDiamonds.tres` line-598 ext_resource parse error ‚Üí `Error loading custom project theme` ‚Üí the whole game silently renders in Godot's default gray theme (and the Card styleboxes vanish, making every overlap catastrophic). Godot boots clean otherwise ‚Äî the user had never seen the shipped Phase-10 look. Fix 1: the 9 `*.import` files are now COMMITTED (the ignore line replaced with a comment; the two `cover_art.png.import` are legitimate ‚Äî their source PNGs are git-tracked, so 11e's "orphaned stubs" note was stale). Fix 2: `Main.WarnIfProjectThemeMissing()` ‚Äî `ThemeDB.GetProjectTheme()` null ‚áí `GD.PushError` + a top-anchored red banner on a Layer-100 CanvasLayer until re-import (dev-facing diagnostic, so the string lives in C# ‚Äî the `[Steam] not available` posture). A stale cache still needs its one `--import` pass; the guard turns that state from invisible into unmissable.
- **12b AtBatView lifecycle:** `visible = false` in the dashboard scene; shown in `StartInteractiveGame`, hidden on both Play/Skip clicks ‚Äî a finished game's recap (scoreboard + play log) stays readable until the next day-advance, and idle days give the space to the card row instead of "Waiting for the pitch..." + inert Take/Swing filling the screen's largest region.

- **12b Pro Shop modal:** converted from the always-visible corner palette (`Visible = true` every `_Process` frame ‚Äî it sat on the scouting card at boot) to the hustle screens' modal idiom: full-rect root, 55% scrim, center-anchored Card (¬±170/¬±140 offsets, grow-both), new CloseButton; `_Process` keeps the avatar-loss auto-close and now skips refresh work while hidden. ## 12c-2 ‚Äî StatLineCard: SHIPPED (2026-07-07, Sonnet 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**The avatar's current-season line, role-aware, per `surface_the_sim.md` ¬ß4/¬ß5 ‚Äî one new single-row query per role, both plans validated against the live save via the SQLite MCP before any C# was written (No Blind Queries).**

New DTOs `BattingSeasonLine`/`PitchingSeasonLine` in `BaseballDtos.cs` carry the counting columns *and* the denormalized rate columns (`avg/obp/slg/ops`, `ip/era/whip`) StatsNormalizer already wrote ‚Äî the card never recomputes a rate itself, mirroring the doc's explicit "rides the UNIQUE index" framing.

Role-aware off the same `isPitcher` split `RefreshScoutingCard` already branches on for the scouting report ‚Äî batting renders H-for-AB/HR/RBI/BB/SO/SB plus the slash line, pitching renders W-L/SV/IP/SO/BB plus ERA/WHIP. A missing row (avatar hasn't recorded a PA/out this season) renders `StatLineNoneText` rather than a zeroed line ‚Äî the doc's "no line yet" requirement.

Refresh rides the existing `RefreshScoutingCard` dirty-flag cadence (day-advance only, called from `RefreshStatLineCard` at the end of that method) ‚Äî no per-frame query or string-format.

AND season_year=?)`. `dotnet build` 0/0 all 8 projects.
