## 12c-3 ‚Äî StandingsCard + LeadersCard: SHIPPED (2026-07-07, Sonnet 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**Fills `LeagueRow` per `surface_the_sim.md` ¬ß3/¬ß4/¬ß5 ‚Äî the `MeRow`/`LeagueRow` split's last empty slot pair, plus the doc's explicitly-deferred rows-vs-tabs density call, settled against a live windowed screenshot rather than assumed. All new query plans validated against the live save via the SQLite MCP before any C# was written (No Blind Queries).**

- **Standings query is the doc's own recovery trick, unchanged:** `BaseballQueries.LoadTeamRecords` (`Players ‚ãà Team_Tiers` scoped to the avatar's tier, `LEFT JOIN Pitching_Stats ‚Ä¶ AND season_year=@seasonYear` so a team with zero decisions still returns a 0-0 row instead of vanishing) sums `w`/`l` per team ‚Äî the same "by current team" join shape as `NormalizeBattingRatesTier`/`LoadLeagueBattingTotals(tier)`. `EXPLAIN QUERY PLAN` against the real dev save (tier 0): `SCAN Players USING INDEX idx_players_team` + `Team_Tiers` PK probe + `Pitching_Stats` UNIQUE-index probe on the LEFT JOIN ‚Äî no full scan. Team identity/name resolves separately through the existing `LoadTeamsByTier`; the doc's prescribed split (no new `TeamStanding` DTO) ‚Äî `BaseballDashboard.RefreshStandingsCard` merges the two lists in C#, sorts by win pct, and computes games-behind itself. **GB is computed as an integer numerator (`(leaderW‚àíteamW)+(teamL‚àíleaderL)`) rather than a double**, since W/L are integers GB is always a whole or half game ‚Äî `FormatGamesBehind` does integer division instead of a culture-sensitive decimal format call, one fewer thing that could render wrong under a non-invariant locale.
- **Leaders is six queries, one per category, not one parameterized query:** `LoadHrLeaders`/`LoadAvgLeaders`/`LoadOpsLeaders` (batting) + `LoadEraLeaders`/`LoadWinLeaders`/`LoadStrikeoutLeaders` (pitching) ‚Äî SQLite can't bind an `ORDER BY` column, so each stat gets its own compile-time-constant SQL (the standing discipline: a built column name is nothing No Blind Queries could validate). All six widen the join to `first_name`/`last_name` so the card never needs a second round-trip per row, sharing one `LeagueLeaderRow` reader (`GetDouble` on an INTEGER column ‚Äî hr/w/so ‚Äî coerces fine at the SQLite C-API level, so count and rate categories share the same read path). Rate categories (`AVG`/`OPS`/`ERA`) carry a qualifying floor (`minPa`/`minOuts`, plain UI-owned constants ‚Äî `MinPaForRateLeaders=10`, `MinOutsForEraLeaders=15` ‚Äî since this is a display-legibility threshold, not a sim rule) per the doc's "a 1-for-1 cameo can't lead the league" correctness note. `EXPLAIN QUERY PLAN` on all six (tier 0, season 2026): full `SCAN` of `Batting_Stats`/`Pitching_Stats` (no index on `hr`/`avg`/`era`/`w`/`so` ‚Äî the `LoadSeasonBattingLines` "deliberate full scan, once per cold read" precedent) + `Players`/`Team_Tiers` PK probes + a temp b-tree for the `ORDER BY`; this rides the same day-advance-only `RefreshScoutingCard` cadence as every other card, never per-frame, so the scan cost is a non-issue.
- **`LeadersCard` is role-aware, not all-six-at-once:** the doc's "HR/AVG/OPS for hitters; ERA/W/SO for pitchers" reads as a per-role split (mirroring the `isPitcher` branch every other card on this dashboard already makes), not a 30-row simultaneous dump ‚Äî a batter avatar sees 3 batting categories √ó top-5, a pitcher avatar sees the 3 pitching categories, keeping the card the same order of magnitude as `StandingsCard`'s ~8 team rows. `RefreshLeadersCard` loads each category through the shared `_leadersBuffer` (cleared/refilled per category, the `LoadRoster`-destination idiom) and formats it into a heading-plus-rows block; three blocks join into the one `LeadersLabel`, the `DevSummaryLabel`/`StatLineLabel` multi-line-in-one-Label precedent ‚Äî no pooled per-row nodes, since both card's row counts are small and fixed (the `ToolRow0..3` precedent, not the Game_Logs "spawned in volume" one).
- **Avatar highlighting uses a plain-ASCII marker (`"* {0}"`), not an arrow glyph:** the vendored Barlow faces don't cover the arrows block (`ToolGradeFormat`'s own note, from 10c) and this is new UI surface where that hasn't been re-verified ‚Äî the `NpcRivalryPaLineFormat = "RIVAL {0}: {1}"` precedent (a text marker, not a glyph) was the safer default. Both new cards' row/format templates stay on `[Export]` strings per `ui_conventions.md` ‚Äî zero new C# string literals.

**Verification:** all standings/leaders query plans checked via the `sqlite` MCP against the real dev save (`dirt_and_diamonds.db`, schema v10, tier 0/season 2026) before writing any C# ‚Äî every join rides an index probe as described above, confirmed against real rows (avatar's team 103/"FRV" correctly reads 1-0, tied for the tier's HR lead at 1). `dotnet build` 0/0 all 8 projects. `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation Tools` empty ‚Äî the whole tree touch is `BaseballDtos.cs`/`BaseballQueries.cs` (new read-only query surface, no schema/write change) + `BaseballDashboard.cs`/`.tscn` (the two cards) + this entry, so `run_monte_carlo_batch` is inert by construction (not re-run). `SchemaValidator` untouched (no DDL edit, `user_version` stays 10). Live windowed boot via the `godot` MCP against the real dev save (schema v10, day 3, avatar + 817 NPCs, 48 teams) ‚Äî zero debug-output errors across the whole run; a `PrintWindow`/`PW_RENDERFULLCONTENT` capture (the 12c-1 review's focus-free technique, process targeted by name) confirms both new `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` paths resolve AND settles **the density call: two rows, not tabs** ‚Äî `LeagueRow` (Standings/Leaders/Plan Today) renders side-by-side with visible slack below it at the shipping window size, well short of overflowing the left panel; the tabbed fallback in the doc is not needed. The screenshot also proves the actual math live: `StandingsCard`'s games-behind reads `1` for a 0-1 team against a 1-0 leader and `0.5` for a still-winless 0-0 team (both hand-verified against the formula); `LeadersCard` marks the avatar's tied HR row with `*` and correctly shows "No qualifying leaders yet" for AVG/OPS at day 3 (nobody has cleared the 10-PA floor yet ‚Äî expected, not a bug).

**Disclosed:** `MinPaForRateLeaders`/`MinOutsForEraLeaders` are first-pass tunable UI constants, not derived from games-played-so-far (a prorated MLB-style 3.1-PA-per-team-game qualifier was considered and rejected as unwarranted complexity for a first cut ‚Äî flagged if a playtest wants the rate boards populated earlier in a season). Not click-driven this session (no headless input-injection path, the standing gap) ‚Äî verification is query-plan proof + a live windowed screenshot, one step further than 12c-2's boot-log-only posture since the density call specifically needed pixels, not just "the tree resolved." `LeaderNoneText`'s branch (zero qualifying rows) is boot-observed on this save (AVG/OPS, day 3) but the populated branch of the *rate* categories is not ‚Äî only the count categories (HR) have live data with real ranks visible yet; a later-day boot or advancing the save further would exercise it for free. Fable 5's 12c-1 path/gate review (DONE) and 12c-2 (never reviewed) both still want folding into one pass over this slice, per the standing note below.

## 12c-2 + 12c-3 ‚Äî Fable 5 review pass + correctness fixes APPLIED (2026-07-07, Fable 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED ‚Äî closes 12c)

**The standing deferred review touchpoint over the whole `MeRow`/`LeagueRow` region (12c-2's `StatLineCard` never had a Fable pass; 12c-3's two cards were new since). The review produced 10 verified findings ‚Äî 7 correctness, 3 cleanup; the 7 correctness fixes are applied in this pass. Two ride sim seams (`CareerManager`/`GameManager`), so `run_monte_carlo_batch` re-ran: 266/266, no band moved.**

The seven, with fixes:

1. **Games-behind sign bug** ‚Äî GB anchors on the win-pct leader, and the numerator `(leaderW‚àíteamW)+(teamL‚àíleaderL)` goes negative in reachable early-season states (a 1-0 pct leader above a 3-1 team); C# integer division truncates toward zero, so ‚àí1 rendered as a wrong-sign `0.5` and ‚àí5 as a conventions-violating `-2.5`. `FormatGamesBehind` now formats the magnitude and renders the sign explicitly through a new `[Export] StandingsAheadGamesBehindFormat = "+{0}"` (the doc's ¬ß5 formula itself is unchanged and never specified the negative case). Supporting determinism fix folded in: the standings comparator gained pct ‚Üí games-above-.500 ‚Üí TeamId tiebreaks ‚Äî `Array.Sort` is unstable, so tied rows could swap between refreshes, and the games-above tiebreak makes the GB anchor among pct-tied teams the one everyone else actually trails.
2. **Stale rates on the post-game refresh** ‚Äî `StatsNormalizer` ran only inside `LeagueSimulator`'s cycle flush; the avatar's attended-game `FlushGame` had no normalize after it, so every `FinishInteractiveGame` ‚Üí `RefreshScoutingCard` read AVG/OBP/SLG/OPS/IP/ERA/WHIP one game stale ‚Äî including `AVG 0.000` beside real hits after the avatar's first game. Fix is the doc-shaped seam: `CareerManager.Normalizer` (optional public field, the `Availability`/`FeedSink` no-ctor-churn precedent, null on every harness path = flush byte-identical) runs a tier-scoped `NormalizeSeason` after ‚Äî never inside ‚Äî the micro-flush batch; `GameManager` wires it with the sims' shared normalizer instance.
3. **Pitcher avatar falsely topping the ERA board** ‚Äî same root cause as (2) surfacing in 12c-3's `LoadEraLeaders` (`ORDER BY era ASC`): a pitcher avatar's stale `era = 0` row outranks every legitimate qualifier once `outs_recorded` clears the floor. The normalize-after-micro-flush closes it; no query change.
4. **Stat line surfaced dead columns (`0 SV` / `0 SB` forever)** ‚Äî both flush sites (`MicroGame.FlushGame`, `LeagueSimulator`) hard-code `sv: 0` and `sb: 0` (the disclosed v4 artifact), so the card showed permanently-zero columns. SV and SB dropped from both `[Export]` templates and their format-arg lists ‚Äî which also restores the design doc's own ¬ß4 pitcher spec (`IP/W-L/ERA/WHIP`, no SV). DTOs/queries still carry the columns for whenever the sim populates them.
5. **Unknown-tier fallback rendered High School standings** ‚Äî `TryGetTeamTier` failure (a team-less avatar: retired to FA at lineage game-over, `team_id NULL`) left `tier` at `default(LeagueTier)` = tier 0, so `StandingsCard`/`LeadersCard` silently rendered High School's tables as the avatar's context. Both cards now gate on `tierKnown` (hidden + queries skipped when the tier can't resolve).
6. **Orphaned recap card** ‚Äî `RefreshScoutingCard`'s no-avatar branch hid every Me/League card but not `RecapCard`, leaving a stale "Last Game" as the lone survivor. The `!show` branch hides it too; when an avatar exists the recap stays game-lifecycle-owned (start/finish swap), untouched by refresh.
7. **Skip Day rendered the pre-tick day** ‚Äî `OnSkipDayPressed` called `RefreshScoutingCard()` synchronously after `AdvanceDay()`, but the bus is deferred-dispatch (publish enqueues; `GameManager._Process` pumps next frame), so the standings/stat-line/leaders always showed *yesterday* after a Skip, until the next click. The skip path now sets `_refreshAfterDayTick` and shares `_awaitingPendingGame`'s existing drain gate (`Events.PendingCount == 0`) in `_Process` ‚Äî one-frame deferral, cards render post-tick truth; the flag also joins the day-button blocked set for that frame. (Pre-existing shape from 10a for the scouting card, but 12c-2/12c-3 attached day-fresh league data to that refresh, which is what made it a correctness defect.)

**Refuted/dropped during verification (recorded so they aren't re-litigated):** the "roster-join W/L reattribution" concern on `LoadTeamRecords` is unreachable today ‚Äî promotions and succession both run only at the yearly rollover, so current-season standings never rewrite under a mid-season roster move; and candidates that re-litigated disclosed decisions were dropped (attended-games-only recap scope, UI-owned qualifier floors, the doc-prescribed standings query split, the leaders full-scan-at-day-advance cadence).

**Not applied (deliberate):** the 3 cleanup findings (allocation/idiom-level in the new card refresh paths ‚Äî day-advance cadence, so no zero-GC mandate applies) are queued for a future Sonnet cleanup slot rather than mixed into a correctness pass.

**Verification:** `dotnet build` 0/0 all 8 projects; **MonteCarloHarness 266/266 (Release), exit 0 ‚Äî same check count as the last recorded run, all ¬ß8/suite-8 band assertions inside it** (mandatory: `CareerManager` is sim-assembly); live windowed boot via the godot MCP against the real dev save (schema v10, day 3, avatar + 817 NPCs, 48 teams, gritty events 19) ‚Äî zero debug errors across the whole run, clean stop, all card paths exercised at `_Ready`. Tree touch: `BaseballDashboard.cs` (all seven UI-side fixes), `CareerManager.cs` + `GameManager.cs` (the normalize seam), this entry. No schema change, no query change, no `.tscn` change (the new/edited `[Export]` strings ship as C# defaults; the scene carries no overrides).

**Disclosed:** the negative-GB render, the tier-unknown gate, the orphaned-recap gate, and the skip-day freshness are code-verified + boot-verified but not state-injected (forcing a 3-1-under-1-0 table or a team-less avatar means bending a live save) ‚Äî they ride the standing manual playtest like every 12b/12c gate. The stale-rate fix's observable symptom (post-game AVG/ERA freshness) is provable in one attended game of normal play. **12c is now closed end to end** (build 12c-1/2/3 + this review), pending the user's commit.

## 12d ‚Äî At-Bat Presentation: DESIGN DOC done (2026-07-07, Opus 4.8, design only ‚Äî NO code)

**`docs/design/at_bat_presentation.md`.** The pending Opus pass `surface_the_sim.md` ¬ß8 flagged (12c's sibling step). Turns the working-but-invisible attended-game micro-sim into a *presented* at-bat. Grounded against the live micro-sim seam this session (`PitchChain.SimulatePa:595`, the per-pitch class draw `:704-727`, `IBatterPolicy:265`; `MicroGame` human-PA driver `:858-891`; `PlayerIntentBridge`/`InteractiveBatterPolicy`; `AtBatView.tscn`/`.cs`; `BaseballDashboard._Process:308-365`). Load-bearing decisions:

- **The decisive finding: the sim computes every pitch's result and throws it away.** `SimulatePa` resolves each pitch to a `PitchClass` (Ball/Strike/Foul/InPlay) + true type + true location, then discards it ‚Äî the UI only ever sees the *pre-pitch* snapshot (count + blurred cue) and the final `PaOutcome`, so the count silently changes with no "strike swinging / fouled back / SMOKED it" beat. The presentation gap is a **data-surfacing gap first**, motion second.
- **The seam is the `FeedSink` pattern one grain finer.** The NPC-PA feed (`NpcPaFeedEvent`/`MicroGame.FeedSink`/`_npcFeed`) is already an optional, observational, UI-only event stream that's null on the macro/harness hot path. 12d extends it from the PA grain to the **pitch grain** of the human's own PA. New `PitchResult` DTO (Class/Type/InZone/BatterSwung/post-count/PaEnded ‚Äî all facts the loop already computed, nothing re-drawn); new `IBatterPolicy.OnPitchResolved(in PitchResult)` (no-op on `NeutralBatterPolicy` + harness policies, forwards to bridge on `InteractiveBatterPolicy`); a third bridge queue mirroring `_npcFeed`. **No `MicroGame` change for batting** (the hook rides the policy).
- **The bit-identity contract (why the sim touch is safe).** 12d is the FIRST sanctioned `Assets/Simulation/Baseball/` touch since Phase 9, so `run_monte_carlo_batch` is **no longer inert by construction** and MUST re-run. The single invariant: **no `rng.` call in `SimulatePa` is added/removed/reordered/made-conditional; the hook consumes no RNG**. Under it the draw sequence is byte-identical ‚Üí 266/266, MLB bit-identity guard exact, tier ladder in-band, all by construction. A moved band = the invariant was violated = the change is wrong. This is the "wrong-is-worse-than-slow" core and the reason 12d owed an Opus pass.
- **Presentation = a beat sequencer (sim races, UI paces, input gated).** The sim BLOCKS at the next human pitch's `AwaitIntent`, so it's at most one pitch ahead within a PA, and at a PA boundary the pending set is causally ordered+bounded (`[terminal pitch]‚Üí[PA outcome]‚Üí[NPC feed‚Ä¶]‚Üí[next snapshot]`). The sequencer drains the FIFO beat queues in order and applies the latest-wins snapshot only when the queue empties ‚Üí enters AwaitingInput + enables controls. **Real input-gating fix:** today `AtBatView.Render` re-enables intent on every snapshot (`:153`), which during a reveal would pre-answer the next pitch; 12d enables controls only on entry to AwaitingInput. States: AwaitingInput ‚Üí PitchInFlight ‚Üí PitchReveal ‚Üí (PaReveal) ‚Üí NpcFeed ‚Üí back.
- **Presentation stays typographic + motion, in-theme** (no sprite art ‚Äî portraits are still procedural; that's the budget). New `ResultReveal` tween'd chip (diamond accent = batter-positive, dirt = negative ‚Äî the 10a tokens, no new palette); count/base/score tick as motion on existing nodes; the timing slider finally earns feedback (œÑ is UI-side ‚Üí "early/on-time/late" with no new sim surface); broadcast play-log; a fast-forward affordance (respect the player's time); beat durations all `[Export]`. Sequencer lives in `AtBatView`; `BaseballDashboard._Process` just forwards bridge events into its queue.
- **Scope:** batter-only (no pitching UI exists ‚Äî symmetric `IPitcherPolicy` hook flagged for later); no schema change (user_version stays 10); **sound is 12e** and 12d builds its SFX-trigger seam (each beat is a trigger point).
- **¬ß6 sub-slices:** 12d-1 the sim seam (harness-gated, no visible change ‚Äî DTO/hook/emit-site/bridge, ends with the authoritative `run_monte_carlo_batch`) ‚Üí 12d-2 sequencer + input-gate fix + pitch `ResultReveal` + count/base tween ‚Üí 12d-3 PaReveal emphasis + timing/read feedback + broadcast log + fast-forward. ¬ß7 verification: the harness gate is mandatory + a suite-7 coherence check (hook fires once/pitch, count reconstructs); `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` must show ONLY `PitchChain.cs`+`InteractiveBatterPolicy.cs`; manual playtest is the real gate (motion/pacing/gating are `AdvanceDay`-is-UI-button-only).
- **¬ß10 model split (recommendation, user decides):** 12d-1 seam = **Sonnet 5 authors** (the FeedSink pattern it has built) but the **authoritative `run_monte_carlo_batch` sign-off is Fable 5's** (sim-assembly touch, the 12c-normalize-seam precedent; a moved band escalates to Fable outright); 12d-2/12d-3 presentation = **Sonnet 5**; review = **Fable 5**. Matches the user's stated "Opus design ‚Üí Sonnet builds it" while the harness gate protects the calibrated core.

## 12d-1 ‚Äî At-bat sim seam: BUILT (2026-07-07, Sonnet 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED; Fable 5's authoritative `run_monte_carlo_batch` sign-off still open)

**Implements `at_bat_presentation.md` ¬ß4 exactly ‚Äî the first sanctioned `Assets/Simulation/Baseball/` touch since Phase 9. Recovers the per-pitch result `SimulatePa` already computes and throws away, so 12d-2/12d-3 have something to render.**

- **`PitchResult` (new, `InteractiveBatterPolicy.cs`, beside `AtBatSnapshot`):** `Class`/`Type`(true)/`InZone`(true)/`BatterSwung`/`Balls`+`Strikes`(post-pitch)/`PaEnded` ‚Äî every field a fact the loop already had this iteration, nothing re-derived or redrawn (deliberately excludes contact quality `q` and the anchor split, per ¬ß4.1). The terminal in-play pitch's `PaOutcome` still travels the existing `OnPaResolved` path unchanged ‚Äî `PitchResult` never duplicates it.
- **`IBatterPolicy.OnPitchResolved(in PitchResult)`** (new, between `NextPitch` and `OnPaResolved`, mirroring the latter's shape exactly). Both implementors updated ‚Äî the full census, confirmed by grepping every `: IBatterPolicy` in the tree (exactly two): `NeutralBatterPolicy` ‚Üí empty `readonly` no-op (the harness's headless stand-in and every autopiloted/skipped/macro game); `InteractiveBatterPolicy` ‚Üí `_bridge.PublishPitchResult(in result)`. The generic constraint on `SimulatePa<TBatter,‚Ä¶>` devirtualizes the call, so the no-op costs nothing on the hot path ‚Äî no new implementor slipped through (no scripted batter policy exists anywhere else in `Tools/`; the one harness-local scripted policy, `AimedPitcherPolicy`, is `IPitcherPolicy` and untouched by this hook).
- **The emit site (`PitchChain.SimulatePa`, the four-way ball/strike/foul/in-play branch):** `batter.OnPitchResolved(...)` inserted between the existing count-update statements and each branch's `continue`/`return`, once per branch, reading `PitchClass` off the *same* branch structure that already existed (`Foul` is only ever reported at the pre-existing two-strike foul-vs-strikeout roll; below two strikes `Strike` covers both called and swinging since the model never rolls that distinction there ‚Äî an honest, not invented, class). **The invariant held exactly as specified: zero `rng.` calls added, removed, reordered, or made conditional** ‚Äî the two structural changes (`bool walked = ++balls == BallStates;` replacing an inline `if`, and naming the previously-implicit two-strike-foul "else" branch) are both behavior-identical refactors of existing statements, not new logic.
- **The bridge (`PlayerIntentBridge`):** third queue `Queue&lt;PitchResult&gt; _pitchResults` exactly mirroring `_npcFeed`'s shape ‚Äî `PublishPitchResult` (sim side, under `_gate`), `TryDequeuePitchResult` (UI side), cleared in `Reset()`. No `MicroGame` change needed (confirmed per ¬ß4.4 ‚Äî the human batter's hook rides its policy, which already holds the bridge).

**The harness gate ‚Äî the load-bearing verification for a sim-assembly touch:** extended suite 7's scripted-interactive-game check (`Tools/MonteCarloHarness/Program.cs`) with a new coherence check per ¬ß7's mandate: collects every `PitchResult` the scripted UI thread dequeues, then an *independent* harness-side reconstruction (Ball ‚Üí +1 ball; Strike-or-Foul ‚Üí +1 strike while under 2; `PaEnded` resets to 0-0) is asserted to match every single reported post-pitch `Balls`/`Strikes` exactly, plus a straight count that the hook fired exactly once per pitch. Result: **20 pitch results vs 20 pitches, coherent=True** ‚Äî the report is proven self-consistent, not just present.

**Verification (`run_monte_carlo_batch`, Release, this session): 267/267 (266 baseline + the 1 new check), exit 0, zero `[FAIL]` lines.** The acceptance gate specifically: **MLB bit-identity regression guard exact** ‚Äî `PA 48384/48384 H 10969/10969 ER 5237/5237`, byte-for-byte the same figures as every prior recorded run; tier ladder still strictly monotone (`AVG .308‚Üí.249 R/G 6.97‚Üí4.28`); the explicit "no band moved" check (¬ß8 generation-3 season) passed. `dotnet build` 0/0 all 8 projects. **Sim-directory touch is scoped exactly as ¬ß7 demands:** `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` shows `CareerManager.cs` (17 lines ‚Äî the pre-existing, already-disclosed 12c-2+3 normalize-seam fix, untouched this session) plus this session's own `InteractiveBatterPolicy.cs` (68 lines) and `PitchChain.cs` (26 lines) ‚Äî no `MicroGame`/resolver/weight file. No schema change (zero Data-layer touch, `SchemaValidator` not re-run ‚Äî nothing to invalidate it). No `.tscn`/UI change ‚Äî 12d-1 is invisible by design (¬ß6: "the queue is drained-and-ignored until 12d-2").

**Disclosed:** this is the Sonnet-build half only. Per the doc's ¬ß10 model split, the **authoritative sign-off is Fable 5's** (sim-assembly touch, the 12c-normalize-seam precedent) ‚Äî the harness run above is this session's own pre-handoff confidence check, not the standing review. A moved band would have been a hard stop; none moved.

## 12d-1 ‚Äî Fable 5 authoritative sign-off: PASSED (2026-07-07, Fable 5 ‚Äî review + `run_monte_carlo_batch`, zero code changed)

**The standing sim-assembly gate, closed. The `PitchResult`/`OnPitchResolved` seam is approved as built; the DTO is now FROZEN for 12d-2/12d-3.**

**Code review (the sim-side diff only ‚Äî `PitchChain.cs` +26, `InteractiveBatterPolicy.cs` +68, harness +42):**

- **Emit site verified branch-by-branch:** the hook fires exactly once on each terminal sub-branch (ball/walk, sub-two-strike strike, two-strike strikeout, two-strike foul, in-play), always *after* the count mutation and *before* the branch's exit ‚Äî and the ¬ß4 invariant holds literally: zero `rng.` calls added/removed/reordered/made-conditional (the two-strike `rng.NextDouble() >= FoulShareOfStrikes` draw sits exactly where it did; `bool swung`/`bool walked` are RNG-free hoists). Bit-identity was therefore expected by construction and confirmed empirically (below).
- **Implementor census re-confirmed independently:** exactly two `: IBatterPolicy` sites in the tree. `NeutralBatterPolicy`'s empty `readonly` no-op devirtualizes through `SimulatePa`'s generic constraint ‚Äî the macro/harness hot path pays nothing; `InteractiveBatterPolicy` forwards `in`-by-ref to the bridge, which enqueues a value type into a pre-sized `Queue&lt;PitchResult&gt;` under the existing `_gate` ‚Äî no per-pitch allocation, `Reset()` clears it with the other queues.
- **The harness coherence check is genuinely independent:** it reconstructs the Balls/Strikes progression from nothing but each `PitchResult.Class` and asserts every reported post-pitch count matches ‚Äî including the deliberate terminal asymmetry (below), which it encodes rather than papers over.

**Two contract notes for 12d-2 (documentation, not defects ‚Äî Sonnet must build to these):**

1. **Terminal-count asymmetry:** on a walk the DTO reports `Balls=4` (the code increments before reporting), but on a strikeout it reports `Strikes=2` (`SimulatePa` never increments to 3 ‚Äî the return short-circuits it). "Count AFTER this pitch" is literal for walks only. 12d-2 must render "strike three" from `PaEnded && Class==Strike`, never from the `Strikes` field.
2. **Sub-two-strike fouls surface as `Class=Strike`:** the model only rolls the foul-vs-strikeout distinction at two strikes (`FoulShareOfStrikes`), so below two strikes a foul is indistinguishable from a called/swinging strike ‚Äî an honest model-fidelity limit, already disclosed in the 12d-1 build entry. `PitchClass.Foul` only ever appears on a two-strike count-preserving pitch.

**Verification (`run_monte_carlo_batch`, Release, five captured runs this session incl. one after `dotnet clean`): 267/267, exit 0, every run.** The load-bearing figures, identical on every run and byte-exact against Sonnet's recorded pre-handoff values: **MLB bit-identity regression guard `PA 48384/48384 H 10969/10969 ER 5237/5237`**; ¬ß8 batch line `.247/.316/.412 OPS .728` in-band; tier ladder strictly monotone (`.308‚Üí.249`, `R/G 6.97‚Üí4.28`); **every zero-alloc check 0 B** (Resolve 10k PAs, warm game day, pitch chain 10k PAs, warm attended games incl. human PAs, geared game day) ‚Äî the hook provably adds nothing to the hot path. **No band moved.**

**Disclosed ‚Äî one unreproducible transient:** the session's *very first* harness invocation (which also performed the cold Release build, with MCP servers spinning up concurrently) exited 1; its console output was truncated so the failing check's name is lost. Five immediate re-runs ‚Äî including a `dotnet clean` cold rebuild ‚Äî all passed 267/267. What bounds the suspect list: every calibration/bit-identity check is seeded and produced byte-identical figures on all five captured runs (those *cannot* flake), leaving only the two load-sensitive check families ‚Äî the `GC.GetAllocatedBytesForCurrentThread()` zero-alloc measurements (tiered-JIT promotion mid-measurement under build load) and suite 7's scripted-UI game, which is scheduling-dependent *by design* (observed 14/20/25/27/27 pitches across the five runs ‚Äî the scripted thread races the bridge; its checks assert liveness + self-consistency, not identity, and all held every time). Verdict: transient environmental, not attributable to the 12d-1 diff. **Recommended (any Sonnet cleanup slot, Tools/ only ‚Äî deliberately NOT applied post-sign-off, to keep the verified tree untouched):** on failure, have the harness re-print a compact `FAILED: <check name>` recap block as its final lines, so a transient failure's identity survives console truncation.

## 12d-2 ‚Äî Beat sequencer + input-gating fix + pitch ResultReveal + count/base/score tween: BUILT (2026-07-07, Sonnet 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED; Fable 5 review still open)

**Implements `at_bat_presentation.md` ¬ß3/¬ß5/¬ß5.7 over the 12d-1 FROZEN `PitchResult` DTO. Pure `Assets/UI/` ‚Äî zero `Assets/Simulation/` touch (verified below); no further sim-assembly risk.**

- **The beat sequencer (`AtBatView.cs`, new):** a light `_Process` state machine (`SequencerPhase`: `Idle`/`Windup`/`Reveal`) draining a single ordered `Queue&lt;BeatEvent&gt;` (a private tagged struct ‚Äî `PitchResult`/PA-outcome-log-line/NPC-log-line ‚Äî no boxing). `Idle` either pops the next queued beat or, once the queue is empty, applies the latest-wins pending `AtBatViewState` and enters `AwaitingInput`. A `PitchResult` beat plays `WindupDurationMs` (default 300) locked, then `PitchRevealDurationMs` (700) showing the `ResultReveal`; a PA-outcome or NPC-feed beat plays its own shorter pace (900 / 250) through the existing play-log. All four durations are `[Export]`, per ¬ß5.6.
- **The real input-gating fix (¬ß3):** `SetIntentEnabled(true)` now fires from exactly one call site ‚Äî the `Idle`-phase pending-snapshot apply ‚Äî instead of on every snapshot arrival. A snapshot that arrives mid-reveal (the sim is already one pitch ahead, blocked on the *next* `AwaitIntent`) sits in `SetPendingSnapshot`'s latest-wins slot and cannot re-enable controls or get pre-answered by a stray click until its beat queue actually drains.
- **`BaseballDashboard._Process` now forwards, never renders (¬ß5.7):** `TryDequeuePitchResult ‚Üí EnqueuePitchBeat`, `TryGetSnapshot ‚Üí SetPendingSnapshot`, `TryDequeuePaOutcome`/`TryDequeueNpcPa ‚Üí EnqueuePaOutcomeBeat`/`EnqueueNpcBeat` (pre-formatted off the existing `PaLineFormat`/`NpcPaLineFormat`/`NpcRivalryPaLineFormat` templates ‚Äî the dashboard still owns text formatting, the view only paces it). Drain order (pitch results, then PA outcomes, then NPC feed, snapshot position immaterial since it's applied lazily) matches the bridge's own causal bound exactly: `[terminal pitch] ‚Üí [PA outcome] ‚Üí [NPC feed‚Ä¶] ‚Üí [next snapshot]`.
- **`ResultReveal` (new nodes in `AtBatView.tscn`):** `RevealOverlay` (`CenterContainer`, `mouse_filter=Ignore`) added as the LAST child of the root `PanelContainer` (draws above `Layout`, so it overlays the whole view ‚Äî the doc's "focal point" ask, read as a broadcast toast rather than pinned to one corner) ‚Üí `RevealChip` (`TierChip` variation, `Visible=false` by default) ‚Üí `RevealLabel`. Text built off `BuildRevealCopy`, narrowed to exactly what the frozen DTO reports (Class/Type/InZone/BatterSwung/PaEnded ‚Äî no timing/read grading, ¬ß5.3 is 12d-3's scope): Ball/Strike/Foul/InPlay call line + a "{true type} ‚Äî {true zone}" flavor line underneath, the doc's "guess (cue) ‚Üí truth (reveal)" arc. **Built literally to both 12d-1 contract notes:** strike three renders from `PaEnded && Class==Strike` (never the `Strikes` field, which never reaches 3); `Foul` is only ever reached at a two-strike pitch, per the model. Two new theme variations (`RevealLabelDiamond`/`RevealLabelDirt`, `DirtAndDiamonds.tres`) recolor the label text only ‚Äî Ball = diamond, Strike = dirt, Foul/InPlay = neutral (base `Label` color) ‚Äî the 10a two-accent budget, no new palette. Tween'd in (fade + `Back`/`Out` scale from 0.85) and out (fade), the two fade legs sized so the whole tween finishes exactly when the beat's own timer says the reveal is done ‚Äî the timer, not the tween, is authoritative for sequencer advancement; `HideReveal()` is an unconditional safety net at beat-end regardless of tween state.
- **Count/base/score "tween, not a silent relabel" (¬ß5.2):** `ApplyState` (the old `Render`, renamed since it no longer owns `SetIntentEnabled`) diffs the incoming snapshot against the last-applied one and fires a small shared scale-pulse (`PulseControl`, 1.0‚Üí1.25‚Üí1.0 over 200ms) on the count label when Balls/Strikes changed, on a score label when it increased, and on a base panel only the pitch it newly lights (not one already occupied). Because the pending snapshot is only ever applied once the beat queue drains, the count/base/score change is structurally guaranteed to land on/after the pitch's own `ResultReveal` ‚Äî never ahead of it ‚Äî with no extra sequencing code required.
- **`AtBatView.ResetSequencer()`** (new, called from `BaseballDashboard.StartInteractiveGame` beside the existing `_bridge.Reset()`): clears the beat queue, the pending-snapshot flag, hides the reveal, and re-locks input ‚Äî so a fresh attended game's first snapshot doesn't inherit a stray pulse-comparison baseline from the previous game and doesn't briefly show stale controls before its own first `AwaitingInput`.

**Disclosed, deliberately deferred to 12d-3 (per the doc's own sub-slice split, not scope creep here):** the PA-outcome beat plays through the existing plain play-log line, not a bigger emphasized `PaReveal` widget (¬ß5.4); no timing/read grading (¬ß5.3 ‚Äî œÑ is already UI-side but unused this slice); no fast-forward affordance (¬ß5.6). The sequencer's causal-order machinery already paces PA-outcome/NPC beats correctly, so 12d-3 only adds presentation on top ‚Äî no further sequencer changes anticipated.

**Verification:** `dotnet build` on `DirtAndDiamonds.sln` ‚Äî **0 warnings / 0 errors, all 8 projects** (main + 7 Tools). **`git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` unchanged from the 12d-1 sign-off entry byte-for-byte** (`CareerManager.cs` 17 / `InteractiveBatterPolicy.cs` 68 / `PitchChain.cs` 26 ‚Äî all pre-existing, none touched this session) ‚Äî **zero new sim-assembly touch, confirming 12d-2 is exactly the doc's "pure UI slices, no further sim touch sanctioned."** `run_monte_carlo_batch` sanity re-run (Release): **267/267, exit 0** ‚Äî inert-by-construction given the zero-`Simulation/` diff, re-run anyway per the standing habit. Live windowed boot via the Godot MCP against the real dev save (schema v10, day 3, avatar + 817 NPCs, 48 teams) with `RevealOverlay`/`RevealChip`/`RevealLabel` in the tree ‚Äî **zero debug-output errors across multiple polls**, confirming every new `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` path (including the two new overlay nodes) resolves; clean stop.

**Not yet verified (disclosed, the standing `AdvanceDay`-is-UI-button-only gap):** the beat pacing, tween motion, and input-gating are only truly provable by actually playing an attended game ‚Äî no headless/MCP input-injection path exists to click Play Game ‚Üí Swing/Take. This is the same gap every prior interactive-UI entry (8a, 9b, 12c) has carried; a manual playtest (confirm every pitch reveals, the count never jumps ahead of the reveal, input is dead mid-reveal and live at the next cue) is the real gate per ¬ß7.6, and is queued as the standing manual-playtest backlog item alongside 12d-3.

## 12d-3 ‚Äî PaReveal + timing/read feedback + broadcast log + fast-forward: BUILT (2026-07-07, Sonnet 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED; Fable 5 review still open, paired with 12d-2)

**Implements `at_bat_presentation.md` ¬ß5.3/¬ß5.4/¬ß5.5/¬ß5.6 ‚Äî the doc's own "full juice pass," closing out ¬ß6's slice table. Pure `Assets/UI/` ‚Äî zero `Assets/Simulation/` touch (`git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` empty), no further sim-assembly risk. Built directly on top of 12d-2's beat sequencer/`ResultReveal` machinery, no restructure.**

- **The `PaReveal` beat (¬ß5.4):** the human's own PA outcome now gets a real chip, not just a log-line append. `BeatEvent` gained a `PaOutcome Outcome` field (both `EnqueuePaOutcomeBeat`/`EnqueueNpcBeat` widened to take it alongside the pre-formatted log line ‚Äî `BaseballDashboard._Process` already had the raw `PaOutcome` in hand from `TryDequeuePaOutcome`/`npcPa.Outcome`, it just wasn't threaded through). `ShowPitchReveal`'s chip tween was factored into a shared `ShowRevealChip(text, accent, durationMs, finishingScale)` primitive; the new `ShowPaReveal` rides it at `PaRevealScale` (`1.35`, `[Export]`) instead of a pitch reveal's `1.0` ‚Äî literally "reusing ResultReveal chip machinery at a bigger scale," per the doc's own wording, no new node. Copy comes off a new `PaRevealNamesCsv` export (`"OUT,STRIKEOUT,WALK,SINGLE,DOUBLE,TRIPLE,HOME RUN!"`, same `PaOutcome` enum order as the existing `OutcomeNamesCsv`) rather than reusing the dashboard's own log-line phrasing, since ¬ß5.4's examples are broadcast-cased/punctuated, not the log's "Your PA: Strikeout." `PaOutcomeBeatDurationMs` default bumped 900‚Üí**1200 ms**, the doc's own recommended default (¬ß5.6) ‚Äî 12d-2 only ever paced a log-line append against it; now there's an actual chip to hold. No windup on this beat (the terminal pitch's own Windup‚ÜíReveal already played the guess‚Üítruth arc) ‚Äî straight to Reveal, matching 12d-2's existing PA-beat shape.
- **¬ß5.3 timing/read feedback ‚Äî no new sim surface, exactly as scoped.** The player's own already-UI-side œÑ is captured at the Swing/Take click (`_committedTau`/`_committedWasSwing`/`_committedGuessInZone`, set in `OnSwingPressed`/`OnTakePressed`) and paired with the *next* `PitchResult` beat ‚Äî safe because at most one human pitch is ever in flight (`PlayerIntentBridge.AwaitIntent` blocking, the same invariant 12d-1/12d-2 lean on), so the last-committed intent is always this pitch's. `TimingBucketText` buckets œÑ into Early/On-time/Late around a `[0,¬±TimingOnTimeToleranceHalfWidth]` band (`0.15` default) and, on a swing, prefixes the reveal's call line via `TimingTagFormat` ("{0} ‚Äî {1}", matching the doc's own illustrative phrasing "you were early ‚Äî swing and miss"). Read-grade tags are the **two literal combos the doc's own table gives**, not a general per-take grade: `ReadGoodEyeText` on a correct-read Ball-took, `ReadFooledText` on a wrong-read Strike-took ‚Äî deliberately not extended to every take/swing permutation the doc didn't actually specify.
- **¬ß5.5 the play-log becomes a broadcast.** `PlayLog` gained `bbcode_enabled = true` (`.tscn`); a new private `AppendPlayLine(string, RevealAccent)` overload wraps the line in `[color=#‚Ä¶]` using colors resolved **once**, at `_Ready`, straight off the existing `RevealLabelDiamond`/`RevealLabelDirt` theme variations via `GetThemeColor("font_color", variation)` ‚Äî a single source of truth for the two accents rather than a second hardcoded hex pair that could drift from the theme (`[` in the line is escaped to `[lb]` first, defending against a stray bracket in future dynamic text breaking the BBCode parse). The public single-arg `AppendPlayLine(string)` stays for the one genuinely neutral caller (`BaseballDashboard`'s game-final summary line). **Every pitch now reaches the log, not just PAs** ‚Äî `ShowPitchReveal` appends the (timing-tag-prefixed) call line the instant the chip reveals, closing the gap 12d-2 left where the log only ever saw PA/NPC lines and the pitch-level truth was purely transient. NPC PA lines are colored too (¬ß5.5's "each per-pitch and per-PA line," read to cover the ambient feed as well) ‚Äî no reveal chip for them, still just a colored log line at `NpcBeatDurationMs`, unchanged pacing.
- **¬ß5.6 fast-forward.** A `FastForwardToggle` `CheckButton` (new node, `Layout/Controls`, `.tscn`) polled directly in `_Process` (`_fastForwardToggle.ButtonPressed`, no signal wiring needed ‚Äî a plain per-frame read, zero-alloc) scales the sequencer's own elapsed-time accumulation by `FastForwardSpeedMultiplier` (`4.0` default) while held. **Disclosed, deliberate simplification:** the doc offered three options (hold-to-fast-forward, click-to-pop-current-beat, persistent toggle) as a "build-time feel decision"; this ships the persistent-toggle variant only, defaulting off (broadcast pace) per ¬ß5.6's own recommendation. Chosen over a click-to-pop skip because every beat's exit is already the same elapsed-time compare ‚Äî scaling that one value compresses every beat kind (windup, pitch reveal, PA reveal, NPC line) uniformly with no new code path, and the existing "`HideReveal()` is an unconditional safety net at beat-end regardless of tween state" note from 12d-2 already makes it safe against the visual tween finishing later than the sped-up phase transition.
- **`git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` unchanged/empty** (12d-1's `PitchChain.cs`/`InteractiveBatterPolicy.cs` untouched, `CareerManager.cs` still the pre-existing 17-line normalize-seam fix) ‚Äî confirmed via `git diff --stat` before build. Full diff this slice: `Assets/UI/AtBatView.cs` (+194/‚àí27 net across insertions/deletions), `Assets/UI/AtBatView.tscn` (+5, the `bbcode_enabled` line + the new `FastForwardToggle` node), `Assets/UI/BaseballDashboard.cs` (+2/‚àí2, the two widened call sites).

**Verification:** `dotnet build` on `DirtAndDiamonds.sln` ‚Äî **0 warnings / 0 errors, all 8 projects.** `run_monte_carlo_batch` sanity re-run (Release): **267/267, exit 0** ‚Äî inert-by-construction given the zero-`Simulation/` diff, run anyway per the standing habit. Live windowed boot via the Godot MCP against the real dev save (schema v10, day 3, avatar + 817 NPCs, 48 teams, 19 gritty events) with the new `FastForwardToggle` node in the always-present `AtBatView` overlay's tree ‚Äî **zero debug-output errors across multiple polls**, confirming the new `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` path resolves; clean stop.

**Not yet verified (disclosed, the standing `AdvanceDay`-is-UI-button-only gap, carried from every prior interactive-UI entry):** the PaReveal's bigger scale actually reading as bigger, the timing tags landing on the right pitches, the broadcast log's colors rendering correctly through BBCode, and fast-forward genuinely compressing a live game are only provable by playing an attended game ‚Äî no headless/MCP input-injection path exists to click Play Game ‚Üí Swing/Take with a timing choice. A manual playtest (a full human PA including a walk, a strikeout, and an in-play PA; toggling fast-forward mid-game; watching the log fill in real time) is the real gate per ¬ß7.6, and per the doc's own ¬ß10 model split, **Fable 5 now reviews 12d-2 and 12d-3 together** ‚Äî this is the point Phase 12d's presentation half closes.

## 12d-2 + 12d-3 ‚Äî Fable 5 review (2026-07-07, paired per ¬ß10): 3 CONFIRMED correctness findings + 7 secondary ‚Äî FIX PASS REQUIRED before commit

**Scope:** the whole presentation half as one diff ‚Äî `9783dd7 ‚Üí working tree` for `AtBatView.cs`/`AtBatView.tscn`/`DirtAndDiamonds.tres`, plus `BaseballDashboard.cs` restricted to the bridge-forwarding/finish seams (the 12c hunks in that file were already reviewed and excluded). Eight angles (line-by-line, removed-behavior, cross-file trace, reuse, simplification, efficiency, altitude, conventions); every finding below was verified against source, not pattern-matched ‚Äî `PitchChain.SimulatePa`'s class draw, the bridge's lock discipline, the `.tscn` paths/slider range (‚àí1..+1 ‚úì), and the `RevealLabelDiamond`/`RevealLabelDirt` variations (font_color = the doc's #53C7A4/#C96A3B ‚úì) were each checked at their definition.

**CONFIRMED 1 ‚Äî game end truncates the presentation (`BaseballDashboard.cs:372`/`419`).** `FinishInteractiveGame` fires the frame `_gameTask.IsCompleted`, but the sim races ahead of the sequencer: after the player's last intent the task completes in microseconds while the view's queue still holds the terminal pitch reveal, the PA outcome's `PaReveal`, and every trailing NPC beat. The view is hidden (`_atBatView.Visible = false`) before any of it plays ‚Äî the player's final PA of every game (the ¬ß5.4 climax, a walk-off included) is never shown ‚Äî and the `FinalFormat` line is appended immediately, so the hidden still-draining queue then appends the last plays *after* "Final: ‚Ä¶" (scrambled log order). This is a 12d-2 regression: pre-12d the dashboard appended lines at dequeue, so the log was current at task completion; the pacing queue removed that invariant and the finish seam never re-established it. There is also a same-frame race: events the sim publishes between the drain loops and the `IsCompleted` check are stranded forever (`_gameTask` is null next frame, drains never run again). **Fix shape:** expose a drained predicate on the view (`_phase == Idle && _beatQueue.Count == 0`) and gate the finish on `_gameTask.IsCompleted && _atBatView.SequencerDrained` ‚Äî which also heals the stranded-event race, since the drains keep running until the gate passes.

**CONFIRMED 2 ‚Äî the ¬ß5.1 "Ball, swung (chase)" row is unimplemented, and it's reachable on roughly a third of swings (`AtBatView.cs:566‚Äì586`).** `PitchChain.SimulatePa` draws the pitch class *independent of intent* (`PitchChain.cs:711‚Äì722`; `DisciplineEdge` = ¬±0.25 with gains 0.30/0.20 shifts the ball mass at most ~7.5%, never to zero), so `Class=Ball && BatterSwung=true` ‚Äî including a swung ball four ‚Äî is a frequent, legal DTO state. `BuildRevealCopy`'s Ball arm ignores `BatterSwung`: a chase renders as "You were early ‚Äî Ball" (or "‚Ä¶‚Äî Ball four ‚Äî take your base") in **diamond-positive**, where the doc's own table row says "Chased it ‚Äî ball" in **dirt**. The 12d-2 comment "every branch the frozen DTO can actually report" was wrong about this branch. **Fix shape:** in the Ball arm, branch on `result.BatterSwung` ‚Üí new `[Export]` chase copy + `RevealAccent.Negative` (walk text presumably still wins on `PaEnded` ‚Äî a designer call to note in the fix).

**CONFIRMED 3 ‚Äî reveal-chip tweens are never killed and don't scale with fast-forward (`AtBatView.cs:543`).** `ShowRevealChip`'s tween runs at real time and its total (fade+hold+fade) equals `durationMs` only by arithmetic; the sequencer's exit compare is scaled by `FastForwardSpeedMultiplier` but the tween is not. At 4x a pitch beat exits after ~durationMs/4 real ms; `HideReveal()` hides the chip but the orphaned tween keeps running, and the *next* beat's `CreateTween` overlaps it ‚Äî the stale tween's chained fade-out then drives `modulate:a ‚Üí 0` while the new tween sits in its hold interval (not writing), so the chip visibly vanishes mid-reveal / flickers under fast-forward. `ResetSequencer` has the same gap (a stale tween survives into the next game's first reveal), and `PulseControl` can double-tween `scale` on the same label when snapshots land inside the 200ms pulse at 4x. The 12d-2 "HideReveal is the safety net" note covered beat *advancement*, not property fights. **Fix shape:** keep the live tween in a field, `Kill()` it at the top of `ShowRevealChip`/`HideReveal`/`ResetSequencer`, and set `tween.SetSpeedScale(speed)` (or scale fade/hold by the multiplier) so the one clock owns both.

**Secondary (verified, fix-with or fold into the standing Sonnet cleanup slot):** (a) BBCode escaping lives only in the colored branch ‚Äî the neutral path and public `AppendPlayLine` reach the now-BBCode log unescaped; escape once in `AppendPlayLineRaw`, markup on top. (b) The committed-intent trio (`_committedWasSwing`/`_committedTau`/`_committedGuessInZone`) is ambient view state paired to "the next pitch beat" by invariant only ‚Äî stamping it into `BeatEvent` at enqueue makes the pairing structural (matters the day click-to-pop or input buffering lands). (c) The `PaOutcome`‚Üíname mapping now has two enum-order CSVs in two files plus `PaRevealAccent`'s positional switch ‚Äî one owner should resolve both strings (dashboard passes chip text alongside the log line). (d) `_revealChip.PivotOffset = Size/2` reads the *pre-relayout* size (text just changed), so the scale-in pivots off-center by one reveal. (e) `ShowPaReveal` inlines a fourth copy of the CSV-index-with-fallback lookup (`PitchTypeName`/`OutcomeName`/`TierName` precedents) ‚Äî collapse to one helper. (f) `_currentRevealDurationMs` is derivable from `_currentBeat.Kind`; a `RevealDurationMs(BeatKind)` switch at the single compare deletes the field and its three scattered assignments. (g) Per-beat `color.ToHtml` + per-frame `ButtonPressed` interop are cacheable (two prebuilt `[color=#‚Ä¶]` prefixes at `_Ready`; a `Toggled`-signal-cached multiplier).

**Verdict: NOT signed off.** No sim touch confirmed across both slices (`git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` empty ‚úì ‚Äî findings 1‚Äì3 are all fixable inside `Assets/UI/`). The pacing/gating architecture, the ¬ß3 causal ordering, the bridge threading, and the timing/read pairing invariant as-built are all sound ‚Äî the findings are seams (game end, a missing table row, tween lifetime), not structure. Fix pass ‚Üí re-build ‚Üí the standing manual playtest (now explicitly including: watch a full game END at pace; swing at a ball and read the chase copy; toggle fast-forward mid-reveal) closes 12d.

## 12d-2 + 12d-3 ‚Äî Fable 5 review fix pass APPLIED (2026-07-07, Sonnet 5 ‚Äî NOT YET COMMITTED)

**All 3 CONFIRMED findings fixed; 6 of 7 secondary items folded in opportunistically. Scope held to exactly what the review sanctioned ‚Äî pure `Assets/UI/AtBatView.cs` plus the one `BaseballDashboard.cs` finish-seam gate ‚Äî so 3 items (secondary (c), the 3 deferred 12c cleanups, the harness `FAILED:`-recap recommendation) are deliberately NOT applied this pass; they'd each require touching `BaseballDashboard.cs` beyond that one gate or `Tools/`, outside the sanctioned surface.**

**The three mandatory fixes:**

1. **Game-end truncation.** New `AtBatView.SequencerDrained` (`_phase == Idle && _beatQueue.Count == 0`). `BaseballDashboard._Process`'s finish check is now `_gameTask.IsCompleted && _atBatView.SequencerDrained` ‚Äî exactly the review's fix shape. Since `_gameTask` stays non-null (and the drain loops above keep running every frame) until both are true, the terminal pitch reveal, the PA reveal, and any trailing NPC beats all get to play before the view tears down ‚Äî and the same fix closes the same-frame stranded-event race the review flagged, since draining no longer stops the instant the task completes.
2. **The chase row.** `BuildRevealCopy`'s Ball arm now branches three ways: `PaEnded` ‚Üí walk (unchanged, wins first), `BatterSwung` ‚Üí new `RevealChaseText` ("Chased it ‚Äî ball") at `RevealAccent.Negative`, else the plain take-a-ball copy (unchanged). Matches the doc's ¬ß5.1 table row the review found unimplemented.
3. **Reveal-chip tween lifetime.** `ShowRevealChip`/`HideReveal`/`ResetSequencer` now `Kill()` the chip's own tracked `_revealTween` before starting a new one, and the new tween's `SetSpeedScale` rides the same `CurrentSpeed()` the sequencer's own elapsed-time accumulation uses ‚Äî one clock owns both, so fast-forward can no longer desync the visual fade from the beat-exit timer or leave an orphaned tween fighting the next reveal. Extended the same kill-before-create pattern to `PulseControl` (tracked per-control in a small `Dictionary<Control, Tween>`) since the review's own diagnosis named it as the same defect class (two snapshots landing inside one 200ms pulse window under 4x).

**Secondary items folded in (6 of 7 ‚Äî all `AtBatView.cs`-only):**

- **(a) BBCode escaping.** `AppendPlayLineRaw` is now the single point every log line passes through (`[` ‚Üí `[lb]`) ‚Äî the public neutral `AppendPlayLine` and the accent-colored path both route through it; previously only the colored branch escaped.
- **(b) Committed-intent stamped structurally.** `BeatEvent` gained `WasSwing`/`Tau`/`GuessInZone`, captured off the ambient `_committed*` fields at `EnqueuePitchBeat` time rather than read back off ambient state when the beat is later revealed ‚Äî the pairing to "the next pitch beat" is now a value on the beat itself, not an invariant a future click-to-pop/buffering scheme could silently break.
- **(d) Reveal-chip pivot.** `PivotOffset` is now set via `Callable.From(UpdateRevealChipPivot).CallDeferred()` instead of read synchronously off `_revealChip.Size` in the same call that just changed the label's text ‚Äî the deferred call lands after this frame's layout pass sees the new size, so the scale-in tween pivots on-center instead of off by one reveal's worth of stale size.
- **(e) The 4th CSV-lookup copy.** New shared `ResolveCsvName(index, names, fallback)`; both `PitchTypeName` and `ShowPaReveal`'s inline lookup now call it instead of each carrying their own index-with-fallback pattern.
- **(f) `_currentRevealDurationMs` deleted.** Replaced by `RevealDurationMs(BeatKind)`, computed at the one compare site in `_Process` ‚Äî removes the field and its three scattered assignment sites (Windup‚ÜíReveal transition, both `StartBeat` non-pitch cases).
- **(g) Cacheable per-frame/per-beat work.** `_diamondColorPrefix`/`_dirtColorPrefix` (full `"[color=#‚Ä¶]"` strings) built once in `_Ready` instead of a `Color.ToHtml` call per colored log line; `_fastForwardToggle.Toggled` is now subscribed in `_Ready` (`OnFastForwardToggled` caches `_fastForwardOn`), so `_Process` reads a cached bool instead of polling `ButtonPressed` every frame.

**Deliberately NOT applied (disclosed, scope-guarded):**

- **Secondary (c)** (consolidating the PaOutcome‚Üíname mapping so one owner resolves both the log-line and chip text) needs `BaseballDashboard.cs` to pass pre-resolved chip text alongside the log line into `EnqueuePaOutcomeBeat` ‚Äî that's a second `BaseballDashboard.cs` touch beyond the sanctioned finish-seam gate, so it's queued for a future slot instead.
- **The 3 deferred 12c cleanups** (allocation/idiom-level, `BaseballDashboard.cs` card-refresh paths) and **the harness `FAILED:`-recap recommendation** (`Tools/MonteCarloHarness/Program.cs`) are both outside `AtBatView.cs`/the one gate entirely ‚Äî untouched, exactly as queued in the prior two entries.

**Verification:** `dotnet build` on `DirtAndDiamonds.sln` ‚Äî **0 warnings / 0 errors, all 8 projects.** `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` **empty** ‚Äî zero sim-directory touch, as required (the fix pass never needed one). Full tree touch: `Assets/UI/AtBatView.cs` (+217/‚àí~47 net) and `Assets/UI/BaseballDashboard.cs` (+8/‚àí2, the one gate line plus its explanatory comment) ‚Äî no `.tscn` change (all fixes are logic-only against existing nodes). `run_monte_carlo_batch` sanity re-run (Release): **267/267, exit 0** ‚Äî inert-by-construction given the zero-`Simulation/` diff, run anyway per the standing habit. Live windowed boot via the Godot MCP against the real dev save (schema v10, day 3, avatar + 817 NPCs, 48 teams, 19 gritty events, 13 relationships) ‚Äî polled twice across the run, **zero debug-output errors both times** (`"errors": []`), confirming every `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` path still resolves after the edits; clean stop.

**Not yet verified (disclosed, the standing `AdvanceDay`-is-UI-button-only gap, carried from every prior interactive-UI entry):** none of the three fixes' actual on-screen behavior is click-driven this session ‚Äî no headless/MCP input-injection path exists to play a game end-to-end, chase a ball, or hold fast-forward through a reveal. **The standing manual playtest (user) is now the real gate for 12d**, explicitly including the three scenarios the review named: watch a full game END at pace (confirm the terminal reveal/PA-reveal/trailing NPC lines all play before the view swaps to the recap, and the log isn't scrambled around "Final: ‚Ä¶"); swing at a pitch that misses the zone and read the chase copy (dirt-accented, not diamond); toggle fast-forward mid-reveal (confirm the chip doesn't flicker/vanish early and the pulse doesn't double-fire). Commit stays user-driven, after this playtest.

## 12d ‚Äî Post-playtest pacing/legibility fix (Sonnet 5, 2026-07-07, NOT YET COMMITTED)

**User playtested 12d live. Two UI issues fixed on the spot, one deeper model finding raised for a dedicated design pass (below).**

- **Play-by-play too fast to read.** The reveal chip can hold up to 3 lines (call, pitch flavor, read-grade tag) but was held only 700 ms ‚Äî unreadable, and the reason fast-forward "seemed to do nothing" (compressing an already-too-fast beat is imperceptible). Bumped the `[Export]` beat defaults in `AtBatView.cs`: `WindupDurationMs` 300‚Üí400, `PitchRevealDurationMs` 700‚Üí**2200**, `PaOutcomeBeatDurationMs` 1200‚Üí**2400**, `NpcBeatDurationMs` 250‚Üí**700**. Still tunable; revisit after the next playtest.
- **Timing slider / zone-read toggle felt inert.** Their only feedback lived inside that same fast-vanishing reveal text. Added a live **`TimingValueLabel`** node (`AtBatView.tscn`) beside the slider, updated on `HSlider.ValueChanged` (subscribed in `_Ready`, unsubscribed in `_ExitTree`) to show Early/On-time/Late as the player drags ‚Äî the effect is now visible *before* committing, not only in the post-swing reveal.
- **Verification:** `dotnet build` 0/0 all 8 projects; `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` still empty (pure `Assets/UI/`); relaunched via the Godot MCP against the live save (schema v10, day 86, avatar + 817 NPCs), zero debug-output errors.
- **The deeper finding (NOT a UI bug ‚Äî pre-existing sim-model gap, now visible):** traced through `PitchChain.SimulatePa:711-748` ‚Äî the pitch *class* (Ball/Strike/Foul/InPlay) is drawn from the location-conditioned mixture **independent of whether the batter swung**; `swung` is recorded into `PitchResult` but never gates the class. So a **Take can resolve as `PitchClass.InPlay`**, and Swing-vs-Take only differs by whether `ContactQuality` is nonzero (the ¬±0.25 read-driven `DisciplineEdge` is identical for both). This is the concrete root cause of the user's "Swing or Take doesn't matter." Invisible before 12d surfaced per-pitch results. Fixing it is a calibrated-core touch ‚Üí handed to a dedicated design pass (next entry).

## At-Bat "Read the Pitch" Input Model ‚Äî DESIGN DOC done (2026-07-07, Opus 4.8, design only ‚Äî NO code)

**`docs/design/at_bat_read_input_model.md`.** The user's redesign of the batter input, prompted by the playtest finding above. Replaces v4 Swing/Take with a **read**: the player guesses **pitch type** + **location (3√ó3 zone grid)** and sets a per-pitch **approach dial** (patient‚Üîaggressive); the **swing becomes emergent** ‚Äî the avatar's plate-discipline/contact ratings decide whether it offers and how well it connects, with **reads decisive** (a correct type+location read plays like a great swing; a wrong read plays like getting fooled). Timing slider removed. (Three design decisions answered by the user via AskUserQuestion: control set = type+location+approach; grain = 3√ó3 grid; weight = reads decisive.) Load-bearing decisions:

- **The calibration-safety seam (INVARIANT N):** `SimulatePa` is used only by the attended micro-game; the macro league sim uses `AtBatResolver.Resolve`, untouched ‚Üí the **MLB bit-identity guard cannot move by construction**. Suites 5 (analytic count-chain pin) and 6 (2000 neutral-policy games in ¬ß8 bands) both run the **neutral** batter policy. So: the `Kind==Neutral` branch keeps today's exact code + RNG byte-for-byte; every new mechanic lives on the new `Kind==Read` (human) branch, which no calibration suite bands (only suite 7's self-consistency checks it ‚Äî the 12d-1 posture, one grain deeper). New RNG on the human branch is allowed; touching the neutral branch is a hard stop.
- **The structural fix for "Take can be In-Play":** on the human branch the class draw is **gated on the emergent swing** ‚Äî a Take yields only Ball / called Strike; a Swing yields only whiff-Strike / Foul / InPlay (never Ball). Count math + `DrawBallInPlay` reused verbatim; only *which classes are reachable* changes. 12d's `BatterSwung` DTO field now genuinely predicts the reachable class set, tightening (not breaking) the frozen contract.
- **The read‚Üíbelief‚Üíswing model** (new `PlayerInputModel` logic, all constants first-pass/`HatchHarness`-tunable): read quality `R` blends type-correctness + location-accuracy, discipline-weighted; belief tracks truth when the read is good and inverts when fooled; `pSwing` shaped by belief + the approach dial + count. Contact quality `q` (replacing the removed timing input) = read accuracy √ó Contact rating ‚Üí the unchanged `DrawBallInPlay`. Power still enters via the anchor.
- **Interfaces:** `BatterIntent` collapses to `{Neutral, Read}` (+GuessType/GuessCell/Approach; Neutral stays `default` = bit-identical); `PitchMatchup` gains `BatterContact`; `PitchResult` gains additive read-grade fields for the reveal narration; bridge `SubmitSwing`/`SubmitTake`‚Üí`SubmitRead`. No schema change (user_version stays 10).
- **¬ß6 sub-slices:** A = sim seam (harness-gated, the sanctioned `Assets/Simulation` touch ‚Äî ends with authoritative `run_monte_carlo_batch`: Invariant N proven + new suite-7 human-branch coherence checks) ‚Üí B = UI (new control bar: 3 type buttons + 3√ó3 grid + approach slider; reveal narrates the read; pure `Assets/UI/`). Optional **A0** 20k-run scripted-read sweep (perfect/random/fooled reader) to confirm "reads decisive" is dramatic but not degenerate *before* the UI is built. ¬ß8 model split: Sonnet builds A & B, **Fable owns the authoritative harness sign-off on A** (a moved neutral-path band escalates to Fable), Fable reviews B.

## Sub-slice A0 ‚Äî "reads decisive" de-risking sweep SHIPPED (2026-07-07, NOT YET COMMITTED)

**The A0 checkpoint of sub-slice A: the read‚Üíbelief‚Üíswing model + the swing-gated human class branch are BUILT, and the scripted perfect/random/fooled sweep proves the feel is dramatic-but-not-degenerate BEFORE the UI is built on top.** Touched `Assets/Simulation/Baseball/PitchChain.cs` (the sanctioned sim touch) + `Tools/MonteCarloHarness/Program.cs` (the sweep). **Deliberately ADDITIVE, not the full collapse** ‚Äî `BatterIntentKind.Read` was added *beside* Neutral/Take/Swing (not collapsed to `{Neutral,Read}` yet), so the existing interactive path (`SubmitSwing`/`SubmitTake` ‚Üí suite 7 + `InteractiveBatterPolicy`) stays byte-identical and green while the new branch is measured in isolation. Collapse + production wiring is the post-checkpoint half.

- **What shipped in `PitchChain.cs`:** (1) `BatterIntentKind.Read` + `BatterIntent.Read(guessType,guessCell,approach)` / `BatterIntent.ScriptedRead(typeOk,inOutOk,locAcc,approach)` factories (all new fields default-zero so `default` is still Neutral); (2) `PitchMatchup.BatterContact` via a **defaulting 3-arg ctor** (existing call sites unchanged ‚Äî `MicroGame` still passes 3 args ‚Üí contact 50); (3) new `ReadInputModel` static class ‚Äî the ¬ß3 pipeline (`GradeRead` ‚Üí `BelievedStrike` ‚Üí `SwingProbability` ‚Üí `ContactProbability`/`ContactQuality`), every constant a first-pass `HatchHarness`-tunable knob; (4) the **swing-gated `Kind==Read` branch** in `SimulatePa`, inserted right after `batter.NextPitch(...)` as a **fully self-contained block that `continue`s/`return`s before the untouched Neutral/Take/Swing switch** ‚Äî the location sub-cell draw (`rng.NextInt(9)`, human-branch-only), belief, emergent swing (1 draw), then Take‚Üí{Ball, called-Strike} / Swing‚Üí{whiff-Strike, Foul, InPlay}. Count math + `DrawBallInPlay` reused verbatim.
- **INVARIANT N held by construction:** the Read branch never touches the calibrated path; the neutral bands are **unmoved** ‚Äî `run_monte_carlo_batch` reports the same `.249/.316/.413/.730`, `K 22.5% BB 9.0% HR 3.2%`, `R/G 4.24`, zero-alloc `0 B`, analytic pin `‚â§1e-9`; MLB macro bit-identity untouched (macro uses `AtBatResolver.Resolve`, never `SimulatePa`). The location sub-cell is drawn only inside `if (inZone)` on the Read branch, so the neutral RNG sequence is byte-identical.
- **The A0 sweep (`RunReadModelA0Sweep`, 20k PAs/archetype, average matchup so the READ is the only lever):**
  - **Perfect** reader `.604/.669/1.229 OPS 1.898` ‚Äî K% 4.1% BB% 16.6% Swing% 46.0% BIP/Sw 54.2% P/PA 3.18
  - **Random** reader `.146/.193/.246 OPS .439` ‚Äî K% 45.8% BB% 5.5% Swing% 48.1% BIP/Sw 28.4% P/PA 3.57
  - **Fooled** reader `.041/.043/.058 OPS .101` ‚Äî K% 66.7% BB% 0.1% Swing% 55.3% BIP/Sw 19.7% P/PA 3.04
  - Approach dial (random reader) Swing%: patient 29.4% ‚Üí neutral 48.1% ‚Üí aggressive 68.6% (monotonic).
  - **Gate verdict ‚Äî PASSED:** perfect < 1.000 (not an auto-win), fooled > .000 (not an auto-out), AVG strictly ordered perfect > random > fooled, perfect walks far more / Ks far less than fooled, approach dial monotonic, all P/PA in a live 2.0‚Äì6.0 band. Six new checks; harness **267 ‚Üí 273/273**.
- **FLAGGED for the playtest (not tuned now, per design ¬ß9 "re-band after the first playtest"):** the perfect-reader **ceiling is high** ‚Äî `.604` AVG / `1.898` OPS at *average* ratings. It's the theoretical asymptote (a mortal never reads perfectly all game; realistic elite play sits between random and perfect), and lowering it blind would be guessing. If the playtest wants it compressed, the levers are `ReadInputModel.ContactQualityReadGain` (0.90) and `ContactProbMax` (0.92). Contact/discipline vanish at 50 in this sweep by design, so a follow-up cut at high-vs-low ratings is the natural next measurement.
- **Measurement note:** the sweep reports **BIP/Sw** (in-play per swing) not whiff% ‚Äî a swung `Class==Strike` conflates true whiffs with sub-two-strike foul-strikes under the frozen 12d-1 DTO (both are `Class=Strike`+swung). Cleanly separating them is exactly what the deferred additive `PitchResult` read-grade fields buy.
- **Follow-on same session ‚Äî additive `PitchResult` read-grade fields + the ¬ß6/¬ß7 human-branch coherence checks landed (build-green, UI-decoupled):** `PitchResult` gained `TypeOk` (bool) + `LocAcc` (double) via a **9-arg ctor**; the original 7-arg ctor now delegates to it with neutral defaults, so the Neutral/Take/Swing path is byte-identical and the DTO stays additive over frozen 12d-1. All 8 Read-branch `OnPitchResolved` calls thread the graded values through. Three new harness checks over the three 20k-PA runs: **a take is only Ball/called-Strike (0 illegal), a swing is only whiff-Strike/Foul/InPlay (0 illegal), and the reported grade reconstructs the scripted read (perfect 0 / fooled 0 mismatches)**. Harness **273 ‚Üí 276/276**; A0 numbers **still byte-identical** (`.604/.146/.041`), zero-alloc **still 0 B** (the extra struct fields don't heap-allocate). This completes the UI-decoupled half of sub-slice A's sim seam.
- **Verification:** `dotnet build` 0/0; `run_monte_carlo_batch` **276/276 exit 0** on a clean run (an earlier run hit the **documented suite-7 timing flake** ‚Äî "scripted UI drives a full interactive game", 24 vs 25 snapshots, the scheduling-dependent bridge poll on the **untouched** Swing/Take path ‚Äî green on re-run; seeded checks can't flake). A0 numbers **byte-identical across runs** (seeded). `git diff --stat -- Assets/Simulation` shows only `PitchChain.cs` + `InteractiveBatterPolicy.cs` (the additive `PitchResult` fields) ‚Äî exactly the sub-slice-A file set (¬ß7.3).

## Sub-slice A collapse + sub-slice B (UI): BUILT (Sonnet 5, 2026-07-07), uncommitted

**The remainder of sub-slice A (the collapse) landed together with sub-slice B (the UI), per the design's own note that flipping the bridge breaks `AtBatView` mid-build.** `run_monte_carlo_batch` **277/277 exit 0** (276 ‚Üí 277, +1 new check), Invariant N held, `dotnet build` 0/0 across the whole solution, headless `--headless --quit` boot against the real dev save clean, plus a standalone headless run of `AtBatView.tscn` as the main scene (`--quit-after 2`) to exercise every `GetNode&lt;T&gt;()` call in `_Ready()` ‚Äî exit 0, no errors.

- **The collapse (`Assets/Simulation/Baseball/PitchChain.cs`):** `BatterIntentKind` is now exactly `{Neutral, Read}` ‚Äî `Take`/`Swing` removed, along with `BatterIntent.Timing`/`GuessInZone`, the `Take`/`Swing` factories, and the whole `PlayerInputModel` static class (`FromTake`/`FromSwing`/`PerceivedStuff`) ‚Äî fully dead once its only two call sites (the Take/Swing switch cases in `SimulatePa`) were removed. The switch collapsed to a single `BatterPitchInput input = default;` (Neutral is the only `Kind` left once `Read` has already `continue`d/`return`ed above it) and `bool swung` became `const bool swung = false;` ‚Äî same runtime behavior, no RNG-sequence change, so suites 5/6 and the MLB bit-identity guard are untouched **by construction**, not just by re-measurement.
- **The bridge (`InteractiveBatterPolicy.cs`):** `PlayerIntentBridge.SubmitSwing`/`SubmitTake` ‚Üí one `SubmitRead(PitchType guessType, byte guessCell, double approach)`; `AwaitIntent` now hands back `(guessType, guessCell, approach)` instead of `(isSwing, timing, guessInZone)`. `InteractiveBatterPolicy.NextPitch` returns `BatterIntent.Read(guessType, guessCell, approach)` directly ‚Äî the swing is emergent sim-side, never chosen UI-side.
- **`MicroGame.cs`:** the interactive-PA `PitchMatchup` now passes `batter.Contact` (was defaulting to 50 via the 3-arg ctor) ‚Äî the Read branch's contact-probability/quality terms are live for real avatars, not just the harness's average-matchup A0 sweep.
- **Suite 7 (`Tools/MonteCarloHarness/Program.cs`):** the scripted UI thread now calls `bridge.SubmitRead(...)` (even pitches: Fastball, center cell 4, approach +0.5; odd pitches: Breaking, `ReadInputModel.OutOfZoneCell`, approach ‚àí0.5) instead of `SubmitSwing`/`SubmitTake`. Added a new coherence check re-verifying, over the **actual bridge/thread handshake** (not just the A0 sweep's direct `SimulatePa` calls): a take is never Foul/InPlay, a swing is never Ball, and `TypeOk`/`LocAcc` reconstruct exactly from the known scripted guess each pitch (index parity matches submission parity 1:1 ‚Äî `pitchResults` is FIFO in submission order). This is the "new suite-7 human-branch coherence checks" the design doc's ¬ß6 sub-slice-A exit criteria called for; the A0 sweep (already shipped) had separately covered the same legality/reconstruction properties over the direct `SimulatePa` path.
- **The UI (`Assets/UI/AtBatView.tscn` + `.cs`, `Assets/UI/BaseballDashboard.cs`):** the Swing/Take buttons + timing slider + zone-read toggle are replaced by: three type buttons (Fastball/Breaking/Offspeed, one `ButtonGroup`), a 3√ó3 zone grid (`Cell0`..`Cell8`, row-major, a second `ButtonGroup`) plus an "Expect a ball" out-of-zone button in the same group, an approach slider (Patient‚ÜîAggressive, live bucket readout, persists between pitches ‚Äî a standing stance, not a per-pitch reset), and a Commit button (enabled only once a type AND a zone/ball are picked while awaiting input). Committing emits `ReadCommitted(int guessType, int guessCell, double approach)`, forwarded straight to `_bridge.SubmitRead`. `SetIntentEnabled(true)` clears the prior type/cell selection (a stale guess must never silently answer the next pitch) but leaves the approach dial alone. The reveal's `BuildRevealCopy` dropped the old timing tag and the two-literal-combo read note, replaced by a `ReadGradeTag(TypeOk, LocAcc)` bucketing that fires on **every** pitch (not just takes): perfect / close / wrong-type-right-zone / wrong-zone / completely-fooled ‚Äî using the frozen `PitchResult.TypeOk`/`LocAcc` fields that sub-slice A already shipped. `BeatEvent` dropped its `WasSwing`/`Tau`/`GuessInZone` stamped-intent fields entirely ‚Äî no longer needed, since `PitchResult.BatterSwung` is already ground truth and the swing is never UI-chosen.
- **Not yet done:** the manual playtest (design ¬ß7.4 ‚Äî the real gate: confirm reads visibly matter, the approach dial visibly trades walks for damage, a Take never reports In-Play, the reveal narrates the read correctly) has NOT been run ‚Äî this session's verification is build/harness/headless-boot only, per the UI-testing disclosure rule (no click-through capability available for a Godot game this session). **Fable 5's review of the collapse (a sim-assembly touch, design ¬ß8 rule) and of the UI (the 12d-2/12d-3 precedent) has also not happened yet** ‚Äî this entry is Sonnet 5's own harness sign-off, not Fable's.

## Sub-slice A collapse + sub-slice B (UI): SIGNED OFF (Fable 5, 2026-07-07)

**The design-¬ß8 escalation review of the collapse (a sim-assembly touch) and the 12d-2/12d-3-precedent review of the UI half: NO DEFECTS FOUND. Authoritative `run_monte_carlo_batch`: 277/277 exit 0 √ó 2 runs; `dotnet build` whole solution 0/0.** The feature's only remaining gate before commit is the ¬ß7.4 manual playtest.

What the review verified (beyond re-measurement ‚Äî each Invariant-N claim was checked *by construction* against the actual code):

- **Collapse equivalence is literal, not just plausible:** every path inside the `Kind == Read` branch of `SimulatePa` ends in `continue` or `return` (read line-by-line, `PitchChain.cs:711-808`), so "Neutral is the only Kind left" at the fall-through is structurally true; `BatterPitchInput input = default;` is byte-for-byte what the removed switch's `default:` case produced, and `const bool swung = false;` is what `intent.Kind == BatterIntentKind.Swing` evaluated to for a Neutral intent. No RNG call added or removed on the neutral path.
- **The `MicroGame` 4-arg `PitchMatchup` change cannot touch calibration:** `matchup.BatterContact` is consumed at exactly two sites, both inside the Read branch (`ContactProbability`, `ContactQuality`) ‚Äî autopilot/neutral attended games flow through the same constructor change but never read the field.
- **The bridge rewrite preserves the concurrency contract verbatim:** `SubmitRead` carries over `SubmitBatter`'s consumed-await guard unchanged (stale click returns; `_awaiting = None` before `Release()` so a double click can never release the semaphore twice and pre-answer the next pitch); approach clamped to [‚àí1,+1] bridge-side.
- **No stale surface anywhere:** repo-wide grep for `SubmitSwing|SubmitTake|PlayerInputModel|BatterIntent(Kind)?.(Take|Swing)|GuessInZone|SwingCommitted|TakeCommitted` over `*.cs` AND `*.tscn` ‚Äî zero matches.
- **UI half:** signal wiring is symmetric `_Ready`/`_ExitTree` *including* the nine per-cell lambda handlers (stored in `_zoneCellHandlers` so unsubscription actually removes them ‚Äî the easy leak was avoided); `ClearReadSelections` uses `SetPressedNoSignal` (no handler re-entry on the programmatic clear); `CommitButton` ships `disabled = true` in the scene so the pre-first-snapshot state is safe even before `SetIntentEnabled` first runs (plus the defensive guard in `OnCommitPressed`); the approach slider carried the old timing slider's `min_value = -1.0` / `max_value = 1.0` / `step = 0.01` (checked in the `.tscn` ‚Äî Godot's 0..100 `HSlider` default would have silently broken the dial); `ReadGradeTag` exactly partitions `GradeRead`'s output space into the five mutually-exclusive buckets (perfect / close / wrong-type / wrong-zone / fooled) with no unreachable or double-matched case.
- **Suite-7's new coherence check is geometrically sound:** the even-pitch guess sits cell 4 (center), which is Chebyshev-adjacent to all eight other cells, so "in-zone LocAcc is only ever 1.0 or `LocAccAdjacent`, never `LocAccFar`" is a theorem of `CellDistance`, not a tuning accident.

**Verification detail:** run 1 ‚Äî 277/277, zero `FAIL` lines, all four zero-alloc checks 0 B, **MLB bit-identity fingerprint byte-exact vs the 12d-1 sign-off record (PA 48384/48384, H 10969/10969, ER 5237/5237)**, A0 sweep byte-identical (`.604/.146/.041`, approach dial 29.4/48.1/68.6%), neutral micro league unmoved (`.249/.316/.413` OPS `.730`), both pipeline seasons in band (R/G 4.21/4.29). Run 2 ‚Äî 277/277 with explicit `EXIT=0` (also the cross-run determinism confirmation). `dotnet build` on the full solution 0/0 (the harness alone doesn't compile the UI csproj; this closes that gap). No suite-7 timing flake in either run.
